## 6010: Sin (id: 6010)

* 6020: sin
* 6040: sinners
* **Associated Articles:** 6020: sin (ID: `6020@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6040: sinners (ID: `6040@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6020: sin (id: 6020)

Primarily a wrong relationship with God, which may express itself in wrong attitudes or actions towards God himself, other human beings, possessions or the environment. Scripture stresses that this condition is deeply rooted in human nature, and that only God is able to break its penalty, power and presence.

* **Associated Articles:** 6021: sin, nature of (ID: `6021@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6022: sin, causes of (ID: `6022@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6023: sin, universality of (ID: `6023@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6024: sin, effects of (ID: `6024@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6025: sin, and God's character (ID: `6025@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6026: sin, God's judgment on (ID: `6026@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6027: sin, God's remedy for (ID: `6027@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6028: sin, God's deliverance from (ID: `6028@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6029: sin, accepting forgiveness of (ID: `6029@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6030: sin, avoidance of (ID: `6030@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6021: sin, nature of (id: 6021)

Scripture portrays sin in terms of wrongness before God in a variety of different ways, such as uncleanness, guilt or rebellion.

The basic nature of sin
-----------------------

### All sin is directed against God

**[PSA 51:4](https://ref.ly/Ps51:4)** *See also* [GEN 13:13](https://ref.ly/Gen13:13); [EXO 10:16](https://ref.ly/Exod10:16); [JDG 10:10](https://ref.ly/Judg10:10); [PSA 41:4](https://ref.ly/Ps41:4); [LUK 15:18](https://ref.ly/Luke15:18)

### Sin is essentially a lack of faith in God

**[ROM 14:23](https://ref.ly/Rom14:23)** *See also* [HEB 11:6](https://ref.ly/Heb11:6)

Descriptions of sin
-------------------

### Corruption of God's good purposes

**[DEU 32:5](https://ref.ly/Deut32:5)** *See also* [GEN 6:11–6:12](https://ref.ly/Gen6:11-Gen6:12); [DEU 9:12](https://ref.ly/Deut9:12), [DEU 31:29](https://ref.ly/Deut31:29); [JDG 2:19](https://ref.ly/Judg2:19)

### Doing evil in God's sight

**[JHN 3:19–3:20](https://ref.ly/John3:19-John3:20)** *See also* [JDG 2:11](https://ref.ly/Judg2:11); [PSA 34:12–34:16](https://ref.ly/Ps34:12-Ps34:16); [PRO 8:13](https://ref.ly/Prov8:13); [ISA 59:6–59:7](https://ref.ly/Isa59:6-Isa59:7); [MAT 12:35](https://ref.ly/Matt12:35) parallel [LUK 6:45](https://ref.ly/Luke6:45)

### Ungodliness

**[JUD 1:14–1:15](https://ref.ly/Jude1:14-Jude1:15)** *See also* [ISA 9:17](https://ref.ly/Isa9:17), [ISA 32:6](https://ref.ly/Isa32:6); [1TI 1:9](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:9)

### Rebellion against God's authority

**[ISA 30:9](https://ref.ly/Isa30:9)** *See also* [DEU 9:7](https://ref.ly/Deut9:7); [1SA 15:23](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:23); [PSA 78:40](https://ref.ly/Ps78:40), [PSA 78:56](https://ref.ly/Ps78:56); [JER 3:13](https://ref.ly/Jer3:13); [HOS 7:13](https://ref.ly/Hos7:13)

### The breaking or transgression of God's laws

**[1JN 3:4](https://ref.ly/1John3:4)** *See also* [1SA 13:13–13:14](https://ref.ly/1Sam13:13-1Sam13:14); [1CH 10:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr10:13); [NEH 9:29](https://ref.ly/Neh9:29); [MIC 1:5](https://ref.ly/Mic1:5), [MIC 7:18](https://ref.ly/Mic7:18); [ROM 2:23](https://ref.ly/Rom2:23), [ROM 4:15](https://ref.ly/Rom4:15), [ROM 5:14–5:17](https://ref.ly/Rom5:14-Rom5:17); [JAS 2:10–2:11](https://ref.ly/Jas2:10-Jas2:11)

### Straying from the right path

**[ISA 53:6](https://ref.ly/Isa53:6)** *See also* [PSA 58:3](https://ref.ly/Ps58:3), [PSA 95:10](https://ref.ly/Ps95:10), [PSA 119:10](https://ref.ly/Ps119:10), [PSA 119:21](https://ref.ly/Ps119:21), [PSA 119:118](https://ref.ly/Ps119:118)

### Incurring a debt

**[MAT 6:12](https://ref.ly/Matt6:12)** *See also* [MAT 18:21–18:35](https://ref.ly/Matt18:21-Matt18:35)

### Falling short of a standard

**[ROM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23)** *The words most commonly used for “sin” in the OT and NT originally signified “missing the mark”.*

### Uncleanness

**[PSA 51:2](https://ref.ly/Ps51:2)**; **[ISA 1:16](https://ref.ly/Isa1:16)** *See also* [PSA 51:7](https://ref.ly/Ps51:7); [HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14)

Kinds of sin
------------

### Sins of omission

**[JAS 4:17](https://ref.ly/Jas4:17)** *See also* [MAT 23:23](https://ref.ly/Matt23:23) parallel [LUK 11:42](https://ref.ly/Luke11:42); [MAT 25:45](https://ref.ly/Matt25:45)

### Deliberate sins

**[LUK 12:47](https://ref.ly/Luke12:47)** *See also* [NUM 15:30–15:31](https://ref.ly/Num15:30-Num15:31); [DEU 1:42–1:43](https://ref.ly/Deut1:42-Deut1:43), [DEU 17:12](https://ref.ly/Deut17:12); [PSA 19:13](https://ref.ly/Ps19:13); [ISA 57:17](https://ref.ly/Isa57:17); [ROM 1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:32)

### Unintentional sins

**[LUK 12:48](https://ref.ly/Luke12:48)** *See also* [LEV 4:1–4:5](https://ref.ly/Lev4:1-Lev4:5); [NUM 15:22–15:29](https://ref.ly/Num15:22-Num15:29); [DEU 4:41–4:42](https://ref.ly/Deut4:41-Deut4:42); [ACT 3:17](https://ref.ly/Acts3:17); [1TI 1:13](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:13)

### Sin against the Holy Spirit

**[MRK 3:29–3:30](https://ref.ly/Mark3:29-Mark3:30)** parallels [MAT 12:31–12:32](https://ref.ly/Matt12:31-Matt12:32), [LUK 12:10](https://ref.ly/Luke12:10) *See also* [1JN 5:16](https://ref.ly/1John5:16)

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 51:4; Genesis 13:13; Exodus 10:16; Judges 10:10; Psalms 41:4; Luke 15:18; Romans 14:23; Hebrews 11:6; Deuteronomy 32:5; Genesis 6:11-12; Deuteronomy 9:12; Deuteronomy 31:29; Judges 2:19; John 3:19-20; Judges 2:11; Psalms 34:12-16; Proverbs 8:13; Isaiah 59:6-7; Matthew 12:35; Luke 6:45; Jude 1:14-15; Isaiah 9:17; Isaiah 32:6; 1 Timothy 1:9; Isaiah 30:9; Deuteronomy 9:7; 1 Samuel 15:23; Psalms 78:40; Psalms 78:56; Jeremiah 3:13; Hosea 7:13; 1 John 3:4; 1 Samuel 13:13-14; 1 Chronicles 10:13; Nehemiah 9:29; Micah 1:5; Micah 7:18; Romans 2:23; Romans 4:15; Romans 5:14-17; James 2:10-11; Isaiah 53:6; Psalms 58:3; Psalms 95:10; Psalms 119:10; Psalms 119:21; Psalms 119:118; Matthew 6:12; Matthew 18:21-35; Romans 3:23; Psalms 51:2; Isaiah 1:16; Psalms 51:7; Hebrews 9:14; James 4:17; Matthew 23:23; Luke 11:42; Matthew 25:45; Luke 12:47; Numbers 15:30-31; Deuteronomy 1:42-43; Deuteronomy 17:12; Psalms 19:13; Isaiah 57:17; Romans 1:32; Luke 12:48; Leviticus 4:1-5; Numbers 15:22-29; Deuteronomy 4:41-42; Acts 3:17; 1 Timothy 1:13; Mark 3:29-30; Matthew 12:31-32; Luke 12:10; 1 John 5:16
* **Associated Articles:** 3245: Holy Spirit, blasphemy against (ID: `3245@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 4811: darkness, as a symbol of sin (ID: `4811@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5135: blindness, spiritual (ID: `5135@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5375: law (ID: `5375@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6040: sinners (ID: `6040@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6206: offence (ID: `6206@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6221: rebellion (ID: `6221@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6237: sexual sin, nature of (ID: `6237@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7422: ritual (ID: `7422@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8802: pride (ID: `8802@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8834: unbelief (ID: `8834@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8846: ungodliness (ID: `8846@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6022: sin, causes of (id: 6022)

Sin is the result of the fall, at which the creation rebels against God its Creator.

Sin as a result of the devil's activity
---------------------------------------

### The devil's instigation of the first sin

**[GEN 3:13](https://ref.ly/Gen3:13)** *See also* [GEN 3:1–3:6](https://ref.ly/Gen3:1-Gen3:6); [2CO 11:3](https://ref.ly/2Cor11:3); [REV 12:9](https://ref.ly/Rev12:9)

### The devil's role as tempter

**[1TH 3:5](https://ref.ly/1Thess3:5)** *See also* [MAT 4:1–4:11](https://ref.ly/Matt4:1-Matt4:11) parallels [MRK 1:12–1:13](https://ref.ly/Mark1:12-Mark1:13), [LUK 4:1–4:13](https://ref.ly/Luke4:1-Luke4:13); [MAT 6:13](https://ref.ly/Matt6:13)

### The devil as the source of sinful behaviour

**[JHN 8:44](https://ref.ly/John8:44)** *See also* [JHN 8:38](https://ref.ly/John8:38), [JHN 8:41](https://ref.ly/John8:41); [1JN 3:8](https://ref.ly/1John3:8), [1JN 3:10](https://ref.ly/1John3:10)

### The sins of angels

**[2PE 2:4](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:4)** *See also* [JUD 1:6](https://ref.ly/Jude1:6)

Sin as a power in the world
---------------------------

### Sin's reign from the time of Adam

**[ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12)** *See also* [GEN 4:7](https://ref.ly/Gen4:7); [JHN 8:34](https://ref.ly/John8:34); [ROM 5:21](https://ref.ly/Rom5:21), [ROM 6:16](https://ref.ly/Rom6:16)

### Sin uses the law to provoke sinful desires

**[ROM 7:5](https://ref.ly/Rom7:5)** *See also* [ROM 7:7–7:12](https://ref.ly/Rom7:7-Rom7:12); [1CO 15:56](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:56)

### The world is under sin's dominion

**[1JN 2:16](https://ref.ly/1John2:16)** *See also* [LUK 21:34](https://ref.ly/Luke21:34); [TIT 2:12](https://ref.ly/Titus2:12)

Sin is rooted in human nature
-----------------------------

### The human heart is dominated by sin

**[JER 17:9](https://ref.ly/Jer17:9)** *See also* [MAT 15:19](https://ref.ly/Matt15:19) parallel [MRK 7:21–7:22](https://ref.ly/Mark7:21-Mark7:22); [ROM 1:24](https://ref.ly/Rom1:24); [HEB 3:12](https://ref.ly/Heb3:12)

### Human nature is fundamentally opposed to God

**[ROM 8:5–8:8](https://ref.ly/Rom8:5-Rom8:8)** *See also* [ROM 7:14–7:25](https://ref.ly/Rom7:14-Rom7:25); [GAL 5:17–5:21](https://ref.ly/Gal5:17-Gal5:21); [EPH 2:3](https://ref.ly/Eph2:3); [2PE 2:10](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:10), [2PE 2:18](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:18)

The act of sinning
------------------

### Sin results from giving in to evil desires

**[JAS 1:14–1:15](https://ref.ly/Jas1:14-Jas1:15)** *See also* [ROM 13:13–13:14](https://ref.ly/Rom13:13-Rom13:14); [JAS 4:1](https://ref.ly/Jas4:1); [JUD 1:16](https://ref.ly/Jude1:16)

### Sin results from the human desire to be like God

**[GEN 3:5](https://ref.ly/Gen3:5)** *See also* [ISA 14:12–14:14](https://ref.ly/Isa14:12-Isa14:14); [EZK 28:2](https://ref.ly/Ezek28:2)

### Sin results when the body is placed at sin's disposal

**[ROM 6:13](https://ref.ly/Rom6:13)** *See also* [MAT 5:29–5:30](https://ref.ly/Matt5:29-Matt5:30), [MAT 18:8–18:9](https://ref.ly/Matt18:8-Matt18:9) parallel [MRK 9:43–9:47](https://ref.ly/Mark9:43-Mark9:47)

### Sin results from the influence of others

**[1CO 15:33](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:33)** *See also* [EXO 23:33](https://ref.ly/Exod23:33); [1KI 11:3](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:3); [PRO 1:10](https://ref.ly/Prov1:10), [PRO 22:24–22:25](https://ref.ly/Prov22:24-Prov22:25)

### The seriousness of leading others into sin

**[MRK 9:42](https://ref.ly/Mark9:42)** parallels [MAT 18:6](https://ref.ly/Matt18:6), [LUK 17:1–17:2](https://ref.ly/Luke17:1-Luke17:2) *See also* [1CO 8:9–8:13](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:9-1Cor8:13)

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 3:13; Genesis 3:1-6; 2 Corinthians 11:3; Revelation 12:9; 1 Thessalonians 3:5; Matthew 4:1-11; Mark 1:12-13; Luke 4:1-13; Matthew 6:13; John 8:44; John 8:38; John 8:41; 1 John 3:8; 1 John 3:10; 2 Peter 2:4; Jude 1:6; Romans 5:12; Genesis 4:7; John 8:34; Romans 5:21; Romans 6:16; Romans 7:5; Romans 7:7-12; 1 Corinthians 15:56; 1 John 2:16; Luke 21:34; Titus 2:12; Jeremiah 17:9; Matthew 15:19; Mark 7:21-22; Romans 1:24; Hebrews 3:12; Romans 8:5-8; Romans 7:14-25; Galatians 5:17-21; Ephesians 2:3; 2 Peter 2:10; 2 Peter 2:18; James 1:14-15; Romans 13:13-14; James 4:1; Jude 1:16; Genesis 3:5; Isaiah 14:12-14; Ezekiel 28:2; Romans 6:13; Matthew 5:29-30; Matthew 18:8-9; Mark 9:43-47; 1 Corinthians 15:33; Exodus 23:33; 1 Kings 11:3; Proverbs 1:10; Proverbs 22:24-25; Mark 9:42; Matthew 18:6; Luke 17:1-2; 1 Corinthians 8:9-13
* **Associated Articles:** 4025: world, the (ID: `4025@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 4120: Satan (ID: `4120@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6154: fall, the (ID: `6154@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6166: flesh, sinful nature (ID: `6166@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6023: sin, universality of (id: 6023)

All human beings sin and are guilty in the sight of God on account of an inherently sinful disposition, which can be traced back to Adam. Acts of sin thus arise from a sinful human heart. The basis of cleansing and cancellation of “original sin” is the atoning death of Jesus Christ.

Adam, the cause of universal sin
--------------------------------

**[ROM 5:19](https://ref.ly/Rom5:19)** *See also* [GEN 3:1–3:24](https://ref.ly/Gen3:1-Gen3:24); [ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12); [1CO 15:22](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:22)

The universe is in subjection to sin
------------------------------------

**[GAL 3:22](https://ref.ly/Gal3:22)** *See also* [ROM 5:21](https://ref.ly/Rom5:21), [ROM 11:32](https://ref.ly/Rom11:32)

Sin is inherent in human nature
-------------------------------

### Sinfulness from birth

**[PSA 51:5](https://ref.ly/Ps51:5)** *See also* [JOB 25:4](https://ref.ly/Job25:4); [PSA 58:3](https://ref.ly/Ps58:3)

### The sinful heart

**[GEN 6:5](https://ref.ly/Gen6:5)** *See also* [GEN 8:21](https://ref.ly/Gen8:21); [ECC 9:3](https://ref.ly/Eccl9:3); [JER 17:9](https://ref.ly/Jer17:9); [MAT 15:19](https://ref.ly/Matt15:19) parallel [MRK 7:21](https://ref.ly/Mark7:21)

### The sinful nature

**[EPH 2:3](https://ref.ly/Eph2:3)** *See also* [ROM 8:6–8:8](https://ref.ly/Rom8:6-Rom8:8); [GAL 5:19–5:21](https://ref.ly/Gal5:19-Gal5:21)

The universality of sin
-----------------------

### No\-one is righteous

**[ROM 3:9–3:19](https://ref.ly/Rom3:9-Rom3:19)** *See also* [PSA 5:9](https://ref.ly/Ps5:9), [PSA 10:7](https://ref.ly/Ps10:7), [PSA 14:1–14:3](https://ref.ly/Ps14:1-Ps14:3) parallel [PSA 53:1–53:3](https://ref.ly/Ps53:1-Ps53:3); [PSA 36:1](https://ref.ly/Ps36:1), [PSA 140:3](https://ref.ly/Ps140:3); [ISA 59:7–59:8](https://ref.ly/Isa59:7-Isa59:8)

### All have sinned

**[ROM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23)** *See also* [GEN 6:11–6:12](https://ref.ly/Gen6:11-Gen6:12); [1KI 8:46](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:46) parallel [2CH 6:36](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:36); [ECC 7:20](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:20); [ISA 53:6](https://ref.ly/Isa53:6); [ROM 1:18–1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18-Rom1:32); [JAS 3:2](https://ref.ly/Jas3:2)

### Everyone is sinful in God's sight

**[1JN 1:8](https://ref.ly/1John1:8)** *See also* [PSA 130:3](https://ref.ly/Ps130:3), [PSA 143:2](https://ref.ly/Ps143:2); [PRO 20:9](https://ref.ly/Prov20:9); [ISA 64:6–64:7](https://ref.ly/Isa64:6-Isa64:7); [MAT 19:17](https://ref.ly/Matt19:17) parallels [MRK 10:18](https://ref.ly/Mark10:18), [LUK 18:19](https://ref.ly/Luke18:19); [1JN 1:10](https://ref.ly/1John1:10)

Some characters in Scripture are described as being blameless in comparison with their contemporaries
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[GEN 5:24](https://ref.ly/Gen5:24) *Enoch*; ; [GEN 6:9](https://ref.ly/Gen6:9) *Noah*; ; [1KI 15:5](https://ref.ly/1Kgs15:5) *David*

Jesus Christ alone is sinless
-----------------------------

**[HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15)**; **[1PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22)** *See also* [ISA 53:9](https://ref.ly/Isa53:9); [LUK 23:47](https://ref.ly/Luke23:47); [2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21); [HEB 7:26](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26); [1JN 3:5](https://ref.ly/1John3:5)

## 6024: sin, effects of (id: 6024)

Sin affects every level of human existence, including the sinner's relationship with God, with other human beings and with the environment.

The effects of sin on individuals
---------------------------------

### Lack of peace of mind

**[ISA 57:20–57:21](https://ref.ly/Isa57:20-Isa57:21)** *See also* [JOB 15:20–15:35](https://ref.ly/Job15:20-Job15:35); [PSA 38:5–38:8](https://ref.ly/Ps38:5-Ps38:8); [PRO 13:15–13:22](https://ref.ly/Prov13:15-Prov13:22); [LAM 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/Lam1:20-Lam1:21)

### Bondage to a continuing habit of sin

**[JHN 8:34](https://ref.ly/John8:34)** *See also* [PRO 5:22](https://ref.ly/Prov5:22); [ROM 6:16](https://ref.ly/Rom6:16); [2TI 2:16](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:16)

### Physical death

**[1CO 15:56](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:56)** *See also* [GEN 2:17](https://ref.ly/Gen2:17), [GEN 3:19](https://ref.ly/Gen3:19); [PRO 21:16](https://ref.ly/Prov21:16); [ROM 5:12–5:14](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12-Rom5:14), [ROM 6:21–6:23](https://ref.ly/Rom6:21-Rom6:23); [1CO 15:22](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:22); [JAS 1:15](https://ref.ly/Jas1:15)

### The sinful life is equivalent to death

**[EPH 2:1](https://ref.ly/Eph2:1)** *See also* [ROM 7:9](https://ref.ly/Rom7:9), [ROM 7:13](https://ref.ly/Rom7:13), [ROM 8:10](https://ref.ly/Rom8:10); [COL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Col2:13)

The effects of sin on the sinner before God
-------------------------------------------

### Uncleanness

**[ISA 64:6](https://ref.ly/Isa64:6)** *See also* [PSA 106:39](https://ref.ly/Ps106:39); [ISA 6:5](https://ref.ly/Isa6:5); [JER 2:22](https://ref.ly/Jer2:22); [LAM 1:8](https://ref.ly/Lam1:8); [MAT 15:18–15:20](https://ref.ly/Matt15:18-Matt15:20) parallel [MRK 7:20–7:23](https://ref.ly/Mark7:20-Mark7:23)

### Guilt

**[EZR 9:6](https://ref.ly/Ezra9:6)** *The prayer of Ezra.* *See also* [GEN 3:10](https://ref.ly/Gen3:10); [PSA 38:3–38:4](https://ref.ly/Ps38:3-Ps38:4), [PSA 44:15](https://ref.ly/Ps44:15); [ISA 59:12–59:13](https://ref.ly/Isa59:12-Isa59:13); [JER 3:25](https://ref.ly/Jer3:25), [JER 14:20](https://ref.ly/Jer14:20)

### Separation from God

**[ISA 59:2](https://ref.ly/Isa59:2)** *See also* [DEU 31:18](https://ref.ly/Deut31:18); [ISA 1:15](https://ref.ly/Isa1:15), [ISA 64:7](https://ref.ly/Isa64:7); [EZK 8:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek8:6); [HOS 5:6](https://ref.ly/Hos5:6); [MIC 3:4](https://ref.ly/Mic3:4); [EPH 2:12](https://ref.ly/Eph2:12)

The effects of sin on Israel
----------------------------

**[PRO 14:34](https://ref.ly/Prov14:34)** *See also* [JOS 7:1–7:16](https://ref.ly/Josh7:1-Josh7:16) *Achan's sin*; [1KI 8:33–8:40](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:33-1Kgs8:40) *the consequences of sin for Israel*; [ISA 1:4–1:9](https://ref.ly/Isa1:4-Isa1:9) *the plight of Judah*; [ROM 1:21–1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:21-Rom1:32) *the condition of humanity*

The effects of sin on the world
-------------------------------

### The ground cursed

**[GEN 3:17–3:18](https://ref.ly/Gen3:17-Gen3:18)** *See also* [JER 12:13](https://ref.ly/Jer12:13); [ROM 8:20–8:22](https://ref.ly/Rom8:20-Rom8:22)

### The land polluted

**[LEV 18:25](https://ref.ly/Lev18:25)** *See also* [GEN 4:10–4:12](https://ref.ly/Gen4:10-Gen4:12); [NUM 35:33–35:34](https://ref.ly/Num35:33-Num35:34); [PSA 106:38](https://ref.ly/Ps106:38); [ISA 24:4–24:6](https://ref.ly/Isa24:4-Isa24:6); [JER 3:1](https://ref.ly/Jer3:1)

## 6025: sin, and God's character (id: 6025)

In his righteousness and holiness, God detests sin and its effects upon humanity. In his mercy and grace, he makes available a means of atonement, by the death and resurrection of Jesus Christ.

God's character and sin
-----------------------

### God himself is perfect

**[HAB 1:13](https://ref.ly/Hab1:13)**; **[1JN 1:5](https://ref.ly/1John1:5)** *See also* [DEU 32:4](https://ref.ly/Deut32:4); [JOS 24:19](https://ref.ly/Josh24:19); [PSA 97:2](https://ref.ly/Ps97:2); [ISA 6:3](https://ref.ly/Isa6:3)

### Jesus Christ is sinless

**[1PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22)** *See also* [ISA 53:9](https://ref.ly/Isa53:9); [2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21); [HEB 1:9](https://ref.ly/Heb1:9), [HEB 7:26–7:27](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26-Heb7:27); [1JN 3:5](https://ref.ly/1John3:5)

### God's people are to be holy

**[1PE 1:15–1:16](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:15-1Pet1:16)** *See also* [LEV 11:44](https://ref.ly/Lev11:44), [LEV 11:45](https://ref.ly/Lev11:45), [LEV 19:2](https://ref.ly/Lev19:2), [LEV 20:7](https://ref.ly/Lev20:7); [MAT 5:48](https://ref.ly/Matt5:48); [1TH 4:7](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:7); [1JN 3:3](https://ref.ly/1John3:3)

God's attitude to sin
---------------------

### God knows all sin

**[JER 16:17](https://ref.ly/Jer16:17)** *See also* [JOB 10:14](https://ref.ly/Job10:14); [PSA 139:1–139:4](https://ref.ly/Ps139:1-Ps139:4); [JER 2:22](https://ref.ly/Jer2:22); [HOS 7:2](https://ref.ly/Hos7:2); [AMO 5:12](https://ref.ly/Amos5:12); [HEB 4:13](https://ref.ly/Heb4:13)

### God grieves over sin

**[GEN 6:6](https://ref.ly/Gen6:6)** *See also* [ISA 63:10](https://ref.ly/Isa63:10); [EPH 4:30](https://ref.ly/Eph4:30)

### God hates sin

**[PSA 11:5](https://ref.ly/Ps11:5)** *See also* [DEU 25:16](https://ref.ly/Deut25:16); [2SA 11:27](https://ref.ly/2Sam11:27); [PSA 5:5](https://ref.ly/Ps5:5); [PRO 6:16–6:19](https://ref.ly/Prov6:16-Prov6:19); [ZEC 8:17](https://ref.ly/Zech8:17); [LUK 16:15](https://ref.ly/Luke16:15)

### Sin provokes God's anger

**[ROM 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18)** *See also* [2CH 36:16](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:16); [EZK 20:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:8); [AMO 1:3](https://ref.ly/Amos1:3); [JHN 3:36](https://ref.ly/John3:36); [EPH 5:5–5:6](https://ref.ly/Eph5:5-Eph5:6); [COL 3:5–3:6](https://ref.ly/Col3:5-Col3:6)

### God is also merciful and gracious

**[EXO 34:6–34:7](https://ref.ly/Exod34:6-Exod34:7)** *See also* [NEH 9:17](https://ref.ly/Neh9:17), [NEH 9:31](https://ref.ly/Neh9:31); [PSA 78:38](https://ref.ly/Ps78:38), [PSA 103:8–103:14](https://ref.ly/Ps103:8-Ps103:14); [LAM 3:22–3:23](https://ref.ly/Lam3:22-Lam3:23); [MIC 7:18–7:19](https://ref.ly/Mic7:18-Mic7:19); [ROM 11:32](https://ref.ly/Rom11:32)

### God's patience with sinners

**[2PE 3:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:9)** *See also* [ROM 2:4](https://ref.ly/Rom2:4), [ROM 9:22](https://ref.ly/Rom9:22); [1TI 1:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:16)

Jesus Christ is the supreme revelation of God's love for sinners
----------------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's ministry of forgiveness

**[1TI 1:15](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:15)** *See also* [MAT 9:2](https://ref.ly/Matt9:2) parallels [MRK 2:5](https://ref.ly/Mark2:5), [LUK 5:20–5:21](https://ref.ly/Luke5:20-Luke5:21); [LUK 7:36–7:50](https://ref.ly/Luke7:36-Luke7:50), [LUK 15:1–15:10](https://ref.ly/Luke15:1-Luke15:10), [LUK 19:5–19:10](https://ref.ly/Luke19:5-Luke19:10); [JHN 8:1–8:11](https://ref.ly/John8:1-John8:11)

### God's love shown in Jesus Christ's death

**[ROM 5:8](https://ref.ly/Rom5:8)** *See also* [JHN 3:16–3:17](https://ref.ly/John3:16-John3:17); [EPH 2:4](https://ref.ly/Eph2:4); [1PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:18); [1JN 4:9–4:10](https://ref.ly/1John4:9-1John4:10)

### The risen Christ gives grace to sinful people

**[1JN 2:1](https://ref.ly/1John2:1)** *See also* [ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34); [HEB 2:17–2:18](https://ref.ly/Heb2:17-Heb2:18), [HEB 4:15–5:2](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15-Heb5:2)

## 6026: sin, God's judgment on (id: 6026)

Sin comes under the judgment of God, in that it contradicts his nature and opposes his purposes.

God's judgment on sin
---------------------

### God is the judge of sin

**[ISA 26:21](https://ref.ly/Isa26:21)** *See also* [PSA 99:8](https://ref.ly/Ps99:8); [ISA 13:11](https://ref.ly/Isa13:11); [AMO 3:14](https://ref.ly/Amos3:14); [ZEP 1:12](https://ref.ly/Zeph1:12); [1TH 4:6](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:6)

### God's judgment is certain

**[ROM 2:12](https://ref.ly/Rom2:12)** *See also* [PSA 37:38](https://ref.ly/Ps37:38); [PRO 11:21](https://ref.ly/Prov11:21); [HEB 9:27](https://ref.ly/Heb9:27)

### God's judgment is in proportion to the seriousness of the sin

**[JER 21:14](https://ref.ly/Jer21:14)** *See also* [DEU 25:2](https://ref.ly/Deut25:2); [ISA 59:18](https://ref.ly/Isa59:18); [MAT 7:1–7:5](https://ref.ly/Matt7:1-Matt7:5); [LUK 12:47–12:48](https://ref.ly/Luke12:47-Luke12:48); [ROM 2:5–2:6](https://ref.ly/Rom2:5-Rom2:6)

### God's judgment under the Sinaitic covenant

**[EXO 20:5](https://ref.ly/Exod20:5)** parallel [DEU 5:9](https://ref.ly/Deut5:9) *The Sinaitic covenant makes references to the judgment of future generations for the sins of their parents but, as a principle, this is abolished by later prophets.* [LEV 26:14–26:39](https://ref.ly/Lev26:14-Lev26:39); ; [DEU 28:15–28:68](https://ref.ly/Deut28:15-Deut28:68); [JER 31:29–31:30](https://ref.ly/Jer31:29-Jer31:30); ; [EZK 18:1–18:32](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:1-Ezek18:32)

### John the Baptist and Jesus Christ warn of judgment

**[MAT 3:10](https://ref.ly/Matt3:10)** parallel [LUK 3:9](https://ref.ly/Luke3:9) *See also* [MAT 3:12](https://ref.ly/Matt3:12), [MAT 7:19](https://ref.ly/Matt7:19), [MAT 12:36–12:37](https://ref.ly/Matt12:36-Matt12:37); [MRK 9:42–9:49](https://ref.ly/Mark9:42-Mark9:49)

Ways in which God judges sin
----------------------------

### God causes sin to bring evil to the sinner

**[2CH 6:23](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:23)** *See also* [DEU 19:19](https://ref.ly/Deut19:19); [EST 7:10](https://ref.ly/Esth7:10); [PSA 7:15–7:16](https://ref.ly/Ps7:15-Ps7:16); [ISA 30:13](https://ref.ly/Isa30:13)

### God abandons people

**[ISA 64:7](https://ref.ly/Isa64:7)** *See also* [DEU 31:17–31:18](https://ref.ly/Deut31:17-Deut31:18); [JOS 7:11–7:12](https://ref.ly/Josh7:11-Josh7:12); [LAM 4:16](https://ref.ly/Lam4:16); [EZK 39:23–39:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:23-Ezek39:24)

### Unrepentant sinners to be expelled from the church

**[MAT 18:17](https://ref.ly/Matt18:17)** *See also* [1CO 5:1–5:13](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:1-1Cor5:13)

### God exercises judgment through a country's legal system

**[1PE 2:14](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:14)** *See also* [ROM 13:3–13:4](https://ref.ly/Rom13:3-Rom13:4)

### Untimely death is God's judgment on all sin

**[GEN 2:17](https://ref.ly/Gen2:17)** *See also* [LEV 20:1–20:17](https://ref.ly/Lev20:1-Lev20:17); [1CH 10:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr10:13); [PRO 11:19](https://ref.ly/Prov11:19); [ROM 1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:32); [1CO 11:29–11:30](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:29-1Cor11:30)

### Sinners are excluded from the kingdom of God

**[REV 22:15](https://ref.ly/Rev22:15)** *See also* [1CO 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:9-1Cor6:10); [GAL 5:9–5:21](https://ref.ly/Gal5:9-Gal5:21); [REV 21:27](https://ref.ly/Rev21:27)

Occasions of God's judgment on sin
----------------------------------

### OT examples

[GEN 3:16–3:24](https://ref.ly/Gen3:16-Gen3:24) *expulsion from Eden*; ; [GEN 6:1–7:24](https://ref.ly/Gen6:1-Gen7:24) *the flood*; ; [GEN 18:20–19:29](https://ref.ly/Gen18:20-Gen19:29) *Sodom and Gomorrah*; ; [DEU 9:1–9:5](https://ref.ly/Deut9:1-Deut9:5) *The Canaanites (the Anakites were earlier inhabitants of Canaan).*; [2KI 17:7–17:23](https://ref.ly/2Kgs17:7-2Kgs17:23), [2KI 24:10–24:20](https://ref.ly/2Kgs24:10-2Kgs24:20)

[LUK 11:47–11:51](https://ref.ly/Luke11:47-Luke11:51), [LUK 13:34–13:35](https://ref.ly/Luke13:34-Luke13:35)

**[REV 21:8](https://ref.ly/Rev21:8)** *See also* [ISA 66:24](https://ref.ly/Isa66:24); [MAT 25:31–25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:46); [2TH 1:8–1:9](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:8-2Thess1:9); [2PE 3:7](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:7); [JUD 1:7](https://ref.ly/Jude1:7)

## 6027: sin, God's remedy for (id: 6027)

Under the old covenant, sin was forgiven through sacrifice, prefiguring the atoning death of Jesus Christ, which brings forgiveness of sins under the new covenant.

Atonement for sins in the OT was through the shedding of blood
--------------------------------------------------------------

**[LEV 17:11](https://ref.ly/Lev17:11)**

Kinds of sin offering in the OT
-------------------------------

### The sin offering was for unintentional sins

**[LEV 4:1–5:13](https://ref.ly/Lev4:1-Lev5:13)** *See also* [NUM 15:22–15:31](https://ref.ly/Num15:22-Num15:31)

### The guilt offering was for unintentional sins, where restitution was required

**[LEV 5:14–6:7](https://ref.ly/Lev5:14-Lev6:7)** *See also* [NUM 5:5–5:10](https://ref.ly/Num5:5-Num5:10)

### The annual Day of Atonement cleansed the nation of sin

**[LEV 16:1–16:34](https://ref.ly/Lev16:1-Lev16:34)** *See also* [EXO 30:11–30:16](https://ref.ly/Exod30:11-Exod30:16); [LEV 23:26–23:32](https://ref.ly/Lev23:26-Lev23:32); [HEB 9:7](https://ref.ly/Heb9:7)

### The priests made atonement on occasions of deliberate national sin

[NUM 16:46–16:48](https://ref.ly/Num16:46-Num16:48) *Aaron stops the plague after Korah's sin*; ; [NUM 25:13](https://ref.ly/Num25:13) *Phinehas stops the plague after Moab caused Israel to sin.*

Sacrifices of atonement needed to be accompanied by repentance and a willingness to obey
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Worshippers recognised the need for repentance and obedience

**[PRO 21:3](https://ref.ly/Prov21:3)** *See also* [PSA 40:6–40:8](https://ref.ly/Ps40:6-Ps40:8), [PSA 51:16–51:17](https://ref.ly/Ps51:16-Ps51:17)

### The prophets declared the need for obedience

**[1SA 15:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:22)** *See also* [ISA 1:11–1:17](https://ref.ly/Isa1:11-Isa1:17); [JER 7:21–7:23](https://ref.ly/Jer7:21-Jer7:23); [HOS 6:6](https://ref.ly/Hos6:6); [MIC 6:6–6:8](https://ref.ly/Mic6:6-Mic6:8)

### The prophets warned of judgment to bring people to repentance

**[2KI 17:13](https://ref.ly/2Kgs17:13)** *See also* [ISA 31:6–31:7](https://ref.ly/Isa31:6-Isa31:7); [JER 4:1–4:4](https://ref.ly/Jer4:1-Jer4:4), [JER 35:15](https://ref.ly/Jer35:15); [EZK 3:16–3:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek3:16-Ezek3:19); [JON 3:4–3:10](https://ref.ly/Jonah3:4-Jonah3:10)

The death of Jesus Christ brings forgiveness for sin
----------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ died on behalf of sinful humanity

**[ROM 5:6](https://ref.ly/Rom5:6)** *See also* [MAT 26:26–26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:26-Matt26:28); [JHN 10:11](https://ref.ly/John10:11), [JHN 15:13](https://ref.ly/John15:13); [GAL 2:20](https://ref.ly/Gal2:20)

### The early church proclaimed that Christ died for the sins of others

**[1CO 15:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:3)** *See also* [ROM 4:25](https://ref.ly/Rom4:25); [GAL 1:4](https://ref.ly/Gal1:4); [1PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:18)

### Jesus Christ bore sin on the cross

**[2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21)** *See also* [ISA 53:10–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10-Isa53:12); [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28); [1PE 2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:24)

### Jesus Christ has redeemed people by taking their place

**[MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28)** parallel [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45) *See also* [GAL 3:13](https://ref.ly/Gal3:13); [1TI 2:6](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:6); [TIT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:14)

### Jesus Christ's death is sacrificial

**[ROM 3:25](https://ref.ly/Rom3:25)** *See also* [ROM 8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:3); [1CO 5:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:7); [EPH 5:2](https://ref.ly/Eph5:2); [HEB 7:27](https://ref.ly/Heb7:27), [HEB 10:5–10:13](https://ref.ly/Heb10:5-Heb10:13); [1JN 2:2](https://ref.ly/1John2:2), [1JN 4:10](https://ref.ly/1John4:10)

### The shedding of Jesus Christ's blood brings forgiveness

**[1JN 1:7](https://ref.ly/1John1:7)** *See also* [JHN 1:29](https://ref.ly/John1:29); [EPH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Eph1:7); [HEB 9:12–9:22](https://ref.ly/Heb9:12-Heb9:22), [HEB 13:12](https://ref.ly/Heb13:12); [1PE 1:18–1:19](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:18-1Pet1:19); [REV 7:14](https://ref.ly/Rev7:14)

## 6028: sin, God's deliverance from (id: 6028)

The gospel reveals the purpose and power of God to deal with sin and all of its effects. Scripture uses a range of images to express the comprehensiveness of salvation.

God's removal of sin
--------------------

### Atonement for sin

**[ISA 6:7](https://ref.ly/Isa6:7)** *See also* [EXO 32:30](https://ref.ly/Exod32:30); [LEV 4:27–4:31](https://ref.ly/Lev4:27-Lev4:31); [PRO 16:6](https://ref.ly/Prov16:6); [ROM 3:25](https://ref.ly/Rom3:25); [HEB 2:17](https://ref.ly/Heb2:17)

### Forgiveness of sin

**[MIC 7:18](https://ref.ly/Mic7:18)**; **[ACT 13:38](https://ref.ly/Acts13:38)** *See also* [1KI 8:35–8:36](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:35-1Kgs8:36); [2CH 30:18–30:20](https://ref.ly/2Chr30:18-2Chr30:20); [PSA 103:2–103:3](https://ref.ly/Ps103:2-Ps103:3); [ISA 33:24](https://ref.ly/Isa33:24), [ISA 55:7](https://ref.ly/Isa55:7); [JOL 3:21](https://ref.ly/Joel3:21); [MAT 26:27–26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:27-Matt26:28); [LUK 24:46–24:47](https://ref.ly/Luke24:46-Luke24:47); [EPH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Eph1:7); [1JN 1:9](https://ref.ly/1John1:9)

### Cancellation of a debt

**[MAT 6:12](https://ref.ly/Matt6:12)** *See also* [MAT 18:21–18:35](https://ref.ly/Matt18:21-Matt18:35); [LUK 7:41–7:50](https://ref.ly/Luke7:41-Luke7:50)

### A covering over of sin

**[1PE 4:8](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:8)** *There is a close relation between “covering over sin” and “atoning for sin”.* *See also* [PSA 32:1](https://ref.ly/Ps32:1), [PSA 85:2](https://ref.ly/Ps85:2); [JAS 5:20](https://ref.ly/Jas5:20)

### The taking away of sin

**[PSA 103:12](https://ref.ly/Ps103:12)** *See also* [2SA 12:13](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:13); [ISA 6:6–6:7](https://ref.ly/Isa6:6-Isa6:7); [ZEC 3:4](https://ref.ly/Zech3:4); [JHN 1:29](https://ref.ly/John1:29); [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28); [1JN 3:5](https://ref.ly/1John3:5)

### Remembering sin no more

**[ISA 43:25](https://ref.ly/Isa43:25)** *See also* [PSA 25:7](https://ref.ly/Ps25:7); [JER 31:33–31:34](https://ref.ly/Jer31:33-Jer31:34); [2CO 5:19](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:19)

--------------------------------

## 6030: sin, avoidance of (id: 6030)

God calls his people to avoid sin, and through Jesus Christ gives them the inner power to be victorious over it.

God's people are to resist sin
------------------------------

**[1PE 2:11](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:11)** *See also* [PSA 97:10](https://ref.ly/Ps97:10); [PRO 4:23–4:27](https://ref.ly/Prov4:23-Prov4:27); [1CO 15:34](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:34); [EPH 4:25–5:20](https://ref.ly/Eph4:25-Eph5:20); [JAS 1:21](https://ref.ly/Jas1:21)

The Christian life is a constant struggle against sin
-----------------------------------------------------

**[HEB 3:13](https://ref.ly/Heb3:13)** *See also* [ACT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Acts20:28); [ROM 7:14–7:25](https://ref.ly/Rom7:14-Rom7:25); [EPH 6:10–6:18](https://ref.ly/Eph6:10-Eph6:18); [1PE 5:8–5:9](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:8-1Pet5:9)

God helps his people to resist sin
----------------------------------

### Release from sin through Jesus Christ's death

**[1PE 2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:24)** *See also* [ROM 6:1–6:7](https://ref.ly/Rom6:1-Rom6:7); [GAL 2:20](https://ref.ly/Gal2:20), [GAL 5:24](https://ref.ly/Gal5:24); [COL 2:11–2:12](https://ref.ly/Col2:11-Col2:12)

### The avoidance of sin through new life in Jesus Christ

**[1JN 3:9](https://ref.ly/1John3:9)** *See also* [2CO 5:17](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:17); [1PE 1:23](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:23); [1JN 3:6](https://ref.ly/1John3:6), [1JN 5:18](https://ref.ly/1John5:18)

Believers co\-operate with Jesus Christ to avoid sin
----------------------------------------------------

**[PHP 2:12–2:13](https://ref.ly/Phil2:12-Phil2:13)**

### Believers are to put to death what is sinful in them

**[COL 3:5](https://ref.ly/Col3:5)** *See also* [ROM 6:11–6:14](https://ref.ly/Rom6:11-Rom6:14), [ROM 8:13](https://ref.ly/Rom8:13)

### Believers are to exchange sinful for righteous behaviour

**[ROM 13:12–13:14](https://ref.ly/Rom13:12-Rom13:14)** *The words used here, and in similar passages, are those used for “taking off” old clothes and “putting on” new ones.* *See also* [EPH 4:22–4:24](https://ref.ly/Eph4:22-Eph4:24); [COL 3:7–3:10](https://ref.ly/Col3:7-Col3:10); [1TI 6:11](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:11); [2TI 2:22](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:22)

### Believers are to allow the Spirit to inform and direct their conduct

**[ROM 12:2](https://ref.ly/Rom12:2)** *See also* [ROM 8:5–8:8](https://ref.ly/Rom8:5-Rom8:8); [GAL 5:16–5:25](https://ref.ly/Gal5:16-Gal5:25)

-------------------------------------------------

### Meditation on Scripture

**[PSA 119:11](https://ref.ly/Ps119:11)** *See also* [PSA 18:22–18:23](https://ref.ly/Ps18:22-Ps18:23); [MAT 4:1–4:11](https://ref.ly/Matt4:1-Matt4:11) parallel [LUK 4:1–4:13](https://ref.ly/Luke4:1-Luke4:13); [2TI 3:16–3:17](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:16-2Tim3:17)

**[ROM 6:19](https://ref.ly/Rom6:19)** *See also* [PSA 34:14](https://ref.ly/Ps34:14); [ISA 1:16–1:17](https://ref.ly/Isa1:16-Isa1:17); [AMO 5:14–5:15](https://ref.ly/Amos5:14-Amos5:15); [1TH 5:22](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:22); [3JN 1:11](https://ref.ly/3John1:11)

Incentives for avoiding sin
---------------------------

### The fear of God

**[PRO 16:6](https://ref.ly/Prov16:6)** *See also* [EXO 20:20](https://ref.ly/Exod20:20); [PRO 3:7](https://ref.ly/Prov3:7), [PRO 8:13](https://ref.ly/Prov8:13)

**[1PE 2:15](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:15)** *See also* [1PE 3:1–3:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:1-1Pet3:2), [1PE 3:15–3:16](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:15-1Pet3:16)

The role of others in avoiding sin
----------------------------------

### Bad company is to be avoided

**[1CO 15:33](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:33)** *See also* [DEU 7:1–7:4](https://ref.ly/Deut7:1-Deut7:4); [PSA 1:1](https://ref.ly/Ps1:1); [PRO 1:10](https://ref.ly/Prov1:10); [1CO 5:1–5:13](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:1-1Cor5:13)

### A good example is to be followed

**[1CO 11:1](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:1)** *See also* [PHP 3:17](https://ref.ly/Phil3:17), [PHP 4:9](https://ref.ly/Phil4:9); [HEB 12:1–12:3](https://ref.ly/Heb12:1-Heb12:3); [1PE 4:1–4:3](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:1-1Pet4:3)

### Believers are to support one another

**[JAS 5:19–5:20](https://ref.ly/Jas5:19-Jas5:20)** *See also* [MAT 18:15–18:17](https://ref.ly/Matt18:15-Matt18:17); [GAL 6:1–6:2](https://ref.ly/Gal6:1-Gal6:2); [1TI 5:20](https://ref.ly/1Tim5:20); [HEB 3:12](https://ref.ly/Heb3:12)

## 6040: sinners (id: 6040)

All who have sinned. The term tends to be used in particular of those regarded as outside God's covenant of grace, whose sins are therefore not forgiven.

The universality of sinful behaviour
------------------------------------

### Only Jesus Christ is sinless

**[1PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22)** *See also* [ISA 53:9](https://ref.ly/Isa53:9); [2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21); [HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15), [HEB 7:26](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26); [1JN 3:5](https://ref.ly/1John3:5)

### Everyone else has sinned

**[GAL 3:22](https://ref.ly/Gal3:22)** *See also* [1KI 8:46](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:46); [ROM 3:9–3:19](https://ref.ly/Rom3:9-Rom3:19), [ROM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23), [ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12), [ROM 5:19](https://ref.ly/Rom5:19)

God's mercy towards sinners
---------------------------

### God graciously extends mercy to sinners within the covenant

**[PSA 25:8–25:10](https://ref.ly/Ps25:8-Ps25:10)** *See also* [1KI 8:30](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:30); [PSA 86:5](https://ref.ly/Ps86:5), [PSA 130:8](https://ref.ly/Ps130:8); [DAN 9:9](https://ref.ly/Dan9:9); [1JN 1:9](https://ref.ly/1John1:9)

### Jesus Christ died for sinners

**[ROM 5:8](https://ref.ly/Rom5:8)**; **[1TI 1:15](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:15)** *See also* [ROM 8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:3)

Sinners as those whose behaviour excludes them from God's covenant
------------------------------------------------------------------

### Prostitutes, tax collectors, idolatrous Gentiles and the ungodly

**[LUK 15:1](https://ref.ly/Luke15:1)** *See also* [DEU 23:17–23:18](https://ref.ly/Deut23:17-Deut23:18); [1SA 15:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:18); [LUK 3:12](https://ref.ly/Luke3:12), [LUK 7:37–7:38](https://ref.ly/Luke7:37-Luke7:38); [GAL 2:15](https://ref.ly/Gal2:15); [1TH 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:5); [1PE 4:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:18); [PRO 11:31](https://ref.ly/Prov11:31); [2PE 2:5–2:6](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:5-2Pet2:6)

### Such sinners shunned by the Jews

**[LUK 7:39](https://ref.ly/Luke7:39)** *See also* [PSA 1:1](https://ref.ly/Ps1:1); [PRO 1:10–1:16](https://ref.ly/Prov1:10-Prov1:16)

The judgment of sinners
-----------------------

### Prayers seeking their judgment

**[PSA 104:35](https://ref.ly/Ps104:35)** *See also* [PSA 109:6–109:20](https://ref.ly/Ps109:6-Ps109:20), [PSA 137:7–137:9](https://ref.ly/Ps137:7-Ps137:9), [PSA 139:19](https://ref.ly/Ps139:19)

**[ISA 59:2](https://ref.ly/Isa59:2)** *See also* [PSA 66:18](https://ref.ly/Ps66:18); [PRO 15:29](https://ref.ly/Prov15:29); [ISA 1:15](https://ref.ly/Isa1:15); [JHN 9:31](https://ref.ly/John9:31); [1CO 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:9-1Cor6:10)

### Prophecies of their judgment

**[ISA 1:28](https://ref.ly/Isa1:28)** *See also* [ISA 13:9](https://ref.ly/Isa13:9), [ISA 33:14](https://ref.ly/Isa33:14); [JER 4:18](https://ref.ly/Jer4:18); [AMO 9:10](https://ref.ly/Amos9:10)

### Their final judgment

**[2PE 3:7](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:7)** *See also* [ISA 66:24](https://ref.ly/Isa66:24); [2TH 1:8–1:9](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:8-2Thess1:9); [2PE 2:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:9); [JUD 1:15](https://ref.ly/Jude1:15)

Jesus Christ's attitude towards sinners
---------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's association with sinners

**[MAT 9:9–9:13](https://ref.ly/Matt9:9-Matt9:13)** parallels [MRK 2:14–2:17](https://ref.ly/Mark2:14-Mark2:17), [LUK 5:27–5:32](https://ref.ly/Luke5:27-Luke5:32) *Jesus Christ's attitude and behaviour were radically different from that of his contemporaries.* *See also* [LUK 15:1–15:10](https://ref.ly/Luke15:1-Luke15:10), [LUK 19:5–19:10](https://ref.ly/Luke19:5-Luke19:10); [ROM 5:8](https://ref.ly/Rom5:8); [1TI 1:15–1:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:15-1Tim1:16)

### Jesus Christ extended God's forgiveness to sinners and welcomed them into his kingdom

**[MAT 21:31–21:32](https://ref.ly/Matt21:31-Matt21:32)** *See also* [MAT 9:2–9:7](https://ref.ly/Matt9:2-Matt9:7) parallels [MRK 2:3–2:12](https://ref.ly/Mark2:3-Mark2:12), [LUK 5:18–5:25](https://ref.ly/Luke5:18-Luke5:25); [LUK 7:40–7:50](https://ref.ly/Luke7:40-Luke7:50), [LUK 15:11–15:32](https://ref.ly/Luke15:11-Luke15:32), [LUK 18:9–18:14](https://ref.ly/Luke18:9-Luke18:14), [LUK 19:9](https://ref.ly/Luke19:9); [JHN 8:3–8:11](https://ref.ly/John8:3-John8:11)

### Jesus Christ's behaviour led to accusations that he himself was a sinner

[JHN 9:16](https://ref.ly/John9:16), [JHN 9:24](https://ref.ly/John9:24)

### Jesus Christ's refusal to accept sinful behaviour

**[JHN 8:10–8:11](https://ref.ly/John8:10-John8:11)** *See also* [MAT 4:17](https://ref.ly/Matt4:17), [MAT 18:8–18:9](https://ref.ly/Matt18:8-Matt18:9) parallel [MRK 9:43–9:48](https://ref.ly/Mark9:43-Mark9:48); [JHN 5:14](https://ref.ly/John5:14)

### Jesus Christ's use of the example of sinners to teach his disciples

**[LUK 6:32–6:34](https://ref.ly/Luke6:32-Luke6:34)** parallel [MAT 5:46–5:47](https://ref.ly/Matt5:46-Matt5:47) *See also* [LUK 16:1–16:9](https://ref.ly/Luke16:1-Luke16:9)

---------------------

**[JAS 5:19–5:20](https://ref.ly/Jas5:19-Jas5:20)** *See also* [PSA 51:13](https://ref.ly/Ps51:13); [MAT 18:12–18:15](https://ref.ly/Matt18:12-Matt18:15); [GAL 6:1](https://ref.ly/Gal6:1)

## 6103: abomination (id: 6103)

That which is utterly detestable in the sight of God, particularly sin and idolatry. Daniel predicts the establishment of an “abomination that causes desolation” on the temple mount and Jesus Christ reiterates this prophecy.

Sin is an abomination
---------------------

### God detests it

**[LEV 20:13](https://ref.ly/Lev20:13)**; **[PRO 26:24–26:26](https://ref.ly/Prov26:24-Prov26:26)** *See also* [LEV 18:26–18:30](https://ref.ly/Lev18:26-Lev18:30); [PRO 6:16–6:19](https://ref.ly/Prov6:16-Prov6:19), [PRO 28:9](https://ref.ly/Prov28:9); [ISA 66:3–66:4](https://ref.ly/Isa66:3-Isa66:4)

### The abomination of Babylon the Great

**[REV 17:3–17:6](https://ref.ly/Rev17:3-Rev17:6)** *See also* [JER 51:6–51:8](https://ref.ly/Jer51:6-Jer51:8); [REV 14:8](https://ref.ly/Rev14:8), [REV 19:1–19:2](https://ref.ly/Rev19:1-Rev19:2)

Idolatry is an abomination
--------------------------

**[JER 32:32–32:35](https://ref.ly/Jer32:32-Jer32:35)** [DEU 7:25–7:26](https://ref.ly/Deut7:25-Deut7:26), [DEU 12:31](https://ref.ly/Deut12:31), [DEU 18:9–18:13](https://ref.ly/Deut18:9-Deut18:13), [DEU 27:15](https://ref.ly/Deut27:15), [DEU 29:17–29:18](https://ref.ly/Deut29:17-Deut29:18); [DEU 32:15–32:16](https://ref.ly/Deut32:15-Deut32:16); [1KI 11:4–11:8](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:4-1Kgs11:8); ; [2KI 23:13](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:13); [ISA 44:19](https://ref.ly/Isa44:19); ; [JER 4:1–4:2](https://ref.ly/Jer4:1-Jer4:2), [JER 7:30](https://ref.ly/Jer7:30), [JER 16:18](https://ref.ly/Jer16:18); ; [EZK 5:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek5:9), [EZK 7:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek7:20), [EZK 8:5–8:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek8:5-Ezek8:18) *idolatry in the temple*; ; [EZK 11:17–11:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek11:17-Ezek11:21), [EZK 20:30](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:30); ; [HOS 9:10](https://ref.ly/Hos9:10); ; [1PE 4:3](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:3)

Unclean animals are an abomination
----------------------------------

**[ISA 66:17](https://ref.ly/Isa66:17)** *See also* [LEV 7:21](https://ref.ly/Lev7:21), [LEV 11:13–11:20](https://ref.ly/Lev11:13-Lev11:20), [LEV 11:41–11:42](https://ref.ly/Lev11:41-Lev11:42); [ISA 65:2–65:5](https://ref.ly/Isa65:2-Isa65:5); [REV 18:2](https://ref.ly/Rev18:2)

The abomination that causes desolation
--------------------------------------

**[DAN 9:25–9:27](https://ref.ly/Dan9:25-Dan9:27)** *See also* [DAN 11:29–11:32](https://ref.ly/Dan11:29-Dan11:32), [DAN 12:11–12:12](https://ref.ly/Dan12:11-Dan12:12); [MAT 24:15–24:21](https://ref.ly/Matt24:15-Matt24:21) parallel [MRK 13:14–13:19](https://ref.ly/Mark13:14-Mark13:19); [REV 13:14–13:15](https://ref.ly/Rev13:14-Rev13:15)

## 6106: addiction (id: 6106)

The devotion of a person to something, whether sin in general or food, alcohol or wealth in particular, so as to become dependent upon it. A person will never be satisfied in such a state of slavery. The answer to addiction is self\-control through the resources of the new life in Christ.

Addiction is the consequence of sin
-----------------------------------

**[2PE 2:19](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:19)** *See also* [JHN 8:34](https://ref.ly/John8:34)

Addiction to food, alcohol or drugs is to become dependent upon them
--------------------------------------------------------------------

**[PHP 3:18–3:19](https://ref.ly/Phil3:18-Phil3:19)** *See also* [ISA 5:11](https://ref.ly/Isa5:11), [ISA 28:7–28:8](https://ref.ly/Isa28:7-Isa28:8), [ISA 56:12](https://ref.ly/Isa56:12); [TIT 2:3](https://ref.ly/Titus2:3)

Addiction to wealth is to be controlled by it
---------------------------------------------

**[MRK 10:21–10:22](https://ref.ly/Mark10:21-Mark10:22)** parallel [LUK 18:22–18:23](https://ref.ly/Luke18:22-Luke18:23) *See also* [MAT 26:14–26:16](https://ref.ly/Matt26:14-Matt26:16) parallels [MRK 14:10–14:11](https://ref.ly/Mark14:10-Mark14:11), [LUK 22:3–22:6](https://ref.ly/Luke22:3-Luke22:6); [ACT 16:19](https://ref.ly/Acts16:19), [ACT 24:26](https://ref.ly/Acts24:26); [2PE 2:15](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:15)

Addiction never satisfies
-------------------------

### Addiction to sinful habits does not satisfy

**[ROM 6:20–6:21](https://ref.ly/Rom6:20-Rom6:21)**

### Addiction to food, alcohol or drugs does not satisfy

**[ECC 6:7](https://ref.ly/Eccl6:7)** *See also* [PRO 20:1](https://ref.ly/Prov20:1), [PRO 21:17](https://ref.ly/Prov21:17), [PRO 23:20–23:21](https://ref.ly/Prov23:20-Prov23:21), [PRO 23:29–23:35](https://ref.ly/Prov23:29-Prov23:35); [HOS 4:10–4:11](https://ref.ly/Hos4:10-Hos4:11) parallel [MAT 19:21–19:22](https://ref.ly/Matt19:21-Matt19:22)

### Addiction to wealth does not satisfy

**[ECC 5:10](https://ref.ly/Eccl5:10)** *See also* [1TI 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:9-1Tim6:10); [JAS 5:1–5:3](https://ref.ly/Jas5:1-Jas5:3)

The answer to addiction: self\-control through the new life in Christ
---------------------------------------------------------------------

## 6109: alienation (id: 6109)

A state of being separate or apart from something or someone, often accompanied by an awareness of the separation. Human beings are alienated from God on account of sin. Alienation is also encountered in other areas of life, including relations between believers, and between believers and secular society.

Alienation from God because of sin
----------------------------------

### Sin causes separation from God

**[GAL 5:4](https://ref.ly/Gal5:4)** *Those seeking to justify themselves cut themselves off from Jesus Christ's saving work*; **[COL 1:21](https://ref.ly/Col1:21)** *See also* [ISA 59:1–59:2](https://ref.ly/Isa59:1-Isa59:2); [EZK 39:23–39:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:23-Ezek39:24)

### Seen in discomfort in God's presence

**[GEN 3:8–3:10](https://ref.ly/Gen3:8-Gen3:10)** *See also* [ISA 6:5](https://ref.ly/Isa6:5); [LUK 5:8](https://ref.ly/Luke5:8)

### Seen in defeat in battle

**[DEU 1:42](https://ref.ly/Deut1:42)** *See also* [NUM 14:41–14:45](https://ref.ly/Num14:41-Num14:45); [JOS 7:11–7:12](https://ref.ly/Josh7:11-Josh7:12); [JDG 2:11–2:15](https://ref.ly/Judg2:11-Judg2:15)

### Seen in unanswered prayer

**[ISA 59:1–59:2](https://ref.ly/Isa59:1-Isa59:2)** *See also* [DEU 1:45](https://ref.ly/Deut1:45); [PSA 66:18](https://ref.ly/Ps66:18); [PRO 1:28–1:30](https://ref.ly/Prov1:28-Prov1:30); [ISA 1:15](https://ref.ly/Isa1:15)

### Seen in unaccepted worship

[ISA 1:11–1:14](https://ref.ly/Isa1:11-Isa1:14); ; [AMO 5:21–5:23](https://ref.ly/Amos5:21-Amos5:23); ; [MAL 1:10](https://ref.ly/Mal1:10)

### Seen in lost closeness with God

[GEN 3:23–3:24](https://ref.ly/Gen3:23-Gen3:24); ; [EXO 33:3](https://ref.ly/Exod33:3); ; [ISA 64:7](https://ref.ly/Isa64:7); ; [EZK 8:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek8:6); ; [HOS 5:6](https://ref.ly/Hos5:6); ; [JON 1:3](https://ref.ly/Jonah1:3)

------------------------------

## 6112: banishment (id: 6112)

A form of punishment in which the guilty party is expelled from a region and forbidden to return. An important example is the banishment of Adam and Eve from Eden as a result of their disobedience to God.

Banishment is a punishment for disobedience
-------------------------------------------

**[EZR 7:26](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:26)** *See also* [EXO 12:15](https://ref.ly/Exod12:15), [EXO 31:14](https://ref.ly/Exod31:14); [LEV 7:20–7:21](https://ref.ly/Lev7:20-Lev7:21); [NUM 15:30](https://ref.ly/Num15:30)

Banishment by God
-----------------

### Adam and Eve were banished from Eden because of their disobedience

**[GEN 3:22–3:24](https://ref.ly/Gen3:22-Gen3:24)**

### God banished kings as a punishment

Nebuchadnezzar was banished from every human being because of his sin: [DAN 4:25](https://ref.ly/Dan4:25), [DAN 4:32–4:33](https://ref.ly/Dan4:32-Dan4:33); [EZK 28:16–28:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek28:16-Ezek28:17) *The king of Tyre was banished from God's presence because of his sin.*

### God punished the people of Judah by banishing them from their land

**[JER 23:39](https://ref.ly/Jer23:39)** *God also promised their return ([Jer 32:37](https://ref.ly/Jer32:37)).* *See also* [JER 8:3](https://ref.ly/Jer8:3), [JER 24:9](https://ref.ly/Jer24:9), [JER 25:10](https://ref.ly/Jer25:10), [JER 27:10](https://ref.ly/Jer27:10)

### At the final judgment, God will banish all evildoers

**[MAT 7:23](https://ref.ly/Matt7:23)** *See also* [MAT 8:12](https://ref.ly/Matt8:12), [MAT 22:13](https://ref.ly/Matt22:13), [MAT 25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:46)

Kings used banishment as a punishment
-------------------------------------

Saul expelled all mediums and spiritists from the land: [1SA 28:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam28:3), [1SA 28:9](https://ref.ly/1Sam28:9); [1KI 15:12](https://ref.ly/1Kgs15:12) *Asa banished all the shrine\-prostitutes from the land.*

The psalmists recognised banishment as the severest of punishments
------------------------------------------------------------------

[PSA 5:10](https://ref.ly/Ps5:10), [PSA 31:22](https://ref.ly/Ps31:22), [PSA 37:22](https://ref.ly/Ps37:22), [PSA 37:28](https://ref.ly/Ps37:28), [PSA 37:34](https://ref.ly/Ps37:34), [PSA 37:38](https://ref.ly/Ps37:38), [PSA 51:11](https://ref.ly/Ps51:11), [PSA 71:9](https://ref.ly/Ps71:9), [PSA 125:5](https://ref.ly/Ps125:5); ; [JON 2:4](https://ref.ly/Jonah2:4) *This portion of the book of Jonah is written in the same manner as the Psalms, i.e., as Hebrew poetry.*

The church is to use banishment as a means of discipline
--------------------------------------------------------

**[1CO 5:12–5:13](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:12-1Cor5:13)** *See also* [DEU 17:7](https://ref.ly/Deut17:7), [DEU 19:19](https://ref.ly/Deut19:19), [DEU 21:21](https://ref.ly/Deut21:21), [DEU 22:21](https://ref.ly/Deut22:21), [DEU 22:24](https://ref.ly/Deut22:24), [DEU 24:7](https://ref.ly/Deut24:7)

* **Associated Passages:** Ezra 7:26; Exodus 12:15; Exodus 31:14; Leviticus 7:20-21; Numbers 15:30; Genesis 3:22-24; Daniel 4:25; Daniel 4:32-33; Ezekiel 28:16-17; Jeremiah 23:39; Jeremiah 32:37; Jeremiah 8:3; Jeremiah 24:9; Jeremiah 25:10; Jeremiah 27:10; Matthew 7:23; Matthew 8:12; Matthew 22:13; Matthew 25:46; 1 Samuel 28:3; 1 Samuel 28:9; 1 Kings 15:12; Psalms 5:10; Psalms 31:22; Psalms 37:22; Psalms 37:28; Psalms 37:34; Psalms 37:38; Psalms 51:11; Psalms 71:9; Psalms 125:5; Jonah 2:4; 1 Corinthians 5:12-13; Deuteronomy 17:7; Deuteronomy 19:19; Deuteronomy 21:21; Deuteronomy 22:21; Deuteronomy 22:24; Deuteronomy 24:7

## 6115: blame (id: 6115)

The state of having been accused, correctly or incorrectly, of doing something wrong. Guilt is felt as a result of having been justly blamed for a crime or wrong against a person. Scripture portrays blaming others as a natural human reaction to events. Blame may often be apportioned by people on the basis of a misunderstanding, whereas God's blame of people is just. Christians should seek to lead blameless lives.

Blaming others: a basic human characteristic since the fall
-----------------------------------------------------------

**[GEN 3:12–3:13](https://ref.ly/Gen3:12-Gen3:13)** [NUM 20:5](https://ref.ly/Num20:5), [NUM 21:5](https://ref.ly/Num21:5); ; [JOS 22:15–22:18](https://ref.ly/Josh22:15-Josh22:18); ; [1SA 22:13–22:15](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:13-1Sam22:15); ; [2SA 3:8](https://ref.ly/2Sam3:8); ; [1KI 18:17–18:18](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:17-1Kgs18:18); ; [NEH 5:4–5:5](https://ref.ly/Neh5:4-Neh5:5); ; [JOB 4:5–4:7](https://ref.ly/Job4:5-Job4:7), [JOB 8:6](https://ref.ly/Job8:6), [JOB 11:14–11:15](https://ref.ly/Job11:14-Job11:15); ; [JER 38:4](https://ref.ly/Jer38:4); ; [JHN 9:1–9:2](https://ref.ly/John9:1-John9:2), [JHN 11:21](https://ref.ly/John11:21); ; [ACT 6:1](https://ref.ly/Acts6:1)

-----------

## 6118: blemish (id: 6118)

A mark or stain which spoils something or lessens its value. The term is often used symbolically to refer to sin. The OT sacrificial system specified that only unblemished animals should be sacrificed.

A blemish is ritually unacceptable
----------------------------------

### In animals to be sacrified

**[DEU 15:21](https://ref.ly/Deut15:21)**; **[MAL 1:13–1:14](https://ref.ly/Mal1:13-Mal1:14)** *See also* [EXO 12:5](https://ref.ly/Exod12:5); [LEV 22:20–22:25](https://ref.ly/Lev22:20-Lev22:25); [DEU 17:1](https://ref.ly/Deut17:1)

### In priests offering sacrifices

**[LEV 21:17–21:23](https://ref.ly/Lev21:17-Lev21:23)**

A blemish or stain as a symbol of sin
-------------------------------------

**[JER 2:22](https://ref.ly/Jer2:22)** *See also* [ISA 59:3](https://ref.ly/Isa59:3); [JUD 1:23](https://ref.ly/Jude1:23)

### Sinful people represented as blemishes

**[2PE 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:13)** *See also* [JUD 1:12](https://ref.ly/Jude1:12)

Without blemish: physical or moral perfection
---------------------------------------------

### Absalom

[2SA 14:25](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:25)

### Daniel and his companions

[DAN 1:3–1:4](https://ref.ly/Dan1:3-Dan1:4)

**[1PE 1:18–1:19](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:18-1Pet1:19)** *See also* [HEB 9:12–9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:12-Heb9:14)

## 6121: boasting (id: 6121)

Negatively, conceitedly praising oneself. Positively, trusting and exulting in who God is, and what he has done.

Boasting condemned
------------------

**[1JN 2:16](https://ref.ly/1John2:16)** *See also* [PSA 10:2–10:6](https://ref.ly/Ps10:2-Ps10:6), [PSA 12:3–12:4](https://ref.ly/Ps12:3-Ps12:4), [PSA 52:1](https://ref.ly/Ps52:1), [PSA 94:4](https://ref.ly/Ps94:4); [HAB 1:10–1:11](https://ref.ly/Hab1:10-Hab1:11); [ROM 1:29–1:30](https://ref.ly/Rom1:29-Rom1:30); [2TI 3:1–3:2](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:1-2Tim3:2)

## 6124: condemnation (id: 6124)

An act of judgment, in which someone rebukes and denounces the actions and motivations of others. Scripture stresses the righteousness and trustworthiness of divine condemnation but notes how human judgments are often tainted and distorted by sin.

* **Associated Articles:** 6125: condemnation, divine (ID: `6125@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6126: condemnation, human (ID: `6126@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6125: condemnation, divine (id: 6125)

God's righteous condemnation is directed against human sin and wickedness.

--------------------------------------

**[ROM 1:18–1:20](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18-Rom1:20)** *See also* [REV 16:1–16:7](https://ref.ly/Rev16:1-Rev16:7)

## 6126: condemnation, human (id: 6126)

The passing of judgment on others. This is valid when authorised by God, but otherwise it is frequently partial, godless and self\-protecting, and therefore unacceptable.

## 6133: coveting (id: 6133)

Desiring to possess something at the expense of the legitimate owner.

* **Associated Articles:** 6134: coveting, prohibition of (ID: `6134@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6135: coveting, and other sins (ID: `6135@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6134: coveting, prohibition of (id: 6134)

Coveting is forbidden by God and can lead to terrible consequences. It occasionally refers to a commendable earnest desiring.

Coveting is forbidden by God
----------------------------

### In the Ten Commandments

**[EXO 20:17](https://ref.ly/Exod20:17)** parallel [DEU 5:21](https://ref.ly/Deut5:21)**[ROM 7:7–7:8](https://ref.ly/Rom7:7-Rom7:8)** *Coveting is provoked by the law that forbids it.* *See also* [ROM 13:9–13:10](https://ref.ly/Rom13:9-Rom13:10)

### Through the prophets

[ISA 5:8](https://ref.ly/Isa5:8), [ISA 57:17](https://ref.ly/Isa57:17); ; [EZK 33:31](https://ref.ly/Ezek33:31); ; [AMO 2:6](https://ref.ly/Amos2:6), [AMO 5:11–5:12](https://ref.ly/Amos5:11-Amos5:12), [AMO 8:5–8:6](https://ref.ly/Amos8:5-Amos8:6); ; [MIC 2:2](https://ref.ly/Mic2:2)

Love of money is covetousness
-----------------------------

### It is a source of evil

**[LUK 16:14](https://ref.ly/Luke16:14)**; **[JHN 12:5–12:6](https://ref.ly/John12:5-John12:6)** *See also* [MAT 23:25](https://ref.ly/Matt23:25) parallel [LUK 11:39](https://ref.ly/Luke11:39); [2PE 2:3](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:3), [2PE 2:14](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:14) *False teachers are “experts in greed”.*

### Believers must not be lovers of money

-----------------------

-----------------------------------

## 6139: deadness, spiritual (id: 6139)

Being morally and spiritually without life, therefore without a relationship with God. This condition, being the result of original sin, brings wrath and judgment and can be changed only by the sovereign, intervening grace of God.

Spiritual deadness is humanity's condition by nature
----------------------------------------------------

### It is linked to physical death

**[GEN 2:17](https://ref.ly/Gen2:17)** *See also* [GEN 3:3](https://ref.ly/Gen3:3), [GEN 3:19](https://ref.ly/Gen3:19); [PRO 11:19](https://ref.ly/Prov11:19); [EZK 18:20–18:31](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:20-Ezek18:31); [JHN 8:21–8:24](https://ref.ly/John8:21-John8:24); [ROM 1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:32), [ROM 6:23](https://ref.ly/Rom6:23)

### It is the universal consequence of sin

**[EPH 2:1](https://ref.ly/Eph2:1)** *See also* [GEN 8:21](https://ref.ly/Gen8:21); [1CH 10:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr10:13); [PSA 51:5](https://ref.ly/Ps51:5), [PSA 58:3](https://ref.ly/Ps58:3); [PRO 21:16](https://ref.ly/Prov21:16); [JHN 6:53](https://ref.ly/John6:53); [ROM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23), [ROM 5:12–5:13](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12-Rom5:13), [ROM 5:17](https://ref.ly/Rom5:17); [COL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Col2:13)

### It is confirmed in the law

**[ROM 5:20](https://ref.ly/Rom5:20)** *See also* [ROM 7:4–7:12](https://ref.ly/Rom7:4-Rom7:12), [ROM 8:2–8:4](https://ref.ly/Rom8:2-Rom8:4); [GAL 2:19](https://ref.ly/Gal2:19)

### It is evidenced in the human mind

[ROM 8:6](https://ref.ly/Rom8:6); ; [2CO 4:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:4); ; [COL 1:21](https://ref.ly/Col1:21); ; [TIT 1:15](https://ref.ly/Titus1:15)

### It is evidenced in the human body

**[ROM 7:24](https://ref.ly/Rom7:24)** *See also* [ROM 6:12–6:14](https://ref.ly/Rom6:12-Rom6:14), [ROM 6:16](https://ref.ly/Rom6:16), [ROM 8:10](https://ref.ly/Rom8:10); [1CO 15:50](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:50); [2CO 5:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:10); [GAL 6:7–6:8](https://ref.ly/Gal6:7-Gal6:8); [EPH 4:22](https://ref.ly/Eph4:22); [1TI 5:6](https://ref.ly/1Tim5:6); [JAS 3:6](https://ref.ly/Jas3:6)

----------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------

## 6142: decay (id: 6142)

As a consequence of the fall, all created things have a tendency to waste away and spoil. Jesus Christ brings deliverance from this.

Decay was decreed as a result of the fall
-----------------------------------------

### In human beings

**[GEN 2:17](https://ref.ly/Gen2:17)**

### In the world

**[GEN 3:17–3:19](https://ref.ly/Gen3:17-Gen3:19)** *See also* [ROM 8:20](https://ref.ly/Rom8:20)

-------------------------------

## 6145: deceit (id: 6145)

Behaviour, in words or actions, which is deliberately intended to make people believe things that are not true.

* **Associated Articles:** 6146: deceit, and God's nature (ID: `6146@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6147: deceit, practice of (ID: `6147@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6146: deceit, and God's nature (id: 6146)

Deceit is totally contrary to the nature and purposes of God. The gospel is grounded in the complete truthfulness and trustworthiness of God, whereas sin is based upon self\-deception.

God's nature and purposes are not based on deception
----------------------------------------------------

### Deceit is contrary to the nature of God

**[TIT 1:2](https://ref.ly/Titus1:2)** *See also* [JHN 16:13](https://ref.ly/John16:13); [1PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22)

### God cannot be deceived

**[1CH 28:9](https://ref.ly/1Chr28:9)** *See also* [PSA 139:1](https://ref.ly/Ps139:1); [ACT 5:3](https://ref.ly/Acts5:3); [1CO 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor4:5)

Jesus Christ does not deceive
-----------------------------

[ISA 53:9](https://ref.ly/Isa53:9)

### Satan's power rests on deception

**[JHN 8:44](https://ref.ly/John8:44)** *See also* [GEN 3:1–3:4](https://ref.ly/Gen3:1-Gen3:4); [2CO 11:3](https://ref.ly/2Cor11:3), [2CO 11:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor11:14); [2TH 2:9–2:10](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:9-2Thess2:10)

--------------------------------------

## 6147: deceit, practice of (id: 6147)

Deceit is condemned by God as an attempt to deny his sovereignty and his revelation of himself.

Deceit is forbidden by God
--------------------------

### Condemnation of deception in general

**[LEV 19:11](https://ref.ly/Lev19:11)** *See also* [PRO 12:22](https://ref.ly/Prov12:22), [PRO 24:28](https://ref.ly/Prov24:28)

### False witnesses condemned

**[EXO 20:16](https://ref.ly/Exod20:16)** parallel [DEU 5:20](https://ref.ly/Deut5:20) *See also* [PRO 12:17](https://ref.ly/Prov12:17), [PRO 14:5](https://ref.ly/Prov14:5), [PRO 19:9](https://ref.ly/Prov19:9)

### False measures prohibited

**[LEV 19:35](https://ref.ly/Lev19:35)** *See also* [DEU 25:13](https://ref.ly/Deut25:13); [PRO 11:1](https://ref.ly/Prov11:1), [PRO 20:10](https://ref.ly/Prov20:10); [MIC 6:11](https://ref.ly/Mic6:11)

### Spiritual deception condemned

**[TIT 1:16](https://ref.ly/Titus1:16)** *See also* [MAL 1:14](https://ref.ly/Mal1:14); [MAT 23:27–23:28](https://ref.ly/Matt23:27-Matt23:28); [LUK 6:46](https://ref.ly/Luke6:46); [ROM 2:21](https://ref.ly/Rom2:21)

Deception must not be found in the people of God
------------------------------------------------

### God's people must not practise deceit

## 6154: fall, the (id: 6154)

The departure by creation, including human beings, from the patterns and standards set for it by God. Creation now exists at a lower level of integrity and fulfilment than that which God originally intended for it.

* **Associated Articles:** 6155: fall, of Adam and Eve (ID: `6155@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6156: fall, of humanity (ID: `6156@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6157: fall, of Satan and his angels (ID: `6157@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6155: fall, of Adam and Eve (id: 6155)

The first human beings abused their God\-given freedom. Their original disobedience and resultant expulsion from the Garden of Eden is usually referred to as “the fall”.

The first sin was the disobedience of Adam and Eve to God's command

All human beings, except for Jesus Christ, are sinful

## 6160: fathers, sin of the (id: 6160)

Children may suffer on account of the sins committed by their forebears, just as they may also be blessed for their sake. Nevertheless, Scripture teaches that each individual must take responsibility for his or her own sin.

Children suffer the ill\-effects of their fathers' sins
-------------------------------------------------------

## 6163: faults (id: 6163)

Human weaknesses and failings which are sinful in themselves, and may lead to further sin. It is common, often as a means of averting blame, to put undue focus on the faults of others. However, where necessary, faults should be exposed and responsibility properly attributed. Jesus Christ lived a faultless life and God's people are challenged to live lives that are above reproach. The church will one day be presented without fault before God.

The variety of human faults
---------------------------

### A flawed human nature

**[ROM 7:14–7:23](https://ref.ly/Rom7:14-Rom7:23)** *See also* [GAL 5:17](https://ref.ly/Gal5:17); [EPH 2:3](https://ref.ly/Eph2:3); [2PE 2:18](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:18)

### Human weaknesses and failings

**[ROM 15:1](https://ref.ly/Rom15:1)** *See also* [ROM 8:28](https://ref.ly/Rom8:28), [ROM 14:1–14:2](https://ref.ly/Rom14:1-Rom14:2)

### Faults in thought, word and deed

[PSA 78:57](https://ref.ly/Ps78:57) *disloyalty and unfaithfulness to God*; ; [PRO 14:21](https://ref.ly/Prov14:21) *not showing concern for others*; ; [ISA 53:6](https://ref.ly/Isa53:6) *selfishness in going one's own way*; ; [HOS 7:16](https://ref.ly/Hos7:16) *unwillingness to turn to God*; ; [JAS 3:2](https://ref.ly/Jas3:2) *failure to control the tongue*; ; [JAS 4:17](https://ref.ly/Jas4:17) *failure to do what is right*

Finding fault with others
-------------------------

### Passing blame to others

**[GEN 3:12](https://ref.ly/Gen3:12)** *Adam blames Eve for his disobedience.* *See also* [EXO 32:22–32:24](https://ref.ly/Exod32:22-Exod32:24) *Aaron blames the Israelites for the golden calf*; [1SA 13:11–13:12](https://ref.ly/1Sam13:11-1Sam13:12) *Saul blames his troops' impatience and Samuel's late arrival for his disobedience*; [1SA 15:20–15:21](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:20-1Sam15:21) *Saul blames his soldiers for the failure to carry out God's instructions*; [MAT 25:24–25:25](https://ref.ly/Matt25:24-Matt25:25) *The man who buried his talent blames his action on his master's hardness.*

### Criticising and judging others

**[MAT 7:1–7:5](https://ref.ly/Matt7:1-Matt7:5)** *See also* [JAS 4:11–4:12](https://ref.ly/Jas4:11-Jas4:12), [JAS 5:9](https://ref.ly/Jas5:9); [JUD 1:16](https://ref.ly/Jude1:16)

### Finding fault with God's appointed leaders

**[EXO 17:3](https://ref.ly/Exod17:3)** *See also* [EXO 15:24](https://ref.ly/Exod15:24); [NUM 14:2](https://ref.ly/Num14:2); [JOS 9:18](https://ref.ly/Josh9:18); [ACT 11:2–11:3](https://ref.ly/Acts11:2-Acts11:3); [2CO 10:1](https://ref.ly/2Cor10:1)

### Finding fault with God's people

**[MAT 5:11](https://ref.ly/Matt5:11)** parallel [LUK 6:22](https://ref.ly/Luke6:22) *See also* [EXO 5:16–5:17](https://ref.ly/Exod5:16-Exod5:17); [PSA 41:6](https://ref.ly/Ps41:6), [PSA 71:10](https://ref.ly/Ps71:10); [DAN 6:24](https://ref.ly/Dan6:24)

### Finding fault with God

**[PSA 78:19](https://ref.ly/Ps78:19)** *See also* [EXO 16:7](https://ref.ly/Exod16:7); [NUM 14:27](https://ref.ly/Num14:27), [NUM 21:5](https://ref.ly/Num21:5); [EZK 35:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek35:13)

### Finding fault with Jesus Christ

**[LUK 6:7](https://ref.ly/Luke6:7)** parallels [MAT 12:10](https://ref.ly/Matt12:10), [MRK 3:4](https://ref.ly/Mark3:4) *See also* [MAT 9:3](https://ref.ly/Matt9:3) parallels [MRK 2:7](https://ref.ly/Mark2:7), [LUK 5:21](https://ref.ly/Luke5:21) *Jesus Christ is accused of blasphemy because he claims to forgive sin*; [MAT 9:11](https://ref.ly/Matt9:11) parallels [MRK 2:16](https://ref.ly/Mark2:16), [LUK 5:30](https://ref.ly/Luke5:30) *Jesus Christ is criticised for his association with “sinners”*; [MAT 15:2](https://ref.ly/Matt15:2) parallel [MRK 7:5](https://ref.ly/Mark7:5) *Jesus Christ is criticised for failure to conform to ceremonial cleansing traditions*; [MAT 26:59–26:61](https://ref.ly/Matt26:59-Matt26:61) parallel [MRK 14:55–14:59](https://ref.ly/Mark14:55-Mark14:59) *false charges brought against Jesus Christ at his trial*; [JHN 9:16](https://ref.ly/John9:16) *Jesus Christ is accused of breaking the Sabbath.*

## 6166: flesh, sinful nature (id: 6166)

The physical aspect of human beings, which distinguishes them from God and is therefore frequently used in the NT as a symbol of human sinful nature in contrast with God's perfection. (The Greek word for “flesh” is sometimes translated by other words and phrases in the passages cited in this theme.).

Flesh as the bodily substance of human beings
---------------------------------------------

### As individuals or in relation to others

**[PSA 84:2](https://ref.ly/Ps84:2)** *See also* [GEN 2:23–2:24](https://ref.ly/Gen2:23-Gen2:24), [GEN 29:14](https://ref.ly/Gen29:14); [1CO 15:39](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:39)GAL [2:20](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:20); [PHP 1:22–1:24](https://ref.ly/Phil1:22-Phil1:24)

### As the means by which Jesus Christ identified with the human race to bring salvation

**[JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14)** *See also* [EPH 2:15](https://ref.ly/Eph2:15); [HEB 10:20](https://ref.ly/Heb10:20); [1JN 4:2](https://ref.ly/1John4:2)

### As subject to mortality

**[ISA 40:6–40:7](https://ref.ly/Isa40:6-Isa40:7)** *See also* [PSA 78:39](https://ref.ly/Ps78:39); [ACT 2:31](https://ref.ly/Acts2:31); [1CO 15:50](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:50)

### As subject to weakness

**[2CH 32:8](https://ref.ly/2Chr32:8)** *See also* [PSA 73:26](https://ref.ly/Ps73:26); [MAT 26:41](https://ref.ly/Matt26:41) parallel [MRK 14:38](https://ref.ly/Mark14:38)

Flesh as contrasting human nature with God's perfection
-------------------------------------------------------

### The powerlessness of human beings contrasted with God's eternal power

**[ISA 31:3](https://ref.ly/Isa31:3)** *See also* [JHN 3:6](https://ref.ly/John3:6), [JHN 6:63](https://ref.ly/John6:63)

### Human or worldly standards contrasted with God's standards

**[JHN 8:15](https://ref.ly/John8:15)** *See also* [1CO 1:26](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:26); [2CO 5:16](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:16), [2CO 10:3–10:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor10:3-2Cor10:4)

Flesh as denoting the sinful nature of human beings
---------------------------------------------------

### The tendency to sin

**[ROM 7:18](https://ref.ly/Rom7:18)** *Paul does not mean that no goodness at all exists in people; nor that the physical aspect of human beings is inherently evil. He means that humans are invariably infected by evil and subject to its power.* *See also* [JER 17:5](https://ref.ly/Jer17:5)

### The conflict in human experience between the sinful nature and the Spirit of God

**[GAL 5:17](https://ref.ly/Gal5:17)** *See also* [ROM 8:4–8:9](https://ref.ly/Rom8:4-Rom8:9); [GAL 5:19–5:25](https://ref.ly/Gal5:19-Gal5:25)

The sinful nature is opposed to God and his will
------------------------------------------------

### This opposition finds expression in a range of acts and attitudes

**[GAL 5:19–5:21](https://ref.ly/Gal5:19-Gal5:21)** *See also* [ROM 7:14–7:25](https://ref.ly/Rom7:14-Rom7:25), [ROM 8:7](https://ref.ly/Rom8:7), [ROM 13:13–13:14](https://ref.ly/Rom13:13-Rom13:14); [1CO 6:9–6:11](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:9-1Cor6:11); [EPH 5:5](https://ref.ly/Eph5:5); [JAS 1:14–1:15](https://ref.ly/Jas1:14-Jas1:15); [1PE 2:11](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:11); [2PE 2:10](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:10), [2PE 2:18](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:18); [1JN 2:16](https://ref.ly/1John2:16)

### Confidence in the law is futile

**[ROM 8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:3)** *Because of the sinfulness of human nature, God's law is powerless to bring people into relationship with God*; **[GAL 3:3](https://ref.ly/Gal3:3)** *Even the attempt to find acceptance with God through keeping his law is an act of the sinful nature because it involves rejecting his offer of salvation through his grace.* *See also* [ROM 7:25](https://ref.ly/Rom7:25); [PHP 3:3–3:9](https://ref.ly/Phil3:3-Phil3:9)

### The sinful nature controls human behaviour in ways which run counter to God's purpose

**[ROM 8:8](https://ref.ly/Rom8:8)** *See also* [ROM 7:5](https://ref.ly/Rom7:5)

The sinful nature therefore makes people subject to God's judgment and to death
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**[ROM 8:13](https://ref.ly/Rom8:13)**; **[EPH 2:3](https://ref.ly/Eph2:3)** *See also* [GAL 6:8](https://ref.ly/Gal6:8)

Believers are not controlled by the sinful nature
-------------------------------------------------

### Through Jesus Christ's entering into human flesh, God delivers from the power and consequences of human sinfulness

**[ROM 8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:3)** *See also* [EPH 2:15](https://ref.ly/Eph2:15)

### Believers have crucified the sinful nature

**[ROM 7:5–7:6](https://ref.ly/Rom7:5-Rom7:6)** *See also* [ROM 8:8–8:9](https://ref.ly/Rom8:8-Rom8:9); [GAL 5:24](https://ref.ly/Gal5:24); [COL 2:11](https://ref.ly/Col2:11)

### The power of God's Spirit enables believers to continue to resist the sinful nature

**[ROM 8:13](https://ref.ly/Rom8:13)** *See also* [ROM 13:14](https://ref.ly/Rom13:14); [GAL 5:13](https://ref.ly/Gal5:13); [COL 3:5–3:6](https://ref.ly/Col3:5-Col3:6); [1PE 2:11](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:11)

### God's provision of church discipline in eliminating the sinful nature

**[1CO 5:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:5)** *The discipline of excluding a sinner from the church community is intended to bring him to repentance and so abandon his sinful course of action. Repentance provoked by physical suffering is possibly also in mind.*

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 84:2; Genesis 2:23-24; Genesis 29:14; 1 Corinthians 15:39; 1 Corinthians 2:20; Philippians 1:22-24; John 1:14; Ephesians 2:15; Hebrews 10:20; 1 John 4:2; Isaiah 40:6-7; Psalms 78:39; Acts 2:31; 1 Corinthians 15:50; 2 Chronicles 32:8; Psalms 73:26; Matthew 26:41; Mark 14:38; Isaiah 31:3; John 3:6; John 6:63; John 8:15; 1 Corinthians 1:26; 2 Corinthians 5:16; 2 Corinthians 10:3-4; Romans 7:18; Jeremiah 17:5; Galatians 5:17; Romans 8:4-9; Galatians 5:19-25; Galatians 5:19-21; Romans 7:14-25; Romans 8:7; Romans 13:13-14; 1 Corinthians 6:9-11; Ephesians 5:5; James 1:14-15; 1 Peter 2:11; 2 Peter 2:10; 2 Peter 2:18; 1 John 2:16; Romans 8:3; Galatians 3:3; Romans 7:25; Philippians 3:3-9; Romans 8:8; Romans 7:5; Romans 8:13; Ephesians 2:3; Galatians 6:8; Romans 7:5-6; Romans 8:8-9; Galatians 5:24; Colossians 2:11; Romans 13:14; Galatians 5:13; Colossians 3:5-6; 1 Corinthians 5:5

## 6169: godlessness (id: 6169)

An outlook and lifestyle which does not acknowledge God. God frustrates the evil purposes of the godless and judges them. Believers are to guard against godlessness.

Godlessness is an outlook and lifestyle which does not acknowledge God
----------------------------------------------------------------------

**[PSA 14:1–14:3](https://ref.ly/Ps14:1-Ps14:3)** parallel [PSA 53:1–53:3](https://ref.ly/Ps53:1-Ps53:3) *See also* [JOB 35:9–35:10](https://ref.ly/Job35:9-Job35:10); [PSA 10:4–10:11](https://ref.ly/Ps10:4-Ps10:11), [PSA 36:1–36:4](https://ref.ly/Ps36:1-Ps36:4); [PRO 11:9](https://ref.ly/Prov11:9), [PRO 30:8–30:9](https://ref.ly/Prov30:8-Prov30:9)

## 6172: guilt (id: 6172)

Primarily a state of being at fault, often accompanied by a feeling of being in the wrong. Scripture affirms that human guilt arises from sin before God, and can only be purged through accepting the forgiveness offered through the death of Jesus Christ.

* **Associated Articles:** 6173: guilt, and God (ID: `6173@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6174: guilt, human aspects of (ID: `6174@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6175: guilt, removal of (ID: `6175@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6173: guilt, and God (id: 6173)

All human beings are guilty in the sight of God, and all require forgiveness and expiation of their sin. Guilt can arise through failing to know what is right, through failing to do what is right and through giving in to temptation to do wrong.

Guilt as the objective condition of sinners
-------------------------------------------

### Guilt results from intentional sin

**[LEV 6:1–6:7](https://ref.ly/Lev6:1-Lev6:7)**; **[JAS 2:10](https://ref.ly/Jas2:10)** *See also* [NUM 5:5–5:7](https://ref.ly/Num5:5-Num5:7); [DEU 24:14–24:15](https://ref.ly/Deut24:14-Deut24:15); [EZR 9:13–9:15](https://ref.ly/Ezra9:13-Ezra9:15); [EZK 22:1–22:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek22:1-Ezek22:4); [JHN 16:7–16:8](https://ref.ly/John16:7-John16:8)

### Guilt results from unintentional sin

**[LEV 4:13](https://ref.ly/Lev4:13)** *See also* [LEV 4:22](https://ref.ly/Lev4:22), [LEV 4:27](https://ref.ly/Lev4:27); [ACT 3:17–3:20](https://ref.ly/Acts3:17-Acts3:20)

### Guilt as an accumulation of sin

**[HOS 13:12](https://ref.ly/Hos13:12)** *See also* [EZR 9:6](https://ref.ly/Ezra9:6); [ISA 1:4](https://ref.ly/Isa1:4), [ISA 24:20](https://ref.ly/Isa24:20)

God's knowledge of human guilt
------------------------------

**[PSA 69:5](https://ref.ly/Ps69:5)** *See also* [GEN 4:8–4:10](https://ref.ly/Gen4:8-Gen4:10); [JOS 7:1–7:26](https://ref.ly/Josh7:1-Josh7:26); [JER 2:22](https://ref.ly/Jer2:22); [1CO 4:4–4:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor4:4-1Cor4:5)

God's anger at human guilt
--------------------------

**[2CH 24:18](https://ref.ly/2Chr24:18)** *See also* [NUM 32:10–32:13](https://ref.ly/Num32:10-Num32:13); [2KI 22:11–22:13](https://ref.ly/2Kgs22:11-2Kgs22:13); [HOS 12:13–12:14](https://ref.ly/Hos12:13-Hos12:14); [ROM 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18), [ROM 2:5–2:8](https://ref.ly/Rom2:5-Rom2:8); [EPH 5:6–5:7](https://ref.ly/Eph5:6-Eph5:7)

God's determination to punish the guilty
----------------------------------------

### God himself punishes the guilty

**[NUM 14:18](https://ref.ly/Num14:18)** *See also* [EXO 20:5](https://ref.ly/Exod20:5); [JER 25:12](https://ref.ly/Jer25:12); [NAM 1:2–1:3](https://ref.ly/Nah1:2-Nah1:3)

### Human judges are to punish the guilty

**[DEU 25:1–25:3](https://ref.ly/Deut25:1-Deut25:3)** *See also* [PRO 17:15](https://ref.ly/Prov17:15), [PRO 24:23–24:25](https://ref.ly/Prov24:23-Prov24:25); [ROM 13:1–13:5](https://ref.ly/Rom13:1-Rom13:5); [1PE 2:13–2:14](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:13-1Pet2:14)

## 6174: guilt, human aspects of (id: 6174)

Scripture affirms that all are guilty in the sight of God, and explores the various ways in which guilt affects human life, before offering forgiveness of guilt through the death of Jesus Christ.

Human awareness of guilt
------------------------

**[PSA 51:3–51:5](https://ref.ly/Ps51:3-Ps51:5)** *See also* [GEN 42:21](https://ref.ly/Gen42:21); [PSA 32:1–32:4](https://ref.ly/Ps32:1-Ps32:4); [JHN 8:3–8:11](https://ref.ly/John8:3-John8:11); [HEB 9:9](https://ref.ly/Heb9:9); [1JN 3:19–3:20](https://ref.ly/1John3:19-1John3:20)

Human beings are held responsible for their guilt
-------------------------------------------------

**[LEV 5:17](https://ref.ly/Lev5:17)** *See also* [ISA 24:5–24:6](https://ref.ly/Isa24:5-Isa24:6); [EZK 18:19–18:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:19-Ezek18:20); [HOS 10:1–10:2](https://ref.ly/Hos10:1-Hos10:2), [HOS 13:16](https://ref.ly/Hos13:16); [MAT 12:35–12:36](https://ref.ly/Matt12:35-Matt12:36); [ROM 14:12](https://ref.ly/Rom14:12); [2CO 5:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:10); [REV 20:12](https://ref.ly/Rev20:12)

Guilt defiles human life
------------------------

**[ISA 59:1–59:3](https://ref.ly/Isa59:1-Isa59:3)** *See also* [PSA 51:1–51:7](https://ref.ly/Ps51:1-Ps51:7); [JER 2:22](https://ref.ly/Jer2:22); [HEB 10:22](https://ref.ly/Heb10:22)
