## 6175: guilt, removal of (id: 6175)

Through the death of Jesus Christ, God has provided a means of removing guilt, thus opening the way for believers to know the blessings of a right relationship with him.

The removal of guilt is God's work
----------------------------------

**[JER 2:22](https://ref.ly/Jer2:22), [JER 50:20](https://ref.ly/Jer50:20)**; **[ROM 8:33](https://ref.ly/Rom8:33)** *“Justify” is a legal term which includes the meaning “to declare not guilty”.* *See also* [2SA 24:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:10) parallel [1CH 21:8](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:8); [PSA 32:1–32:5](https://ref.ly/Ps32:1-Ps32:5); [ISA 6:1–6:6](https://ref.ly/Isa6:1-Isa6:6)

The removal of guilt requires confession
----------------------------------------

**[PSA 32:5](https://ref.ly/Ps32:5)** *See also* [2SA 24:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:10) parallel [1CH 21:8](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:8); [PSA 51:14](https://ref.ly/Ps51:14); [JER 3:12–3:13](https://ref.ly/Jer3:12-Jer3:13); [ACT 11:21](https://ref.ly/Acts11:21); [ROM 2:4](https://ref.ly/Rom2:4); [2TI 2:25](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:25); [1JN 1:8–1:9](https://ref.ly/1John1:8-1John1:9)

[LEV 16:20–16:34](https://ref.ly/Lev16:20-Lev16:34)

**[HEB 10:1–10:4](https://ref.ly/Heb10:1-Heb10:4)** *See also* [HEB 9:9](https://ref.ly/Heb9:9)

The removal of guilt by Jesus Christ's sacrificial death
--------------------------------------------------------

**[ISA 53:10–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10-Isa53:12)** *This prophecy finds its ultimate fulfilment in the person of Jesus Christ*; **[HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14)** *See also* [JHN 1:29](https://ref.ly/John1:29) *The point of John's image is that Jesus Christ will be sacrificed, as lambs were, to remove people's guilt*; [ROM 5:9](https://ref.ly/Rom5:9) *The blood of Jesus Christ referred to here is his shed blood, and therefore speaks of his (sacrificial) death*; [2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21) *Human guilt is transferred to Jesus Christ, in order that believers might become righteous before God*; [TIT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:14); [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28), [HEB 10:11–10:14](https://ref.ly/Heb10:11-Heb10:14); [1JN 1:7](https://ref.ly/1John1:7)

## 6178: hardness of heart (id: 6178)

Primarily, in Scripture, a persistent inner refusal to hear and obey the word of God. Also, in a more general sense, an uncaring or unsympathetic attitude towards other people.

Kinds of hardness of heart
--------------------------

### As disobedience towards God

**[PSA 95:8–95:9](https://ref.ly/Ps95:8-Ps95:9)** *Referring to the disobedience of the Israelites in their wilderness wanderings.* *See also* [HEB 3:7–3:9](https://ref.ly/Heb3:7-Heb3:9)**[EPH 4:18](https://ref.ly/Eph4:18)** *See also* [PRO 28:14](https://ref.ly/Prov28:14); [ZEC 7:12](https://ref.ly/Zech7:12); [ROM 2:5](https://ref.ly/Rom2:5); [HEB 3:12–3:15](https://ref.ly/Heb3:12-Heb3:15), [HEB 4:5–4:7](https://ref.ly/Heb4:5-Heb4:7)

### As the work of God

**[EXO 10:20](https://ref.ly/Exod10:20)** *God's judgment on Pharaoh was to confirm him in his stubbornness so that he might feel the full weight of his wrath*; **[ISA 6:10](https://ref.ly/Isa6:10)** *See also* [JHN 12:40](https://ref.ly/John12:40)

### As an uncaring attitude towards other people

**[DEU 15:7](https://ref.ly/Deut15:7)** *See also* [PSA 17:10](https://ref.ly/Ps17:10), [PSA 73:7](https://ref.ly/Ps73:7), [PSA 119:70](https://ref.ly/Ps119:70); [MAT 19:8](https://ref.ly/Matt19:8) parallel [MRK 10:5](https://ref.ly/Mark10:5); [JAS 2:15–2:16](https://ref.ly/Jas2:15-Jas2:16); [1JN 3:17](https://ref.ly/1John3:17)

-----------------------------

### Pharaoh

------------------------------------

## 6181: ignorance (id: 6181)

A state of lack of knowledge or information, including a failure to know the person, will and ways of God. Scripture emphasises the importance of a true knowledge of God and makes such knowledge available.

* **Associated Articles:** 6182: ignorance, and human situation (ID: `6182@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6183: ignorance, of God (ID: `6183@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6182: ignorance, and human situation (id: 6182)

Ignorance is part of the human condition: as finite creatures, human knowledge is incomplete, but human beings can trust God, whose knowledge is complete, to guide their steps.

Ignorance of God
----------------

### Finite human beings cannot know God completely

**[ECC 11:5](https://ref.ly/Eccl11:5)** *See also* [JOB 38:1–38:7](https://ref.ly/Job38:1-Job38:7); [ECC 3:11](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:11)

### This ignorance will be dispelled at Jesus Christ's return

**[1CO 13:9–13:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor13:9-1Cor13:12)**

Ignorance of the future
-----------------------

### Human beings are ignorant of future events

**[ECC 8:7–8:8](https://ref.ly/Eccl8:7-Eccl8:8)** *See also* [ECC 3:22](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:22), [ECC 9:12](https://ref.ly/Eccl9:12), [ECC 10:14](https://ref.ly/Eccl10:14), [ECC 11:2](https://ref.ly/Eccl11:2), [ECC 11:6](https://ref.ly/Eccl11:6); [ACT 20:22](https://ref.ly/Acts20:22)

### Human beings are ignorant of the time of Jesus Christ's return

**[MRK 13:32–13:36](https://ref.ly/Mark13:32-Mark13:36)** parallel [MAT 24:36–24:44](https://ref.ly/Matt24:36-Matt24:44)

### Presumptious plans should therefore be avoided

**[JAS 4:13–4:16](https://ref.ly/Jas4:13-Jas4:16)** *See also* [PSA 39:6](https://ref.ly/Ps39:6); [PRO 27:1](https://ref.ly/Prov27:1); [LUK 12:16–12:21](https://ref.ly/Luke12:16-Luke12:21)

### God's guidance is essential

**[PRO 20:24](https://ref.ly/Prov20:24)** *See also* [PRO 19:21](https://ref.ly/Prov19:21); [JER 10:23](https://ref.ly/Jer10:23)

Ignorance of doctrinal matters
------------------------------

### Within the church

**[1TH 4:13–4:18](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:13-1Thess4:18)** *See also* [1CO 10:1–10:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor10:1-1Cor10:10), [1CO 12:1–12:11](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:1-1Cor12:11)

### God has established teachers to combat ignorance

**[1CO 12:28](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:28)** *See also* [EPH 4:11–4:13](https://ref.ly/Eph4:11-Eph4:13); [1TI 4:13](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:13), [1TI 5:17](https://ref.ly/1Tim5:17); [2TI 3:16–3:17](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:16-2Tim3:17)

---------------------------

## 6183: ignorance, of God (id: 6183)

A lack of knowledge of God, regarded as inexcusable by Scripture. God has made his existence, nature and power known to all through creation. God himself is not ignorant of human sin, but is able to discern the real intentions of human minds and wills.

Ignorance of God is inexcusable
-------------------------------

### God is made known through creation

**[ROM 1:18–1:20](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18-Rom1:20)** *As God is made known to all through nature, human ignorance of God is inexcusable.* *See also* [PSA 19:1–19:4](https://ref.ly/Ps19:1-Ps19:4); [ACT 14:17](https://ref.ly/Acts14:17), [ACT 17:24–17:28](https://ref.ly/Acts17:24-Acts17:28); [ROM 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Rom2:14-Rom2:15)

### God revealed himself to Israel

**[NEH 9:13–9:14](https://ref.ly/Neh9:13-Neh9:14)** *See also* [EXO 19:10–19:11](https://ref.ly/Exod19:10-Exod19:11), [EXO 19:16–19:19](https://ref.ly/Exod19:16-Exod19:19); [PSA 103:7](https://ref.ly/Ps103:7), [PSA 147:19–147:20](https://ref.ly/Ps147:19-Ps147:20); [EZK 20:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:5)

Ignorance of God is linked to sin and rebellion
-----------------------------------------------

### Among the Gentiles

## 6184: imagination (id: 6184)

The human ability to form mental pictures, often used to refer to human desires or schemes which are inclined towards evil. Scripture often treats the human heart as the focus of the imagination.

* **Associated Articles:** 6185: imagination, inward desires (ID: `6185@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6186: imagination, evil scheming (ID: `6186@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6185: imagination, inward desires (id: 6185)

The usually sinful inclinations of a heart which is by nature corrupt and stubborn, but which may be renewed by God, resulting in purified desires.

The heart is the source of human desires
----------------------------------------

**[PRO 4:23](https://ref.ly/Prov4:23)** *See also* [PSA 10:3](https://ref.ly/Ps10:3); [MAT 12:34–12:35](https://ref.ly/Matt12:34-Matt12:35) parallel [LUK 6:45](https://ref.ly/Luke6:45)

-------------------------

## 6186: imagination, evil scheming (id: 6186)

Human thinking, darkened by sin, expressed in plans which are in opposition to God and which seek to take advantage of others.

Human thought is darkened by sin
--------------------------------

### As a result of rejecting God's revelation

## 6187: immorality (id: 6187)

Behaviour which is contrary to the will of God for his people. Although the term may be used to refer to a wide range of immoral actions, it is used especially in relation to unacceptable sexual behaviour.

* **Associated Articles:** 6188: immorality, nature of sexual (ID: `6188@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6189: immorality, examples of sexual (ID: `6189@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6188: immorality, nature of sexual (id: 6188)

Sexual behaviour which is contrary to God's law.

Sexual immorality is widespread in the world
--------------------------------------------

## 6193: impenitence (id: 6193)

A deliberate and persistent refusal to repent or to submit to God's will.

* **Associated Articles:** 6194: impenitence, warnings against (ID: `6194@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6195: impenitence, results of (ID: `6195@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6194: impenitence, warnings against (id: 6194)

Scripture stresses the seriousness of impenitence. Despite the goodness of God, some sinners refuse to repent and turn to him in faith.

Impenitence is a refusal to turn from sin
-----------------------------------------

**[HOS 7:10](https://ref.ly/Hos7:10)**; **[ACT 7:51](https://ref.ly/Acts7:51)** *See also* [JOB 34:33](https://ref.ly/Job34:33); [ISA 1:4](https://ref.ly/Isa1:4); [JER 9:6](https://ref.ly/Jer9:6); [HOS 11:5](https://ref.ly/Hos11:5)

Impenitence in spite of God's invitations and and warnings
----------------------------------------------------------

**[ISA 66:4](https://ref.ly/Isa66:4)**; **[ZEC 7:11–7:12](https://ref.ly/Zech7:11-Zech7:12)** *See also* [2KI 17:14](https://ref.ly/2Kgs17:14); [ZEC 1:4](https://ref.ly/Zech1:4)JER [7:25–7:26](https://ref.ly/Zech7:25-Zech7:26), [JER 11:7–11:8](https://ref.ly/Jer11:7-Jer11:8), [JER 11:10](https://ref.ly/Jer11:10), [JER 13:10](https://ref.ly/Jer13:10), [JER 17:23](https://ref.ly/Jer17:23), [JER 25:3–25:4](https://ref.ly/Jer25:3-Jer25:4), [JER 32:33](https://ref.ly/Jer32:33), [JER 44:4–44:5](https://ref.ly/Jer44:4-Jer44:5), [JER 44:16](https://ref.ly/Jer44:16)

--------------------------------------

----------------------------------------

**[PSA 78:31–78:32](https://ref.ly/Ps78:31-Ps78:32)**; **[AMO 4:6](https://ref.ly/Amos4:6)** *See also* [ISA 9:13](https://ref.ly/Isa9:13); [JER 2:30](https://ref.ly/Jer2:30), [JER 3:2–3:3](https://ref.ly/Jer3:2-Jer3:3), [JER 5:3](https://ref.ly/Jer5:3), [JER 30:15](https://ref.ly/Jer30:15); [ZEP 3:2](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:2); [HAG 2:17](https://ref.ly/Hag2:17)

## 6195: impenitence, results of (id: 6195)

The seriousness of the failure to repent is frequently underlined in Scripture, which provides numerous examples of impenitence and its consequences.

----------------------------

## 6199: imperfection (id: 6199)

The state of incompletion or decay that characterises the fallen world. Although God created the world perfect, it lapsed into its present state of imperfection through human sin.

* **Associated Articles:** 6200: imperfection, influence of (ID: `6200@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6201: imperfection, and God's purposes (ID: `6201@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6200: imperfection, influence of (id: 6200)

Scripture indicates that the world, including human beings and institutions, are imperfect because of the contaminating influence of sin. This influence extends to the household of faith: both Israel and the Christian church are portrayed as prone to sin and weakness.

The creation is imperfect because of sin
----------------------------------------

**[GEN 3:17–3:19](https://ref.ly/Gen3:17-Gen3:19)** *See also* [GEN 5:29](https://ref.ly/Gen5:29); [ROM 8:20–8:22](https://ref.ly/Rom8:20-Rom8:22)

Imperfection is expressed in corruption and death
-------------------------------------------------

**[PSA 103:15–103:16](https://ref.ly/Ps103:15-Ps103:16)**; **[2PE 1:4](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:4)** *See also* [2SA 14:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:14); [PSA 90:3–90:10](https://ref.ly/Ps90:3-Ps90:10); [ECC 12:1–12:7](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:1-Eccl12:7); [JAS 1:10](https://ref.ly/Jas1:10); [1PE 1:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:24)

The imperfection of the spiritual creation
------------------------------------------

**[JOB 4:18](https://ref.ly/Job4:18)**; **[JUD 1:6](https://ref.ly/Jude1:6)** *See also* [2PE 2:4](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:4)

The universal imperfection of human beings
------------------------------------------

**[ROM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23)** *See also* [GEN 6:5](https://ref.ly/Gen6:5); [1KI 8:46](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:46) parallel [2CH 6:36](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:36); [PSA 14:3](https://ref.ly/Ps14:3), [PSA 130:3](https://ref.ly/Ps130:3); [PRO 20:9](https://ref.ly/Prov20:9); [ECC 7:20](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:20); [ISA 53:6](https://ref.ly/Isa53:6), [ISA 64:6](https://ref.ly/Isa64:6); [GAL 3:22](https://ref.ly/Gal3:22); [JAS 3:2](https://ref.ly/Jas3:2)

------------------------------------------

### Israel and her leaders

### Sacrificial animals must be unblemished

**[LEV 21:17–21:23](https://ref.ly/Lev21:17-Lev21:23)**

## 6203: mortality (id: 6203)

The human state of being subject to death and decay. God did not create human beings to be like this; mortality is the consequence of sin and is countered by the gospel promise of eternal life in Jesus Christ.

Mortality originated in the fall
--------------------------------

**[GEN 2:16–2:17](https://ref.ly/Gen2:16-Gen2:17)**

### It is the decree of God

**[PSA 90:3](https://ref.ly/Ps90:3), [PSA 90:5](https://ref.ly/Ps90:5)** *See also* [GEN 3:19](https://ref.ly/Gen3:19), [GEN 6:3](https://ref.ly/Gen6:3)

### It is universal

**[ECC 3:20](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:20)** *See also* [1CO 15:22](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:22)

### It is inevitable

[2SA 14:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:14); ; [JOB 30:23](https://ref.ly/Job30:23); ; [ECC 3:2](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:2); ; [ROM 6:23](https://ref.ly/Rom6:23)

### It is a judgment from God

**[ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12)** *See also* [ROM 5:15–5:19](https://ref.ly/Rom5:15-Rom5:19)

### It leads to judgment

**[HEB 9:27](https://ref.ly/Heb9:27)** *See also* [2CO 5:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:10)

Mortality extends to the creation
---------------------------------

[ROM 8:20–8:21](https://ref.ly/Rom8:20-Rom8:21)

[ECC 3:19](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:19)

## 6206: offence (id: 6206)

A transgression or affront against the law or an individual. The gospel itself is seen as offensive by unbelievers, who are often unable to cope with its radical challenge to their unbelief.

Legal offence
-------------

**[DEU 21:22–21:23](https://ref.ly/Deut21:22-Deut21:23)** *See also* [EXO 21:15–21:25](https://ref.ly/Exod21:15-Exod21:25), [EXO 22:1–22:5](https://ref.ly/Exod22:1-Exod22:5); [DEU 19:15–19:21](https://ref.ly/Deut19:15-Deut19:21)

Moral offence
-------------

**[EZK 22:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek22:11)** *See also* [EXO 22:16–22:17](https://ref.ly/Exod22:16-Exod22:17); [LEV 18:6–18:23](https://ref.ly/Lev18:6-Lev18:23); [DEU 22:13–22:30](https://ref.ly/Deut22:13-Deut22:30); [2SA 3:8](https://ref.ly/2Sam3:8); [1CO 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:9-1Cor6:10)

An offence to others
--------------------

### On a national level

**[1SA 13:4](https://ref.ly/1Sam13:4)** *See also* [2SA 10:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam10:6) parallel [1CH 19:6](https://ref.ly/1Chr19:6); [JER 24:9](https://ref.ly/Jer24:9)

### On a personal level

**[2SA 16:21](https://ref.ly/2Sam16:21)** *See also* [GEN 20:1–20:16](https://ref.ly/Gen20:1-Gen20:16), [GEN 40:1](https://ref.ly/Gen40:1); [1SA 25:14–25:28](https://ref.ly/1Sam25:14-1Sam25:28) *Abigail seeks David's forgiveness for Nabal's offence*; [JOB 19:17](https://ref.ly/Job19:17); [PRO 17:9](https://ref.ly/Prov17:9), [PRO 18:19](https://ref.ly/Prov18:19), [PRO 19:11](https://ref.ly/Prov19:11); [MAT 13:54–13:57](https://ref.ly/Matt13:54-Matt13:57) parallel [MRK 6:1–6:4](https://ref.ly/Mark6:1-Mark6:4) *The people of Nazareth take offence at Jesus Christ*; [MAT 15:1–15:12](https://ref.ly/Matt15:1-Matt15:12), [MAT 17:24–17:27](https://ref.ly/Matt17:24-Matt17:27); [JHN 6:53–6:66](https://ref.ly/John6:53-John6:66)

Offence against God
-------------------

**[1KI 8:50–8:51](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:50-1Kgs8:51)** *Offence against God is synonymous with sin.* *See also* [JOB 7:21](https://ref.ly/Job7:21), [JOB 10:14](https://ref.ly/Job10:14), [JOB 13:23](https://ref.ly/Job13:23) *“wrongs”, “sins” and “offence” are three important OT terms for sin*; [JOB 14:16–14:17](https://ref.ly/Job14:16-Job14:17), [JOB 34:31–34:33](https://ref.ly/Job34:31-Job34:33); [PSA 59:3](https://ref.ly/Ps59:3), [PSA 139:24](https://ref.ly/Ps139:24); [ISA 43:24](https://ref.ly/Isa43:24), [ISA 44:22](https://ref.ly/Isa44:22), [ISA 59:12](https://ref.ly/Isa59:12); [EZK 18:1–18:32](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:1-Ezek18:32) *Ezekiel warns that the soul who sins will die*; [EZK 33:10](https://ref.ly/Ezek33:10), [EZK 37:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:23), [EZK 39:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:24); [AMO 5:12](https://ref.ly/Amos5:12)

---------------------------

**[NUM 18:1](https://ref.ly/Num18:1)** *See also* [NUM 18:23](https://ref.ly/Num18:23)

The things of God are an offence to sinful people
-------------------------------------------------

**[JER 6:10](https://ref.ly/Jer6:10)**; **[1CO 1:22–1:24](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:22-1Cor1:24)** *See also* [GAL 5:11](https://ref.ly/Gal5:11)

A stumbling\-block as an object of offence
------------------------------------------

### A stumbling\-block for others

**[ROM 14:13](https://ref.ly/Rom14:13)** *The concept behind the English word “offence” is one of striking against something or someone. The image of a stumbling\-block conveys the idea of tripping or falling as a result of striking against such an object.* *See also* [LEV 19:14](https://ref.ly/Lev19:14); [MAT 16:23](https://ref.ly/Matt16:23); [ROM 11:9–11:10](https://ref.ly/Rom11:9-Rom11:10); [PSA 69:22–69:23](https://ref.ly/Ps69:22-Ps69:23); [1CO 8:9](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:9); [2CO 6:3](https://ref.ly/2Cor6:3)

**[EZK 14:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek14:7)** *See also* [EZK 14:3–14:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek14:3-Ezek14:4)

### A stumbling\-block set up by God

**[EZK 3:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek3:20)**

## 6209: pagans (id: 6209)

OT use of the term \`\`pagan''
------------------------------

## 6212: participation (id: 6212)

Sharing in actions or identifying with actions or people. All human beings share in Adam's fall and its consequences; believers share in Christ and his life.

* **Associated Articles:** 6213: participation, in sin (ID: `6213@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6214: participation, in Christ (ID: `6214@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6213: participation, in sin (id: 6213)

The natural condition of all human beings as a result of sharing in Adam's fall. Believers are called not to associate with, nor give approval to wickedness but to stand apart from evil as God's holy people.

Participation in Adam
---------------------

### In Adam's humanity

[GEN 3:20](https://ref.ly/Gen3:20), [GEN 5:1–5:3](https://ref.ly/Gen5:1-Gen5:3); ; [JHN 3:6](https://ref.ly/John3:6); ; [ACT 17:26](https://ref.ly/Acts17:26); ; [1CO 15:48–15:49](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:48-1Cor15:49)

### In Adam's sin

**[ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12)** *See also* [HOS 6:7](https://ref.ly/Hos6:7); [ROM 5:15–5:19](https://ref.ly/Rom5:15-Rom5:19); [1CO 15:21–15:22](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:21-1Cor15:22)GEN [3:17](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:17); [ROM 8:20–8:21](https://ref.ly/Rom8:20-Rom8:21)

### In a sinful nature

**[EPH 2:3](https://ref.ly/Eph2:3)** *See also* [ROM 7:5](https://ref.ly/Rom7:5), [ROM 7:14–7:20](https://ref.ly/Rom7:14-Rom7:20)

Ways of participating in evil
-----------------------------

### Associating with evildoers

**[PSA 50:18](https://ref.ly/Ps50:18)** *See also* [GEN 49:6](https://ref.ly/Gen49:6); [LEV 15:31](https://ref.ly/Lev15:31); [JOS 23:12–23:13](https://ref.ly/Josh23:12-Josh23:13); [JOB 34:8](https://ref.ly/Job34:8); [PSA 141:4](https://ref.ly/Ps141:4); [PRO 22:24–22:25](https://ref.ly/Prov22:24-Prov22:25); [2JN 1:10–1:11](https://ref.ly/2John1:10-2John1:11) *giving hospitality to evildoers*

### Giving approval to evil

**[LEV 19:17](https://ref.ly/Lev19:17)**; **[PSA 64:5](https://ref.ly/Ps64:5)**; **[ROM 1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:32)** *See also* [2SA 3:28–3:29](https://ref.ly/2Sam3:28-2Sam3:29), [2SA 3:37](https://ref.ly/2Sam3:37); [PSA 49:13](https://ref.ly/Ps49:13); [EZK 13:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek13:22); [LUK 11:48](https://ref.ly/Luke11:48); [ACT 7:60](https://ref.ly/Acts7:60), [ACT 22:20](https://ref.ly/Acts22:20); [ROM 14:22](https://ref.ly/Rom14:22); [EPH 5:11](https://ref.ly/Eph5:11)

### Sacrifice and idolatry

**[NUM 25:1–25:3](https://ref.ly/Num25:1-Num25:3)** *See also* [2KI 17:33](https://ref.ly/2Kgs17:33); [HOS 4:17](https://ref.ly/Hos4:17); [1CO 10:18–10:20](https://ref.ly/1Cor10:18-1Cor10:20)

God's people are not to participate in evil
-------------------------------------------

### God's people are called to be holy

**[LEV 20:26](https://ref.ly/Lev20:26)** *See also* [LEV 11:44–11:45](https://ref.ly/Lev11:44-Lev11:45), [LEV 19:2](https://ref.ly/Lev19:2); [1PE 1:15–1:16](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:15-1Pet1:16)

### Separation from foreign gods

**[JOS 23:7](https://ref.ly/Josh23:7)** *See also* [DEU 12:30](https://ref.ly/Deut12:30), [DEU 29:18](https://ref.ly/Deut29:18); [1KI 11:2](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:2)

### Separation from the godless

## 6214: participation, in Christ (id: 6214)

The joining of believers to Jesus Christ, through faith, whereby they are freed from participation in Adam by sharing in Christ's death and resurrection, his nature, sufferings and glory and whereby, too, they become part of his body. Believers therefore share in the fellowship, ministry and hope of God's people, which is anticipated by the OT and fulfilled in the church.

Believers are united with Christ
--------------------------------

**[EPH 1:13](https://ref.ly/Eph1:13)** *See also* [JHN 13:8](https://ref.ly/John13:8); [1CO 1:9](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:9), [1CO 6:17](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:17); [HEB 3:14](https://ref.ly/Heb3:14)

Faith liberates from participation in sin
-----------------------------------------

## 6221: rebellion (id: 6221)

A state of revolt against established divine or human authority. Scripture condemns rebellion against God and indicates the futility of Israel's frequent rebellions against him.

* **Associated Articles:** 6222: rebellion, against God (ID: `6222@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6223: rebellion, of Israel (ID: `6223@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6224: rebellion, against human authority (ID: `6224@DictionaryBibleThemes`)

## 6224: rebellion, against human authority (id: 6224)

Human authority is frequently defied and resisted. To rebel against God's chosen leaders is to defy God himself.

## 6227: regret (id: 6227)

Deep feelings of sorrow arising from past events now seen as sins, mistakes or misfortunes. It can either lead to true repentance or destructive bitterness.

Examples and expressions of regret
----------------------------------

**[1SA 26:21](https://ref.ly/1Sam26:21)** *See also* [GEN 27:33–27:35](https://ref.ly/Gen27:33-Gen27:35); [NUM 12:10–12:12](https://ref.ly/Num12:10-Num12:12) *Aaron and Miriam when they had spoken against Moses*; [NUM 14:1–14:2](https://ref.ly/Num14:1-Num14:2); [JDG 11:34–11:35](https://ref.ly/Judg11:34-Judg11:35) *Jephthah when he returned home from fighting the Ammonites*[2SA 24:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:10) parallel [1CH 21:8](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:8); [2SA 24:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:14) parallel [1CH 21:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:13)[1KI 21:27](https://ref.ly/1Kgs21:27) *Ahab after he murdered Naboth and seized his vineyard*; [DAN 6:14](https://ref.ly/Dan6:14); [MAT 26:75](https://ref.ly/Matt26:75) parallels [MRK 14:72](https://ref.ly/Mark14:72), [LUK 22:61–22:62](https://ref.ly/Luke22:61-Luke22:62) *Peter when he disowned Jesus Christ*; [MAT 27:3–27:4](https://ref.ly/Matt27:3-Matt27:4) *Judas after betraying Jesus Christ*

----------------------------

**[GEN 6:6](https://ref.ly/Gen6:6)** *See also* [1SA 15:10–15:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:10-1Sam15:11), [1SA 15:35](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:35); [2SA 24:16](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:16) parallel [1CH 21:15](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:15)

## 6230: rejection (id: 6230)

The deliberate and conscious act of turning away from someone, or refusing to accept something that is being offered.

* **Associated Articles:** 6231: rejection of God (ID: `6231@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6232: rejection of God, results of (ID: `6232@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6233: rejection, human experience of (ID: `6233@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6231: rejection of God (id: 6231)

The deliberate rejection of God lies at the heart of human sin. It is seen in rebellion against God's authority, purpose and instruction and results in the rejection of God's servants and, ultimately, in the rejection of his Son.

Rejection of God
----------------

### Rejection of God's authority

**[2KI 17:15](https://ref.ly/2Kgs17:15)** *See also* [ISA 1:4](https://ref.ly/Isa1:4)

### Rejection of God in favour of other gods

**[DEU 32:15–32:18](https://ref.ly/Deut32:15-Deut32:18)** *See also* [EXO 22:20](https://ref.ly/Exod22:20); [DEU 31:20](https://ref.ly/Deut31:20); [1SA 8:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam8:8); [ISA 1:28](https://ref.ly/Isa1:28), [ISA 65:11](https://ref.ly/Isa65:11); [JER 15:6](https://ref.ly/Jer15:6); [EZK 14:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek14:5)

### Rejection of God as king

**[1SA 8:7](https://ref.ly/1Sam8:7)** *See also* [1SA 10:19](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:19)

### Rejection of God's ways

**[PSA 95:10](https://ref.ly/Ps95:10)**; **[ISA 30:15](https://ref.ly/Isa30:15)** *See also* [EXO 16:7–16:8](https://ref.ly/Exod16:7-Exod16:8); [NUM 11:18–11:20](https://ref.ly/Num11:18-Num11:20), [NUM 14:27](https://ref.ly/Num14:27); [PSA 81:11–81:13](https://ref.ly/Ps81:11-Ps81:13); [ISA 8:6](https://ref.ly/Isa8:6), [ISA 30:1–30:2](https://ref.ly/Isa30:1-Isa30:2); [LUK 7:30](https://ref.ly/Luke7:30)

## 6232: rejection of God, results of (id: 6232)

Rejecting God angers and grieves him. To reject God can be to reject all the benefits of the gospel, and can lead to judgment and punishment.

Rejection grieves God
---------------------

### God rejected as Creator

**[GEN 6:6](https://ref.ly/Gen6:6)**

### God rejected as a husband

**[EZK 6:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek6:9)** *See also* [JER 2:2](https://ref.ly/Jer2:2), [JER 3:20](https://ref.ly/Jer3:20), [JER 31:32](https://ref.ly/Jer31:32); [HOS 1:2](https://ref.ly/Hos1:2)

### God rejected as a father

**[HOS 11:1–11:4](https://ref.ly/Hos11:1-Hos11:4)** *See also* [DEU 32:18](https://ref.ly/Deut32:18); [JER 3:19](https://ref.ly/Jer3:19), [JER 31:20](https://ref.ly/Jer31:20)

### God rejected by Israel, his vineyard

**[ISA 5:4](https://ref.ly/Isa5:4)** *See also* [JER 2:21](https://ref.ly/Jer2:21)

Rejection angers God and brings his wrath
-----------------------------------------

**[EZR 8:22](https://ref.ly/Ezra8:22)**; **[JHN 3:36](https://ref.ly/John3:36)** *See also* [LEV 26:27–26:28](https://ref.ly/Lev26:27-Lev26:28); [2CH 36:16](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:16); [ZEC 7:12](https://ref.ly/Zech7:12); [ROM 2:8](https://ref.ly/Rom2:8)

## 6233: rejection, human experience of (id: 6233)

Feelings of rejection by God may be a result of alienation caused directly or indirectly by sin. God's people also experience rejection by a hostile world. Experiences and feelings of rejection are to be met with prayer, forgiveness and perseverance, together with confidence in God's commitment to and compassion for, his people.

Feelings of rejection by God
----------------------------

### Feelings of national rejection

**[PSA 74:1](https://ref.ly/Ps74:1)**; **[ISA 49:14](https://ref.ly/Isa49:14)** *See also* [PSA 44:9](https://ref.ly/Ps44:9), [PSA 108:11](https://ref.ly/Ps108:11); [ISA 40:27](https://ref.ly/Isa40:27); [JER 13:17](https://ref.ly/Jer13:17), [JER 14:9](https://ref.ly/Jer14:9); [LAM 1:2](https://ref.ly/Lam1:2), [LAM 5:20](https://ref.ly/Lam5:20); [EZK 37:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:11)

### Feelings of personal rejection

**[PSA 13:1](https://ref.ly/Ps13:1)**; **[MAT 27:46](https://ref.ly/Matt27:46)** parallel [MRK 15:34](https://ref.ly/Mark15:34) *Jesus Christ experiences separation from his Father as a consequence of bearing human sin.* *See also* [PSA 22:1–22:2](https://ref.ly/Ps22:1-Ps22:2), [PSA 43:2](https://ref.ly/Ps43:2), [PSA 88:14](https://ref.ly/Ps88:14)

## 6236: sexual sin (id: 6236)

Sexual relations are to be seen as an aspect of God's good creation which can be corrupted and devalued through human sin.

* **Associated Articles:** 6237: sexual sin, nature of (ID: `6237@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6238: homosexuality (ID: `6238@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6239: prostitution (ID: `6239@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6240: rape (ID: `6240@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6241: seduction (ID: `6241@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6242: adultery (ID: `6242@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6243: adultery, spiritual (ID: `6243@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6237: sexual sin, nature of (id: 6237)

Any transgression of the limits that God has set for the enjoyment of sex. Such sins are often life\-dominating, but may be broken through the power and grace of Jesus Christ.

The origin of sexual sin
------------------------

### Fallen human nature

**[GAL 5:19](https://ref.ly/Gal5:19)** *See also* [ROM 13:12–13:14](https://ref.ly/Rom13:12-Rom13:14); [COL 3:5–3:6](https://ref.ly/Col3:5-Col3:6)

### The heart

**[MAT 15:19](https://ref.ly/Matt15:19)** parallel [MRK 7:21–7:22](https://ref.ly/Mark7:21-Mark7:22)

The offensiveness of sexual sin
-------------------------------

### It defiles the sinner

**[MAT 15:20](https://ref.ly/Matt15:20)** parallel [MRK 7:23](https://ref.ly/Mark7:23) *See also* [ROM 1:24](https://ref.ly/Rom1:24); [1CO 6:18](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:18)

### It defiles society

**[LEV 18:24–18:25](https://ref.ly/Lev18:24-Lev18:25)** *See also* [1CO 5:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:6); [REV 19:2](https://ref.ly/Rev19:2)

### It offends other people

**[2PE 2:7–2:8](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:7-2Pet2:8)** *See also* [GEN 9:22–9:25](https://ref.ly/Gen9:22-Gen9:25), [GEN 34:7](https://ref.ly/Gen34:7), [GEN 38:24](https://ref.ly/Gen38:24); [2SA 13:21–13:22](https://ref.ly/2Sam13:21-2Sam13:22); [2CO 12:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:21)

### It offends God

**[2SA 11:27](https://ref.ly/2Sam11:27)** *See also* [JER 13:26–13:27](https://ref.ly/Jer13:26-Jer13:27); [MAL 3:5](https://ref.ly/Mal3:5)

---------------------------------

### Pre\-marital sex

## 6238: homosexuality (id: 6238)

Sexual relations between people of the same sex. The biblical emphasis upon the loving union of male and female, as an integral part of God's creation ordinance, establishes the context against which the censure of homosexual practice is to be set.

God's creation order for sexuality
----------------------------------

[GEN 1:27–1:28](https://ref.ly/Gen1:27-Gen1:28), [GEN 2:18–2:24](https://ref.ly/Gen2:18-Gen2:24); [MRK 10:6–10:9](https://ref.ly/Mark10:6-Mark10:9) parallel [MAT 19:4–19:5](https://ref.ly/Matt19:4-Matt19:5); ; [EPH 5:31](https://ref.ly/Eph5:31)

OT prohibitions of homosexual practice
--------------------------------------

**[LEV 18:22](https://ref.ly/Lev18:22)** *See also* [LEV 20:13](https://ref.ly/Lev20:13)

Homosexual practice is incompatible with the kingdom of God
-----------------------------------------------------------

**[1CO 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:9-1Cor6:10)** *The meanings of the Greek words for “male prostitutes” and “homosexual offenders” are disputed, but the terms are commonly associated with particular forms of homosexual behaviour.* *See also* [1TI 1:9–1:11](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:9-1Tim1:11)

Sexual disorder is one consequence of rejecting God
---------------------------------------------------

**[ROM 1:21–1:27](https://ref.ly/Rom1:21-Rom1:27)** [1KI 14:24](https://ref.ly/1Kgs14:24), [1KI 15:12](https://ref.ly/1Kgs15:12); ; [2KI 23:7](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:7)

Examples of homosexual practice
-------------------------------

In Sodom and Gomorrah: [GEN 19:4–19:8](https://ref.ly/Gen19:4-Gen19:8); ; [JUD 1:7](https://ref.ly/Jude1:7); [JDG 19:16–19:24](https://ref.ly/Judg19:16-Judg19:24) *in Israel in a time of moral decadence*

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 1:27-28; Genesis 2:18-24; Mark 10:6-9; Matthew 19:4-5; Ephesians 5:31; Leviticus 18:22; Leviticus 20:13; 1 Corinthians 6:9-10; 1 Timothy 1:9-11; Romans 1:21-27; 1 Kings 14:24; 1 Kings 15:12; 2 Kings 23:7; Genesis 19:4-8; Jude 1:7; Judges 19:16-24
* **Associated Articles:** 4005: creation (ID: `4005@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5707: male and female (ID: `5707@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5717: monogamy (ID: `5717@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6239: prostitution (id: 6239)

Scripture condemns the offering of sex for money or favours. However, it also stresses the prospect of new life in Christ for prostitutes, and points to some prostitutes as examples of faith.

Prostitution among the heathen
------------------------------

### For money

[GEN 38:15–38:16](https://ref.ly/Gen38:15-Gen38:16); ; [JOS 2:1](https://ref.ly/Josh2:1); ; [JOL 3:3](https://ref.ly/Joel3:3)

### Religious prostitution

[GEN 38:21–38:22](https://ref.ly/Gen38:21-Gen38:22); ; [JOB 36:14](https://ref.ly/Job36:14)

Prostitution in Israel
----------------------

### It was forbidden under God's law

**[LEV 19:29](https://ref.ly/Lev19:29)**; **[DEU 23:17–23:18](https://ref.ly/Deut23:17-Deut23:18)**

### Priests were forbidden to marry prostitutes

*See also* [LEV 21:7](https://ref.ly/Lev21:7), [LEV 21:14](https://ref.ly/Lev21:14)

### The penalties for prostitution

[GEN 38:24](https://ref.ly/Gen38:24); ; [LEV 21:9](https://ref.ly/Lev21:9)

**[PRO 7:10](https://ref.ly/Prov7:10)** *See also* [1CO 6:9](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:9)

## 6240: rape (id: 6240)

The sexual violation of an individual (normally, though not necessarily, female). This is a deeply traumatic and degrading experience for the victim and is an evil that Scripture condemns.

Lust is the motivation for rape
-------------------------------

**[2SA 13:1–13:15](https://ref.ly/2Sam13:1-2Sam13:15)**

Women and rape
--------------

### Women are particularly vulnerable to male assault

**[2SA 13:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam13:14)** *See also* [ZEC 14:2](https://ref.ly/Zech14:2)

### Women were protected under the law

[DEU 22:25–22:29](https://ref.ly/Deut22:25-Deut22:29)

### Women are to be loved and cared for

**[EPH 5:25](https://ref.ly/Eph5:25), [EPH 5:28–5:29](https://ref.ly/Eph5:28-Eph5:29)** *See also* [GEN 12:18–12:20](https://ref.ly/Gen12:18-Gen12:20); [1PE 3:7](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:7)

------------------

**[2SA 13:19–13:20](https://ref.ly/2Sam13:19-2Sam13:20)** *See also* [GEN 34:6–34:7](https://ref.ly/Gen34:6-Gen34:7)

### Its physical effects

**[JDG 19:26–19:28](https://ref.ly/Judg19:26-Judg19:28)** *See also* [JDG 20:4–20:5](https://ref.ly/Judg20:4-Judg20:5)

---------------------------

[GEN 34:7–34:31](https://ref.ly/Gen34:7-Gen34:31); ; [2SA 13:22–13:32](https://ref.ly/2Sam13:22-2Sam13:32); ; [JDG 20:6–20:11](https://ref.ly/Judg20:6-Judg20:11); ; [ROM 12:19](https://ref.ly/Rom12:19), [ROM 13:3–13:4](https://ref.ly/Rom13:3-Rom13:4); ; [JAS 1:20](https://ref.ly/Jas1:20)

## 6241: seduction (id: 6241)

The deliberate enticement or persuasion of someone into the abandonment of godly principles. Scripture speaks of both sexual and spiritual seduction.

Sexual seduction
----------------

### Warnings to avoid temptation

**[PRO 7:1–7:22](https://ref.ly/Prov7:1-Prov7:22)**; **[2TI 2:22](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:22)** *See also* [PRO 1:10](https://ref.ly/Prov1:10), [PRO 2:16–2:19](https://ref.ly/Prov2:16-Prov2:19)

### Examples of enticement

**[GEN 39:6–39:12](https://ref.ly/Gen39:6-Gen39:12)**; **[NUM 25:1–25:3](https://ref.ly/Num25:1-Num25:3)** *See also* [NUM 31:15–31:16](https://ref.ly/Num31:15-Num31:16); [JDG 16:1](https://ref.ly/Judg16:1), [JDG 16:4–16:5](https://ref.ly/Judg16:4-Judg16:5); [2SA 11:1–11:4](https://ref.ly/2Sam11:1-2Sam11:4); [1KI 11:1–11:6](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:1-1Kgs11:6); [REV 2:14–2:16](https://ref.ly/Rev2:14-Rev2:16), [REV 2:20–2:22](https://ref.ly/Rev2:20-Rev2:22)

### The law as a deterrent

**[EXO 22:16–22:17](https://ref.ly/Exod22:16-Exod22:17)** *See also* [HEB 13:4](https://ref.ly/Heb13:4)

### Resisting temptation

**[JOB 31:1](https://ref.ly/Job31:1)** *See also* [MAL 2:14](https://ref.ly/Mal2:14); [MAT 5:27–5:30](https://ref.ly/Matt5:27-Matt5:30); [1CO 7:2–7:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor7:2-1Cor7:3); [PHP 4:8](https://ref.ly/Phil4:8); [1TH 4:3–4:6](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:3-1Thess4:6)

-------------------

------------------------

### A thought planted

**[GEN 3:2–3:3](https://ref.ly/Gen3:2-Gen3:3)** *See also* [MAT 4:3](https://ref.ly/Matt4:3); [JAS 1:14](https://ref.ly/Jas1:14); [1JN 2:15](https://ref.ly/1John2:15)

### Attraction

**[GEN 3:6](https://ref.ly/Gen3:6)** *See also* [JAS 1:15](https://ref.ly/Jas1:15)

## 6242: adultery (id: 6242)

Sexual relations involving at least one partner who is married to someone else. Such relations break the marriage covenant and are condemned in Scripture. Jesus Christ extended the understanding of adultery to include inner lust.

Adultery is condemned by God
----------------------------

### God's law forbids it

**[EXO 20:14](https://ref.ly/Exod20:14)** parallel [DEU 5:18](https://ref.ly/Deut5:18) *See also* [LEV 18:20](https://ref.ly/Lev18:20); [MAT 19:18](https://ref.ly/Matt19:18) parallels [MRK 10:19](https://ref.ly/Mark10:19), [LUK 18:20](https://ref.ly/Luke18:20); [JAS 2:11](https://ref.ly/Jas2:11)

### It is listed with other evil practices

[PSA 50:18](https://ref.ly/Ps50:18); ; [JER 7:9–7:10](https://ref.ly/Jer7:9-Jer7:10); ; [HOS 4:1–4:2](https://ref.ly/Hos4:1-Hos4:2); ; [LUK 18:11](https://ref.ly/Luke18:11); ; [1TI 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:9-1Tim1:10)

The lure of adultery
--------------------

### It begins with lust

**[PRO 6:25](https://ref.ly/Prov6:25)**; **[MAT 5:27–5:28](https://ref.ly/Matt5:27-Matt5:28)** *See also* [2SA 11:2–11:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam11:2-2Sam11:3); [JOB 31:1](https://ref.ly/Job31:1), [JOB 31:9](https://ref.ly/Job31:9); [JER 5:8](https://ref.ly/Jer5:8); [MAT 15:19](https://ref.ly/Matt15:19)

### It is seductive

**[PRO 7:14–7:21](https://ref.ly/Prov7:14-Prov7:21)** *See also* [PRO 5:3](https://ref.ly/Prov5:3), [PRO 5:20](https://ref.ly/Prov5:20)

### It is secretive

[JOB 24:15](https://ref.ly/Job24:15); ; [PRO 7:8–7:10](https://ref.ly/Prov7:8-Prov7:10), [PRO 30:20](https://ref.ly/Prov30:20)

### It is a snare to the unwary

[PRO 7:7](https://ref.ly/Prov7:7), [PRO 22:14](https://ref.ly/Prov22:14); ; [ECC 7:26](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:26)

### It is resisted by the wise

**[PRO 2:16](https://ref.ly/Prov2:16)** *See also* [GEN 39:7–39:12](https://ref.ly/Gen39:7-Gen39:12); [PRO 7:4–7:5](https://ref.ly/Prov7:4-Prov7:5)

Adultery breaks the marriage covenant
-------------------------------------

**[PRO 2:17](https://ref.ly/Prov2:17)** *See also* [HOS 2:2](https://ref.ly/Hos2:2); [MAL 2:14](https://ref.ly/Mal2:14)

The consequences of adultery
----------------------------

### It destroys individuals and society

**[PRO 6:32–6:34](https://ref.ly/Prov6:32-Prov6:34)** *See also* [PRO 5:4–5:5](https://ref.ly/Prov5:4-Prov5:5), [PRO 5:9–5:11](https://ref.ly/Prov5:9-Prov5:11), [PRO 6:26–6:29](https://ref.ly/Prov6:26-Prov6:29), [PRO 7:22–7:27](https://ref.ly/Prov7:22-Prov7:27); [JOB 31:11–31:12](https://ref.ly/Job31:11-Job31:12)

### It was punishable by death under OT law

**[LEV 20:10](https://ref.ly/Lev20:10)** *See also* [DEU 22:22](https://ref.ly/Deut22:22), [DEU 22:23–22:24](https://ref.ly/Deut22:23-Deut22:24); [JHN 8:4–8:5](https://ref.ly/John8:4-John8:5)

### Adulterers face God's judgment

**[HEB 13:4](https://ref.ly/Heb13:4)** *See also* [2SA 12:11–12:12](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:11-2Sam12:12); [MAL 3:5](https://ref.ly/Mal3:5); [1CO 6:9](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:9); [REV 2:22](https://ref.ly/Rev2:22)

Remarriage after divorce may be adultery
----------------------------------------

**[MAT 19:9](https://ref.ly/Matt19:9)** parallel [MRK 10:11](https://ref.ly/Mark10:11) *See also* [MAT 5:32](https://ref.ly/Matt5:32); [LUK 16:18](https://ref.ly/Luke16:18); [ROM 7:3](https://ref.ly/Rom7:3)

Hypocrisy in relation to adultery
---------------------------------

**[ROM 2:22](https://ref.ly/Rom2:22)** *See also* [2SA 12:5–12:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:5-2Sam12:6); [HOS 4:14](https://ref.ly/Hos4:14); [JHN 8:7–8:9](https://ref.ly/John8:7-John8:9)

--------------------

## 6243: adultery, spiritual (id: 6243)

In Scripture there is a close link between sexual sin and spiritual corruption and immorality as promoted by false teachers. Scripture frequently uses the language of sexual sin to expose the infidelity of God's people.

The link between sexual sin and spiritual adultery
--------------------------------------------------

### In practice

**[NUM 25:1–25:3](https://ref.ly/Num25:1-Num25:3)** *See also* [EXO 34:15](https://ref.ly/Exod34:15); [HOS 4:14](https://ref.ly/Hos4:14)

### In false teaching

**[REV 2:20–2:25](https://ref.ly/Rev2:20-Rev2:25)** *See also* [NUM 31:15–31:16](https://ref.ly/Num31:15-Num31:16); [2TI 3:6](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:6); [2PE 2:13–2:15](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:13-2Pet2:15); [JUD 1:4](https://ref.ly/Jude1:4), [JUD 1:8](https://ref.ly/Jude1:8); [REV 2:14–2:16](https://ref.ly/Rev2:14-Rev2:16)

Spiritual adultery and God's covenant relationship with his people
------------------------------------------------------------------

### God as a husband to his people

**[EZK 16:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:8)** *The spiritual relationship between God and his people is defined in terms of the intimate and exclusive bond of marriage.* *See also* [ISA 54:5](https://ref.ly/Isa54:5); [JER 3:14](https://ref.ly/Jer3:14), [JER 31:32](https://ref.ly/Jer31:32); [EPH 5:31–5:32](https://ref.ly/Eph5:31-Eph5:32)

### God is jealous for his people's affections

**[EXO 34:14](https://ref.ly/Exod34:14)** *Just as husband and wife are jealous for their relationship in love, so God is jealous for the affections of his people.* *See also* [EXO 20:4–20:5](https://ref.ly/Exod20:4-Exod20:5); [DEU 4:23–4:24](https://ref.ly/Deut4:23-Deut4:24), [DEU 6:13–6:15](https://ref.ly/Deut6:13-Deut6:15)

The history of spiritual adultery among God's people
----------------------------------------------------

### Before Israel's kings

**[DEU 31:16](https://ref.ly/Deut31:16)** *See also* [LEV 17:7–17:9](https://ref.ly/Lev17:7-Lev17:9), [LEV 20:4–20:6](https://ref.ly/Lev20:4-Lev20:6); [JDG 2:16–2:17](https://ref.ly/Judg2:16-Judg2:17), [JDG 8:27](https://ref.ly/Judg8:27), [JDG 8:33–8:34](https://ref.ly/Judg8:33-Judg8:34)

### In the northern kingdom of Israel

**[HOS 1:2](https://ref.ly/Hos1:2)** *See also* [1CH 5:25](https://ref.ly/1Chr5:25); [EZK 23:1–23:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek23:1-Ezek23:8); [HOS 2:2–2:3](https://ref.ly/Hos2:2-Hos2:3), [HOS 4:10–4:12](https://ref.ly/Hos4:10-Hos4:12), [HOS 5:3–5:4](https://ref.ly/Hos5:3-Hos5:4)

### In the southern kingdom of Judah

**[JER 3:1–3:3](https://ref.ly/Jer3:1-Jer3:3)** *See also* [2CH 21:10–21:11](https://ref.ly/2Chr21:10-2Chr21:11); [ISA 57:3–57:8](https://ref.ly/Isa57:3-Isa57:8); [JER 2:20](https://ref.ly/Jer2:20), [JER 5:7–5:8](https://ref.ly/Jer5:7-Jer5:8), [JER 23:13–23:14](https://ref.ly/Jer23:13-Jer23:14); [EZK 16:15–16:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:15-Ezek16:22), [EZK 23:11–23:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek23:11-Ezek23:21)

### In Jesus Christ's generation

**[MAT 12:38–12:39](https://ref.ly/Matt12:38-Matt12:39)** *See also* [MAT 16:4](https://ref.ly/Matt16:4)

God's judgment on spiritual adultery
------------------------------------

**[JER 19:3–19:5](https://ref.ly/Jer19:3-Jer19:5)** *See also* [JER 3:6–3:10](https://ref.ly/Jer3:6-Jer3:10), [JER 16:10–16:13](https://ref.ly/Jer16:10-Jer16:13); [EZK 23:36–23:49](https://ref.ly/Ezek23:36-Ezek23:49)

## 6245: stubbornness (id: 6245)

Proud and disobedient resistance to God's will and rejection of his commands.

Stubbornness is an attitude of heart
------------------------------------

**[JER 7:24](https://ref.ly/Jer7:24)** *See also* [DEU 9:27](https://ref.ly/Deut9:27); [JDG 2:19](https://ref.ly/Judg2:19); [PSA 78:8](https://ref.ly/Ps78:8); [ISA 48:4](https://ref.ly/Isa48:4); [JER 3:17](https://ref.ly/Jer3:17), [JER 5:3](https://ref.ly/Jer5:3), [JER 9:14](https://ref.ly/Jer9:14), [JER 16:12](https://ref.ly/Jer16:12), [JER 18:12](https://ref.ly/Jer18:12); [HOS 4:16](https://ref.ly/Hos4:16); [ZEC 7:11](https://ref.ly/Zech7:11)

------------------------------------------

## 6248: temptation (id: 6248)

Pressure to yield to influences that can lead people away from God and into sin.

* **Associated Articles:** 6249: temptation, universality of (ID: `6249@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6250: temptation, sources of (ID: `6250@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6251: temptation, resisting (ID: `6251@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6252: temptation, and Jesus Christ (ID: `6252@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6253: temptation, avoiding causing (ID: `6253@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6249: temptation, universality of (id: 6249)

Scripture makes clear that all human beings are subject to temptation. It provides examples of individuals who have faced and yielded to such influences.

The inevitability of temptation to do wrong
-------------------------------------------

**[1CO 10:13](https://ref.ly/1Cor10:13)** *See also* [PRO 7:21–7:23](https://ref.ly/Prov7:21-Prov7:23); [MAT 13:20–13:21](https://ref.ly/Matt13:20-Matt13:21) parallels [MRK 4:16–4:17](https://ref.ly/Mark4:16-Mark4:17), [LUK 8:13](https://ref.ly/Luke8:13); [LUK 17:1](https://ref.ly/Luke17:1); [ROM 7:15](https://ref.ly/Rom7:15); [1CO 10:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor10:12); [2CO 11:3](https://ref.ly/2Cor11:3); [1PE 1:6](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:6)

----------------------------------

**[GEN 3:6–3:7](https://ref.ly/Gen3:6-Gen3:7)** *Sin enters the world through temptation, which leads to the fall of humanity.*

*See also* [GEN 25:29–25:34](https://ref.ly/Gen25:29-Gen25:34)

## 6251: temptation, resisting (id: 6251)

Being tempted is not in itself a sin. Sin arises when believers give in to temptation. Scripture urges believers to resist temptation, and gives them encouragement to face it.

Encouragement to those facing temptation
----------------------------------------

**[JAS 1:12](https://ref.ly/Jas1:12)** *See also* [ROM 8:37](https://ref.ly/Rom8:37); [HEB 2:18](https://ref.ly/Heb2:18), [HEB 4:15–4:16](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15-Heb4:16); [JAS 1:2–1:3](https://ref.ly/Jas1:2-Jas1:3); [1JN 4:4](https://ref.ly/1John4:4)

Finding in God and his word resources to overcome temptation
------------------------------------------------------------

**[DAN 11:32](https://ref.ly/Dan11:32)** *See also* [PRO 2:1–2:2](https://ref.ly/Prov2:1-Prov2:2), [PRO 2:12–2:15](https://ref.ly/Prov2:12-Prov2:15); [MAT 6:13](https://ref.ly/Matt6:13) parallel [LUK 11:4](https://ref.ly/Luke11:4); [1TI 6:11–6:12](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:11-1Tim6:12); [JAS 4:7](https://ref.ly/Jas4:7)

## 6252: temptation, and Jesus Christ (id: 6252)

Jesus Christ, like every other human being, knew temptation. However, he never yielded to it. The sinlessness of Christ refers to his obedient refusal to give in to temptation. It does not mean that he did not experience temptation himself.

The temptation of Jesus Christ
------------------------------

**[MRK 1:13](https://ref.ly/Mark1:13)** parallels [MAT 4:1–4:10](https://ref.ly/Matt4:1-Matt4:10), [LUK 4:1–4:13](https://ref.ly/Luke4:1-Luke4:13)

The temptation to avoid the cross
---------------------------------

**[MAT 16:21–16:23](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21-Matt16:23)** parallel [MRK 8:31–8:33](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31-Mark8:33) *See also* [MAT 26:36–26:44](https://ref.ly/Matt26:36-Matt26:44) parallels [MRK 14:32–14:42](https://ref.ly/Mark14:32-Mark14:42), [LUK 22:40–22:46](https://ref.ly/Luke22:40-Luke22:46); [MAT 27:39–27:44](https://ref.ly/Matt27:39-Matt27:44) parallels [MRK 15:31–15:32](https://ref.ly/Mark15:31-Mark15:32), [LUK 23:36–23:37](https://ref.ly/Luke23:36-Luke23:37), [LUK 23:39](https://ref.ly/Luke23:39)

The temptation to please the crowd
----------------------------------

**[LUK 11:16](https://ref.ly/Luke11:16)** *See also* [MAT 12:38–12:39](https://ref.ly/Matt12:38-Matt12:39) parallel [LUK 11:29](https://ref.ly/Luke11:29); [JHN 2:18](https://ref.ly/John2:18), [JHN 6:30](https://ref.ly/John6:30)

## 6500: Salvation (id: 6500)

* 6510: salvation
* **Associated Articles:** 6510: salvation (ID: `6510@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6510: salvation (id: 6510)

The transformation of a person's individual nature and relationship with God as a result of repentance and faith in the atoning death of Jesus Christ on the cross. All humanity stands in need of salvation, which is only possible through faith in Jesus Christ.

* **Associated Articles:** 6511: salvation, nature of (ID: `6511@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6512: salvation, necessity and basis of (ID: `6512@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6513: Saviour, God as (ID: `6513@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6514: Saviour, Jesus Christ as (ID: `6514@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6511: salvation, nature of (id: 6511)

Salvation involves a change in the relationship between God and a person. Salvation includes God's adoption of believers into his family, his acceptance of them as righteous and his forgiveness of their sins. It also includes personal renewal and transformation through the work of the Holy Spirit.

Salvation as a change in status before God
------------------------------------------

### Access to God

**[ROM 5:1–5:2](https://ref.ly/Rom5:1-Rom5:2)** *See also* [EPH 2:13](https://ref.ly/Eph2:13); [HEB 4:16](https://ref.ly/Heb4:16)

### Adoption into the family of God

[JHN 1:12](https://ref.ly/John1:12); ; [ROM 8:22–8:24](https://ref.ly/Rom8:22-Rom8:24); ; [GAL 4:4–4:7](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4-Gal4:7)

### Forgiveness of sin

**[ACT 5:30–5:31](https://ref.ly/Acts5:30-Acts5:31)** *See also* [PSA 32:1–32:2](https://ref.ly/Ps32:1-Ps32:2); [MAT 26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:28); [ACT 10:43](https://ref.ly/Acts10:43), [ACT 13:38](https://ref.ly/Acts13:38); [EPH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Eph1:7); [COL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Col2:13)

## 6512: salvation, necessity and basis of (id: 6512)

Scripture stresses that fallen human beings are cut off from God on account of their sin. All need to be saved, if they are to enter into a new relationship with God as their Creator and Redeemer. Salvation is not the result of human achievement, privilege or wisdom, but depends totally upon the graciousness of a loving God, supremely expressed in the cross of Jesus Christ. People must respond in repentance and faith if they are to benefit from God's offer of salvation in Christ.

The necessity of salvation
--------------------------

### The universal rule of sin in human nature

[ISA 64:6](https://ref.ly/Isa64:6); ; [ROM 3:19–3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:19-Rom3:23), [ROM 5:12–5:18](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12-Rom5:18), [ROM 7:24](https://ref.ly/Rom7:24); ; [EPH 2:3](https://ref.ly/Eph2:3)

### Sin cuts humanity off from God

**[ISA 59:1–59:2](https://ref.ly/Isa59:1-Isa59:2)** *See also* [GEN 3:22–3:24](https://ref.ly/Gen3:22-Gen3:24); [EPH 2:1–2:5](https://ref.ly/Eph2:1-Eph2:5), [EPH 4:18](https://ref.ly/Eph4:18)

### Sin enslaves humanity to evil

[JER 13:23](https://ref.ly/Jer13:23); ; [HOS 5:4](https://ref.ly/Hos5:4); ; [ZEC 7:11–7:12](https://ref.ly/Zech7:11-Zech7:12); ; [ROM 7:14–7:20](https://ref.ly/Rom7:14-Rom7:20); ; [2PE 2:13–2:19](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:13-2Pet2:19)

## 6602: acceptance (id: 6602)

The favourable reception of someone or something. God in his grace accepts human beings, their worship and their offerings. People are called to accept Jesus Christ and the message of the gospel and to respond to being accepted by accepting one another.

* **Associated Articles:** 6603: acceptance, divine (ID: `6603@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6604: acceptance, human (ID: `6604@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6603: acceptance, divine (id: 6603)

God's gracious favour shown both to Israel and to the Gentiles. God accepts people who respond to him, and worship that is offered sincerely and is accompanied by wholehearted commitment.

God's acceptance of human beings
--------------------------------

### God's gracious acceptance of Israel

**[2KI 13:23](https://ref.ly/2Kgs13:23)** *See also* [EZK 20:40–20:41](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:40-Ezek20:41); [ROM 11:1](https://ref.ly/Rom11:1)

### God's acceptance of those who respond to him

### God's acceptance of the Gentiles

**[ROM 15:16](https://ref.ly/Rom15:16)** *See also* [ISA 56:6–56:7](https://ref.ly/Isa56:6-Isa56:7); [ACT 10:34–10:35](https://ref.ly/Acts10:34-Acts10:35), [ACT 15:7–15:8](https://ref.ly/Acts15:7-Acts15:8)

## 6604: acceptance, human (id: 6604)

The response of human beings to the revelation and grace of God. It is seen in receiving Jesus Christ, his words and the message of the gospel, and in the acceptance of one another for his sake. Believers are called, too, to accept instruction and discipline and to submit to God's will for their lives.

Human beings are to accept Jesus Christ
---------------------------------------

### Receiving Jesus Christ

**[JHN 1:12](https://ref.ly/John1:12)** *See also* [COL 2:6](https://ref.ly/Col2:6)

### Accepting Jesus Christ by accepting others

**[JHN 13:20](https://ref.ly/John13:20)** *See also* [MAT 10:40](https://ref.ly/Matt10:40), [MAT 18:5](https://ref.ly/Matt18:5) parallels [MRK 9:37](https://ref.ly/Mark9:37), [LUK 9:48](https://ref.ly/Luke9:48); [LUK 10:16](https://ref.ly/Luke10:16); [JHN 12:44](https://ref.ly/John12:44)

### Accepting Jesus Christ's words

**[JHN 17:8](https://ref.ly/John17:8)** *See also* [MAT 11:14](https://ref.ly/Matt11:14), [MAT 19:11–19:12](https://ref.ly/Matt19:11-Matt19:12); [JHN 3:33–3:34](https://ref.ly/John3:33-John3:34)

### Refusing to accept Jesus Christ and his words

[JHN 1:11](https://ref.ly/John1:11), [JHN 3:11](https://ref.ly/John3:11), [JHN 3:32](https://ref.ly/John3:32), [JHN 5:43–5:44](https://ref.ly/John5:43-John5:44), [JHN 6:60](https://ref.ly/John6:60)

Acceptance of the gospel
------------------------

### The gospel is worthy of acceptance

**[1TI 1:15](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:15)**; **[JAS 1:21](https://ref.ly/Jas1:21)** *See also* [MAT 13:23](https://ref.ly/Matt13:23) parallels [MRK 4:20](https://ref.ly/Mark4:20), [LUK 8:15](https://ref.ly/Luke8:15); [1CO 15:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:3); [1TI 4:9–4:10](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:9-1Tim4:10)

## 6606: access to God (id: 6606)

The privilege of entering into the presence of God through the work of Jesus Christ.

Only the pure have access to God
--------------------------------

**[PSA 24:3–24:4](https://ref.ly/Ps24:3-Ps24:4)**; **[1JN 3:21–3:22](https://ref.ly/1John3:21-1John3:22)** *See also* [PSA 41:12](https://ref.ly/Ps41:12), [PSA 66:18–66:19](https://ref.ly/Ps66:18-Ps66:19), [PSA 73:28](https://ref.ly/Ps73:28); [MAT 5:8](https://ref.ly/Matt5:8); [1PE 3:12](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:12); [PSA 34:15–34:16](https://ref.ly/Ps34:15-Ps34:16)

The wicked do not have access to God
------------------------------------

**[PSA 101:7](https://ref.ly/Ps101:7)**; **[ISA 59:2](https://ref.ly/Isa59:2)** *See also* [GEN 4:14](https://ref.ly/Gen4:14), [GEN 4:16](https://ref.ly/Gen4:16); [LEV 22:3](https://ref.ly/Lev22:3); [DEU 31:18](https://ref.ly/Deut31:18); [PSA 5:5](https://ref.ly/Ps5:5); [ISA 1:15](https://ref.ly/Isa1:15), [ISA 64:7](https://ref.ly/Isa64:7); [JER 7:15](https://ref.ly/Jer7:15), [JER 15:1](https://ref.ly/Jer15:1), [JER 23:39](https://ref.ly/Jer23:39), [JER 52:3](https://ref.ly/Jer52:3); [EZK 39:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:23); [HOS 5:6](https://ref.ly/Hos5:6); [MIC 3:4](https://ref.ly/Mic3:4)

## 6608: adoption (id: 6608)

The deliberate action by which a family gives to a person all the privileges of being a member of that family.

* **Associated Articles:** 6609: adoption, nature of (ID: `6609@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6610: adoption, descriptions of (ID: `6610@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6611: adoption, privileges and duties of (ID: `6611@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6609: adoption, nature of (id: 6609)

The giving by God of the status and privileges of being his children. God adopts those who believe in him and grants them the benefits of his salvation.

A family adopts a child
-----------------------

**[GEN 15:3](https://ref.ly/Gen15:3)** *See also* [GEN 48:5](https://ref.ly/Gen48:5); [EXO 2:10](https://ref.ly/Exod2:10); [EST 2:7](https://ref.ly/Esth2:7)

-------------------------------

## 6610: adoption, descriptions of (id: 6610)

The words used by the NT to describe believers point to their status and privileges as the adopted children of God.

Believers are no longer slaves but sons
---------------------------------------

**[GAL 4:7–4:9](https://ref.ly/Gal4:7-Gal4:9)** *See also* [JHN 8:34–8:36](https://ref.ly/John8:34-John8:36); [ROM 8:15](https://ref.ly/Rom8:15); [PHM 1:16](https://ref.ly/Phlm1:16)

Believers are children of God
-----------------------------

**[1JN 3:1–3:2](https://ref.ly/1John3:1-1John3:2)** *The title “child of God” is thought by some to be distinct from that of “son of God” (see below). “child” is thought to emphasise God's fatherhood, whilst “son” is thought to emphasise the Christian's privileges. These terms are however, sometimes used interchangeably.* *See also* [LUK 20:36](https://ref.ly/Luke20:36); [ROM 8:21](https://ref.ly/Rom8:21); [PHP 2:15](https://ref.ly/Phil2:15); [1JN 3:2](https://ref.ly/1John3:2), [1JN 5:2](https://ref.ly/1John5:2)

Believers are sons of God
-------------------------

**[ROM 8:14](https://ref.ly/Rom8:14)** *See also* [ROM 9:26](https://ref.ly/Rom9:26); [GAL 3:26](https://ref.ly/Gal3:26)

Believers are children of the resurrection
------------------------------------------

[LUK 20:36](https://ref.ly/Luke20:36)

Believers are children of light, sons of light
----------------------------------------------

[JHN 12:36](https://ref.ly/John12:36); ; [EPH 5:8](https://ref.ly/Eph5:8); ; [1TH 5:5](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:5)

Believers are heirs of God
--------------------------

**[ROM 8:17](https://ref.ly/Rom8:17)** *See also* [GAL 3:29](https://ref.ly/Gal3:29), [GAL 4:7](https://ref.ly/Gal4:7); [TIT 3:7](https://ref.ly/Titus3:7); [HEB 6:17](https://ref.ly/Heb6:17)

Believers are brothers of Jesus Christ
--------------------------------------

**[HEB 2:11–2:12](https://ref.ly/Heb2:11-Heb2:12)** *See also* [MAT 12:48–12:50](https://ref.ly/Matt12:48-Matt12:50); [ROM 8:29](https://ref.ly/Rom8:29); [HEB 2:17](https://ref.ly/Heb2:17)

-----------------------------------------

**[1JN 3:14](https://ref.ly/1John3:14)** *See also* [1JN 4:19–4:20](https://ref.ly/1John4:19-1John4:20); [REV 12:10](https://ref.ly/Rev12:10), [REV 19:10](https://ref.ly/Rev19:10)

**[EPH 2:19](https://ref.ly/Eph2:19)** *See also* [GAL 6:10](https://ref.ly/Gal6:10); [HEB 3:2–3:6](https://ref.ly/Heb3:2-Heb3:6)

## 6611: adoption, privileges and duties of (id: 6611)

As adopted members of the family of God, believers receive both the privileges and responsibilities of being children of God.

The privileges received by believers through adoption
-----------------------------------------------------

### Believers are given the Spirit of adoption

**[GAL 4:6](https://ref.ly/Gal4:6)** *See also* [ROM 8:15](https://ref.ly/Rom8:15)

### Believers have access to their heavenly Father

**[EPH 2:18](https://ref.ly/Eph2:18)** *See also* [EPH 3:12](https://ref.ly/Eph3:12); [HEB 4:16](https://ref.ly/Heb4:16)

### Believers become heirs with Christ of heaven

**[ROM 8:17](https://ref.ly/Rom8:17)** *See also* [GAL 3:29](https://ref.ly/Gal3:29), [GAL 4:7](https://ref.ly/Gal4:7); [COL 1:12](https://ref.ly/Col1:12); [1PE 1:4](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:4)

The benefits God gives to those he adopts
-----------------------------------------

### Believers are pitied by him

**[PSA 103:13](https://ref.ly/Ps103:13)**

### Believers are protected

**[PRO 14:26](https://ref.ly/Prov14:26)**

### Believers are provided for

**[MAT 6:31–6:33](https://ref.ly/Matt6:31-Matt6:33)**

### Believers receive loving discipline

**[HEB 12:6](https://ref.ly/Heb12:6)**

### Believers are never forsaken

**[PSA 94:14](https://ref.ly/Ps94:14)**

### Believers are assured by the Spirit

**[ROM 8:16](https://ref.ly/Rom8:16)**

----------------------------------------------

*See also* [JHN 12:35–12:36](https://ref.ly/John12:35-John12:36); [EPH 5:8](https://ref.ly/Eph5:8); [1TH 5:4–5:5](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:4-1Thess5:5)

## 6614: atonement (id: 6614)

Reconciliation; sin has alienated humanity from God and provoked God's anger. God has responded by providing the means of restoring this broken relationship, bringing both sides to a place where they are at one again (“at\-one\-ment”).

* **Associated Articles:** 6615: atonement, necessity and nature of (ID: `6615@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6616: atonement, in OT (ID: `6616@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6617: atonement, in NT (ID: `6617@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6615: atonement, necessity and nature of (id: 6615)

Scripture stresses the seriousness and reality of human sin, and that human beings are unable to atone for their own sins. In his grace, God provides a means by which the situation can be remedied.

Atonement is necessary because of human sinfulness
--------------------------------------------------

### Atonement is necessary because sin cuts people off from God

**[ISA 59:2](https://ref.ly/Isa59:2)** *See also* [ISA 64:7](https://ref.ly/Isa64:7); [EZK 39:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:23); [HAB 1:13](https://ref.ly/Hab1:13); [JHN 9:31](https://ref.ly/John9:31)

### Atonement is necessary because sin provokes God's wrath

**[EPH 2:1–2:3](https://ref.ly/Eph2:1-Eph2:3)** *See also* [GEN 6:5–6:7](https://ref.ly/Gen6:5-Gen6:7); [EXO 32:30–32:35](https://ref.ly/Exod32:30-Exod32:35); [ROM 1:18–1:20](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18-Rom1:20), [ROM 2:8](https://ref.ly/Rom2:8)

God's gracious nature is the basis for atonement
------------------------------------------------

### Atonement is grounded in God's reluctance to punish sinners

**[EZK 18:32](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:32)** *See also* [EZK 33:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek33:11); [1TI 2:1–2:4](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:1-1Tim2:4); [2PE 3:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:9)

### Atonement is grounded in God's readiness to forgive sin

**[EXO 34:6–34:7](https://ref.ly/Exod34:6-Exod34:7)** *The punishment of subsequent generations makes God's abhorrence of sin quite clear, but the extension of his love and forgiveness “to thousands” puts the emphasis in these verses on God's grace and compassion.* *See also* [PSA 145:8](https://ref.ly/Ps145:8); [DAN 9:9](https://ref.ly/Dan9:9); [JON 4:2](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:2)

### Atonement is grounded in God's covenant love

**[NUM 14:19](https://ref.ly/Num14:19)** *The Hebrew word for “great love” means God's loving faithfulness to those within the covenant.* *See also* [PSA 25:6–25:7](https://ref.ly/Ps25:6-Ps25:7), [PSA 103:8–103:12](https://ref.ly/Ps103:8-Ps103:12); [JOL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Joel2:13)

God's provision of atonement is a means of dealing with sin
-----------------------------------------------------------

### Atonement through sacrifice

**[LEV 9:7](https://ref.ly/Lev9:7)** *See also* [EXO 30:10](https://ref.ly/Exod30:10); [NUM 15:22–15:26](https://ref.ly/Num15:22-Num15:26)

### God's promised new covenant of forgiveness was fulfilled in Jesus Christ's atoning death

**[HEB 10:16–10:17](https://ref.ly/Heb10:16-Heb10:17)** *See also* [JER 31:33–31:34](https://ref.ly/Jer31:33-Jer31:34); [MAT 26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:28); [HEB 9:15](https://ref.ly/Heb9:15), [HEB 12:24](https://ref.ly/Heb12:24)

Images used to portray the at\-one\-ment, or restored relationship, between God and humanity
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Atonement as forgiveness of sins

**[EPH 1:7–1:8](https://ref.ly/Eph1:7-Eph1:8)** *See also* [LEV 19:22](https://ref.ly/Lev19:22); [ACT 13:38](https://ref.ly/Acts13:38); [COL 2:13–2:14](https://ref.ly/Col2:13-Col2:14)

### Atonement as cleansing and purification

**[LEV 16:30](https://ref.ly/Lev16:30)** *See also* [ISA 6:6–6:7](https://ref.ly/Isa6:6-Isa6:7); [TIT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:14); [1JN 1:7](https://ref.ly/1John1:7); [REV 7:14](https://ref.ly/Rev7:14)

### Atonement as reconciliation

**[2CO 5:19](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:19)** *See also* [ROM 5:9–5:11](https://ref.ly/Rom5:9-Rom5:11); [EPH 2:14–2:16](https://ref.ly/Eph2:14-Eph2:16)

### Atonement as healing

**[1PE 2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:24)** *See also* [2CH 7:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:14); [PSA 103:2–103:3](https://ref.ly/Ps103:2-Ps103:3); [ISA 53:5](https://ref.ly/Isa53:5)

### Atonement as God buying people back for himself

**[REV 5:9](https://ref.ly/Rev5:9)** *See also* [MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28) parallel [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45); [ACT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Acts20:28); [1PE 1:18–1:19](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:18-1Pet1:19)

### Atonement as making holy: creating a relationship of consecrated nearness to God

**[HEB 10:10](https://ref.ly/Heb10:10)** *See also* [COL 1:22](https://ref.ly/Col1:22); [HEB 13:12](https://ref.ly/Heb13:12)

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 59:2; Isaiah 64:7; Ezekiel 39:23; Habakkuk 1:13; John 9:31; Ephesians 2:1-3; Genesis 6:5-7; Exodus 32:30-35; Romans 1:18-20; Romans 2:8; Ezekiel 18:32; Ezekiel 33:11; 1 Timothy 2:1-4; 2 Peter 3:9; Exodus 34:6-7; Psalms 145:8; Daniel 9:9; Jonah 4:2; Numbers 14:19; Psalms 25:6-7; Psalms 103:8-12; Joel 2:13; Leviticus 9:7; Exodus 30:10; Numbers 15:22-26; Hebrews 10:16-17; Jeremiah 31:33-34; Matthew 26:28; Hebrews 9:15; Hebrews 12:24; Ephesians 1:7-8; Leviticus 19:22; Acts 13:38; Colossians 2:13-14; Leviticus 16:30; Isaiah 6:6-7; Titus 2:14; 1 John 1:7; Revelation 7:14; 2 Corinthians 5:19; Romans 5:9-11; Ephesians 2:14-16; 1 Peter 2:24; 2 Chronicles 7:14; Psalms 103:2-3; Isaiah 53:5; Revelation 5:9; Matthew 20:28; Mark 10:45; Acts 20:28; 1 Peter 1:18-19; Hebrews 10:10; Colossians 1:22; Hebrews 13:12
* **Associated Articles:** 1055: God, grace and mercy of (ID: `1055@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6025: sin, and God's character (ID: `6025@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6510: salvation (ID: `6510@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6653: forgiveness, divine (ID: `6653@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6717: reconciliation, of the world to God (ID: `6717@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6720: redemption (ID: `6720@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7314: blood (ID: `7314@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8266: holiness (ID: `8266@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6616: atonement, in OT (id: 6616)

The OT laid down complex regulations by which the guilt of sin could be removed through the sacrificial system. Particular emphasis was placed upon the role of the high priest, who was required to make annual atonement for the sins of the people.

The covenantal framework of atonement
-------------------------------------

### As God's covenant partners, the Israelites undertook to keep his laws

**[EXO 24:3](https://ref.ly/Exod24:3)** *See also* [DEU 26:17](https://ref.ly/Deut26:17); [JOS 24:24](https://ref.ly/Josh24:24)

### The sin offering made atonement for unintentional sins under the covenant

**[LEV 9:7](https://ref.ly/Lev9:7)** *See also* [LEV 4:13–4:14](https://ref.ly/Lev4:13-Lev4:14); [NUM 15:22–15:26](https://ref.ly/Num15:22-Num15:26)

### The guilt offering atoned for sins where reparation was required

**[LEV 19:20–19:22](https://ref.ly/Lev19:20-Lev19:22)** *See also* [LEV 6:1–6:7](https://ref.ly/Lev6:1-Lev6:7)

### Deliberate flouting of God's law could not be atoned for

**[NUM 15:30–15:31](https://ref.ly/Num15:30-Num15:31)** *See also* [NUM 35:33](https://ref.ly/Num35:33); [1SA 3:14](https://ref.ly/1Sam3:14)

### The Day of Atonement provided for the removal of the nation's sin

**[LEV 16:34](https://ref.ly/Lev16:34)** *See also* [EXO 30:10](https://ref.ly/Exod30:10); [LEV 16:1–16:33](https://ref.ly/Lev16:1-Lev16:33) *The nation's sin was atoned for by sprinkling the atonement cover in the Most Holy Place with the blood of the sacrificial goat; the removal of the people's sin was symbolised by the driving of the scapegoat into the wilderness*; [HEB 9:7](https://ref.ly/Heb9:7)

### The atonement cover

**[EXO 25:17–25:22](https://ref.ly/Exod25:17-Exod25:22)** *The locating of God's presence above the atonement cover in the tabernacle demonstrated that it was only on the basis of atonement that God could accompany his people.* *See also* [EXO 30:6](https://ref.ly/Exod30:6); [LEV 16:2](https://ref.ly/Lev16:2); [NUM 7:89](https://ref.ly/Num7:89)

### Atonement was effected by the blood of the sacrifice

**[LEV 17:11](https://ref.ly/Lev17:11)** *The blood signified that the life of the animal had been given in place of that of the worshipper.* *See also* [HEB 9:22](https://ref.ly/Heb9:22)

The role of priests in making atonement
---------------------------------------

### Priests were dedicated to God in order to make atonement for others

**[EXO 29:44](https://ref.ly/Exod29:44)** *See also* [LEV 8:22–8:30](https://ref.ly/Lev8:22-Lev8:30)

### The priests had to make atonement for their own sins

**[HEB 5:1–5:3](https://ref.ly/Heb5:1-Heb5:3)** *See also* [LEV 9:8–9:11](https://ref.ly/Lev9:8-Lev9:11)

### The priests represented the people before God to atone for their sin

**[HEB 5:1](https://ref.ly/Heb5:1)** *See also* [EXO 28:36–28:38](https://ref.ly/Exod28:36-Exod28:38); [LEV 10:16–10:17](https://ref.ly/Lev10:16-Lev10:17)

The people had constant reminders of the need for atonement
-----------------------------------------------------------

### Rituals of cleansing included an atoning offering

[LEV 12:7–12:8](https://ref.ly/Lev12:7-Lev12:8), [LEV 14:18–14:22](https://ref.ly/Lev14:18-Lev14:22), [LEV 14:53](https://ref.ly/Lev14:53), [LEV 15:15](https://ref.ly/Lev15:15)

### Atonement was a feature of Israel's festivals

[NUM 28:22](https://ref.ly/Num28:22), [NUM 28:30](https://ref.ly/Num28:30), [NUM 29:5](https://ref.ly/Num29:5), [NUM 29:11](https://ref.ly/Num29:11)

Abuses of the system of atonement
---------------------------------

### The sinful conduct of the priests who made atonement

**[HOS 4:7–4:8](https://ref.ly/Hos4:7-Hos4:8)** *See also* [1SA 2:12–2:17](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:12-1Sam2:17); [JER 6:13–6:14](https://ref.ly/Jer6:13-Jer6:14); [EZK 22:26](https://ref.ly/Ezek22:26); [MAL 1:6–1:8](https://ref.ly/Mal1:6-Mal1:8)

### The sinful conduct of the people who sought atonement without repenting of their sins

**[HOS 8:11–8:13](https://ref.ly/Hos8:11-Hos8:13)** *See also* [ISA 1:10–1:17](https://ref.ly/Isa1:10-Isa1:17), [ISA 66:3](https://ref.ly/Isa66:3); [JER 7:21–7:24](https://ref.ly/Jer7:21-Jer7:24); [AMO 4:4](https://ref.ly/Amos4:4)

### The need for repentance for a relationship of atonement

**[PRO 16:6](https://ref.ly/Prov16:6)** *See also* [1SA 15:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:22); [PSA 51:16–51:17](https://ref.ly/Ps51:16-Ps51:17); [MIC 6:6–6:8](https://ref.ly/Mic6:6-Mic6:8)

The prophets foretold a renewing of God's relationship with Israel, involving atonement for sin
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Isaiah's message about the obedient servant

[ISA 53:4–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa53:4-Isa53:12)

### Jeremiah's prophecy of a new covenant

[JER 31:31–31:34](https://ref.ly/Jer31:31-Jer31:34)

### Ezekiel's vision of a new temple

[EZK 43:18–43:27](https://ref.ly/Ezek43:18-Ezek43:27)

* **Associated Passages:** Exodus 24:3; Deuteronomy 26:17; Joshua 24:24; Leviticus 9:7; Leviticus 4:13-14; Numbers 15:22-26; Leviticus 19:20-22; Leviticus 6:1-7; Numbers 15:30-31; Numbers 35:33; 1 Samuel 3:14; Leviticus 16:34; Exodus 30:10; Leviticus 16:1-33; Hebrews 9:7; Exodus 25:17-22; Exodus 30:6; Leviticus 16:2; Numbers 7:89; Leviticus 17:11; Hebrews 9:22; Exodus 29:44; Leviticus 8:22-30; Hebrews 5:1-3; Leviticus 9:8-11; Hebrews 5:1; Exodus 28:36-38; Leviticus 10:16-17; Leviticus 12:7-8; Leviticus 14:18-22; Leviticus 14:53; Leviticus 15:15; Numbers 28:22; Numbers 28:30; Numbers 29:5; Numbers 29:11; Hosea 4:7-8; 1 Samuel 2:12-17; Jeremiah 6:13-14; Ezekiel 22:26; Malachi 1:6-8; Hosea 8:11-13; Isaiah 1:10-17; Isaiah 66:3; Jeremiah 7:21-24; Amos 4:4; Proverbs 16:6; 1 Samuel 15:22; Psalms 51:16-17; Micah 6:6-8; Isaiah 53:4-12; Jeremiah 31:31-34; Ezekiel 43:18-27
* **Associated Articles:** 1345: covenant (ID: `1345@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6172: guilt (ID: `6172@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6648: expiation (ID: `6648@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6712: propitiation (ID: `6712@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7308: Atonement, Day of (ID: `7308@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7376: high priest (ID: `7376@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7412: priesthood (ID: `7412@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7435: sacrifice, in OT (ID: `7435@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7440: scapegoat (ID: `7440@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7444: sin offering (ID: `7444@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7454: sprinkling (ID: `7454@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8622: worship (ID: `8622@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6617: atonement, in NT (id: 6617)

In dying for the sins of the world, Jesus Christ fulfilled and replaced the OT sacrificial system, so that all who believe in him are restored to fellowship with God. Christ is the true high priest, who finally liberates his people from the guilt of sin, by offering himself as the supreme sacrifice.

The atoning purpose of Jesus Christ's death
-------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's death on behalf of others

**[JHN 10:11](https://ref.ly/John10:11)** *See also* [JHN 10:14–10:18](https://ref.ly/John10:14-John10:18); [2CO 5:15](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:15); [HEB 2:9](https://ref.ly/Heb2:9); [1JN 3:16](https://ref.ly/1John3:16)

### Jesus Christ's atoning death for sin

**[1CO 15:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:3)** *See also* [ROM 4:25](https://ref.ly/Rom4:25), [ROM 8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:3); [GAL 1:4](https://ref.ly/Gal1:4); [1PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:18)

### The atoning significance of Jesus Christ's death is expressed by references to his blood

**[ROM 5:9](https://ref.ly/Rom5:9)**; **[REV 5:9](https://ref.ly/Rev5:9)** *See also* [EPH 2:13](https://ref.ly/Eph2:13); [1PE 1:18–1:19](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:18-1Pet1:19); [1JN 1:7](https://ref.ly/1John1:7); [REV 7:14](https://ref.ly/Rev7:14)

### Jesus Christ's atoning death is commemorated in the Lord's Supper

**[1CO 11:23–11:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:23-1Cor11:25)** *See also* [MAT 26:26–26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:26-Matt26:28) parallels [MRK 14:22–14:24](https://ref.ly/Mark14:22-Mark14:24), [LUK 22:19–22:20](https://ref.ly/Luke22:19-Luke22:20)

Explanations of the atonement
-----------------------------

### Jesus Christ's death as an atoning sacrifice

**[ROM 3:25](https://ref.ly/Rom3:25)** *See also* [1CO 5:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:7); [EPH 5:2](https://ref.ly/Eph5:2); [1JN 4:10](https://ref.ly/1John4:10); [REV 5:6](https://ref.ly/Rev5:6)

### Jesus Christ's atoning death as redemption

**[MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45)** parallel [MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28) *See also* [ACT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Acts20:28); [GAL 3:13–3:14](https://ref.ly/Gal3:13-Gal3:14); [EPH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Eph1:7); [COL 1:13–1:14](https://ref.ly/Col1:13-Col1:14)

The atonement is effective because of Jesus Christ's sinlessness
----------------------------------------------------------------

**[2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21)** *See also* [HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15); [1PE 2:22–2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22-1Pet2:24); [1JN 3:5](https://ref.ly/1John3:5)

Jesus Christ's death fulfils and replaces the Day of Atonement
--------------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ makes atonement as the new high priest

[HEB 7:26–7:28](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26-Heb7:28)

### Jesus Christ is the mediator of the new and better covenant

[HEB 8:6–8:7](https://ref.ly/Heb8:6-Heb8:7), [HEB 9:15](https://ref.ly/Heb9:15)

### Jesus Christ has made atonement in the true heavenly sanctuary

[HEB 8:1–8:2](https://ref.ly/Heb8:1-Heb8:2), [HEB 9:24](https://ref.ly/Heb9:24)

### Jesus Christ's atoning blood brings effective cleansing

[HEB 9:12–9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:12-Heb9:14)

### Jesus Christ's single sacrifice replaces the many required under the old covenant

[HEB 10:11–10:14](https://ref.ly/Heb10:11-Heb10:14)

### Access to the heavenly sanctuary is now open

[HEB 10:19–10:20](https://ref.ly/Heb10:19-Heb10:20)

By dying with Christ, believers are released from this age into the life of the age to come
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**[ROM 6:1–6:7](https://ref.ly/Rom6:1-Rom6:7)** *See also* [ROM 7:4–7:6](https://ref.ly/Rom7:4-Rom7:6); [GAL 2:19–2:20](https://ref.ly/Gal2:19-Gal2:20), [GAL 6:14](https://ref.ly/Gal6:14); [EPH 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Eph2:6-Eph2:7); [COL 2:11–2:13](https://ref.ly/Col2:11-Col2:13)

God the Father and the atoning death of his Son
-----------------------------------------------

### God's sending of his Son to make atonement

**[1JN 4:14](https://ref.ly/1John4:14)** *See also* [JHN 3:16](https://ref.ly/John3:16); [ROM 8:32](https://ref.ly/Rom8:32); [2CO 5:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:18); [GAL 4:4–4:5](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4-Gal4:5)

### God's grace displayed in making atonement for the ungodly

**[EPH 2:4–2:5](https://ref.ly/Eph2:4-Eph2:5)** *See also* [ROM 5:6–5:8](https://ref.ly/Rom5:6-Rom5:8); [EPH 2:8–2:9](https://ref.ly/Eph2:8-Eph2:9); [TIT 3:4–3:5](https://ref.ly/Titus3:4-Titus3:5)

The worldwide scope of Jesus Christ's atoning death
---------------------------------------------------

## 6620: calling (id: 6620)

God's summoning of individuals and people to himself, so that they will belong to him and serve him in his world. The calling of a believer may involve a specific place, task or vocation in life.

God calls individuals to belong to him and serve him
----------------------------------------------------

### God calls all people everywhere

## 6622: choice (id: 6622)

A deliberate act of will or decision, in which God chooses individuals or peoples to be his or calls them to perform certain tasks or responsibilities. Human beings are also required to make choices, particularly between good and evil.

----------------------
