## 6626: conversion (id: 6626)

Turning or returning to God in repentance, faith and obedience by those who do not know God or who have turned from him. Although conversion can be seen as a human act or decision, Scripture stresses that the work of God lies behind this human decision, guiding and motivating it.

* **Associated Articles:** 6627: conversion, nature of (ID: `6627@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6628: conversion, God's demands for (ID: `6628@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6629: conversion, examples of (ID: `6629@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6627: conversion, nature of (id: 6627)

True repentance results in a turning from sin and an inner renewal which can only be brought about by God, who draws people to himself and who, through Jesus Christ, gives forgiveness and new life.

Conversion as turning to God
----------------------------

### Turning back to God

**[DEU 4:30–4:31](https://ref.ly/Deut4:30-Deut4:31)**; **[LUK 1:16–1:17](https://ref.ly/Luke1:16-Luke1:17)** *See also* [DEU 30:2–30:3](https://ref.ly/Deut30:2-Deut30:3), [DEU 30:10](https://ref.ly/Deut30:10); [LUK 22:32](https://ref.ly/Luke22:32); [JAS 5:19–5:20](https://ref.ly/Jas5:19-Jas5:20)

### Turning from idolatry

**[ACT 14:15](https://ref.ly/Acts14:15)** *See also* [1SA 7:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam7:3); [JER 3:12–3:13](https://ref.ly/Jer3:12-Jer3:13), [JER 4:1–4:2](https://ref.ly/Jer4:1-Jer4:2); [1TH 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/1Thess1:9-1Thess1:10)

### Turning from sinful ways

**[2KI 17:13–17:14](https://ref.ly/2Kgs17:13-2Kgs17:14)**; **[ISA 55:6–55:7](https://ref.ly/Isa55:6-Isa55:7)** *See also* [2KI 13:11](https://ref.ly/2Kgs13:11), [2KI 14:24](https://ref.ly/2Kgs14:24), [2KI 15:9](https://ref.ly/2Kgs15:9); [JER 18:11](https://ref.ly/Jer18:11), [JER 25:5](https://ref.ly/Jer25:5); [EZK 18:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:23); [DAN 9:13](https://ref.ly/Dan9:13)

Conversion as a turning away from unbelief to faith
---------------------------------------------------

### It is linked to repentance

**[ACT 3:19](https://ref.ly/Acts3:19)** *See also* [EZK 14:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek14:6), [EZK 18:30](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:30); [ACT 26:20](https://ref.ly/Acts26:20)

### It is linked to coming to faith

**[ACT 11:21](https://ref.ly/Acts11:21)**

## 6628: conversion, God's demands for (id: 6628)

Through his servants, God calls people to turn to him. He wants to save the world which is alienated from him, and to restore those of his backslidden people who return to him and renew their commitment to the covenant.

The need for conversion
-----------------------

### The world is alienated from God

**[ROM 1:21–1:23](https://ref.ly/Rom1:21-Rom1:23)** *See also* [ROM 1:28](https://ref.ly/Rom1:28), [ROM 3:11–3:12](https://ref.ly/Rom3:11-Rom3:12); [PSA 14:3](https://ref.ly/Ps14:3)

### The world does not know God

**[GAL 4:8](https://ref.ly/Gal4:8)** *See also* [1CO 1:21](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:21), [1CO 15:34](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:34); [1TH 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:5); [2TH 1:8](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:8)

### God's people have turned away from him

**[MAL 3:7](https://ref.ly/Mal3:7)** *See also* [NUM 14:43](https://ref.ly/Num14:43); [DEU 9:12](https://ref.ly/Deut9:12); [1SA 15:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:11) *Saul*; [1KI 11:9](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:9) *Solomon*; [2CH 25:27](https://ref.ly/2Chr25:27) *Amaziah*; [JER 8:5](https://ref.ly/Jer8:5); [EZK 6:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek6:9); [DAN 9:11](https://ref.ly/Dan9:11); [ACT 7:39](https://ref.ly/Acts7:39)

God's demands for the conversion of all people
----------------------------------------------

**[ISA 45:22](https://ref.ly/Isa45:22)**; **[ACT 17:30](https://ref.ly/Acts17:30)** *See also* [PSA 65:5](https://ref.ly/Ps65:5); [JON 4:11](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:11); [ZEC 9:10](https://ref.ly/Zech9:10)

God's demands for the conversion of his own people
--------------------------------------------------

### God's desire to save his people

**[EZK 33:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek33:11)** *See also* [JER 3:22](https://ref.ly/Jer3:22); [JOL 2:12–2:13](https://ref.ly/Joel2:12-Joel2:13); [ZEC 1:3](https://ref.ly/Zech1:3)

### God's faithfulness to his people

**[JER 3:14](https://ref.ly/Jer3:14)** *See also* [LEV 26:40–26:42](https://ref.ly/Lev26:40-Lev26:42); [2CH 30:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr30:9); [HOS 3:5](https://ref.ly/Hos3:5), [HOS 6:1–6:3](https://ref.ly/Hos6:1-Hos6:3)

### God's promise of restoration

**[2CH 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:13-2Chr7:14)** *See also* [1KI 8:48–8:49](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:48-1Kgs8:49) parallel [2CH 6:38–6:39](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:38-2Chr6:39); [NEH 1:9](https://ref.ly/Neh1:9)

---------------------------------------------

## 6632: conviction (id: 6632)

The proving of a person guilty of sin or a crime. Scripture stresses that God has declared the guilt, together with its consequences, of sinful humanity. The term can also refer to a state of being convinced; i.e., the holding of a strong belief, especially a conscious awareness of one's guilt and the atoning death of Jesus Christ as the means of remission of that guilt.

Conviction is proving a person guilty of sin or a crime
-------------------------------------------------------

### Proving someone guilty of sin

**[JHN 8:46](https://ref.ly/John8:46)** *See also* [JHN 16:8–16:9](https://ref.ly/John16:8-John16:9) *NIV footnote at verse 8*; [1CO 14:24](https://ref.ly/1Cor14:24); [JAS 2:9](https://ref.ly/Jas2:9); [JUD 1:15](https://ref.ly/Jude1:15)

### Proving someone guilty of a crime

**[DEU 19:15](https://ref.ly/Deut19:15)** *See also* [EXO 22:9](https://ref.ly/Exod22:9); [LEV 17:3–17:4](https://ref.ly/Lev17:3-Lev17:4)NUM [35:30](https://ref.ly/Lev35:30); [DEU 17:6](https://ref.ly/Deut17:6)[2SA 14:13](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:13); [PSA 5:10](https://ref.ly/Ps5:10), [PSA 109:7](https://ref.ly/Ps109:7); [PRO 24:25](https://ref.ly/Prov24:25)LUK [23:4](https://ref.ly/Prov23:4), [LUK 23:14](https://ref.ly/Luke23:14), [LUK 23:22](https://ref.ly/Luke23:22); [JHN 18:38](https://ref.ly/John18:38)ACT [24:13](https://ref.ly/John24:13), [ACT 25:7](https://ref.ly/Acts25:7)

God's conviction of sinful humanity
-----------------------------------

### He declares them to be guilty

**[ROM 3:19–3:20](https://ref.ly/Rom3:19-Rom3:20)** *See also* [PSA 5:9](https://ref.ly/Ps5:9), [PSA 10:7](https://ref.ly/Ps10:7), [PSA 14:1–14:3](https://ref.ly/Ps14:1-Ps14:3) parallel [PSA 53:1–53:3](https://ref.ly/Ps53:1-Ps53:3); [PSA 140:3](https://ref.ly/Ps140:3); [ECC 7:20](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:20); [ISA 59:7–59:8](https://ref.ly/Isa59:7-Isa59:8); [ROM 3:10–3:18](https://ref.ly/Rom3:10-Rom3:18)

### He also declares the consequences of their guilt

[GEN 2:17](https://ref.ly/Gen2:17), [GEN 3:17–3:19](https://ref.ly/Gen3:17-Gen3:19); ; [ROM 1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:32), [ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12), [ROM 5:16–5:19](https://ref.ly/Rom5:16-Rom5:19); ; [1CO 15:22](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:22)

Conviction as holding a strong belief
-------------------------------------

**[ROM 14:5](https://ref.ly/Rom14:5)** *See also* [GEN 45:28](https://ref.ly/Gen45:28); [MAT 17:20](https://ref.ly/Matt17:20); [LUK 20:6](https://ref.ly/Luke20:6) parallels [MAT 21:26](https://ref.ly/Matt21:26), [MRK 11:32](https://ref.ly/Mark11:32) *The people were convinced that John was a prophet*; [LUK 16:31](https://ref.ly/Luke16:31)ACT [17:4](https://ref.ly/Luke17:4), [ACT 19:26](https://ref.ly/Acts19:26), [ACT 28:24](https://ref.ly/Acts28:24)[ACT 26:9](https://ref.ly/Acts26:9), [ACT 26:26](https://ref.ly/Acts26:26); [ROM 2:19](https://ref.ly/Rom2:19), [ROM 4:21](https://ref.ly/Rom4:21), [ROM 8:38–8:39](https://ref.ly/Rom8:38-Rom8:39) *Paul's conviction that it is impossible to be separated from God's love*; [ROM 14:14](https://ref.ly/Rom14:14) *Paul's personal convictions about food regulations*; [ROM 15:14](https://ref.ly/Rom15:14); [2CO 5:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:14); [PHP 1:25](https://ref.ly/Phil1:25); [1TH 1:5](https://ref.ly/1Thess1:5); [2TI 1:5](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:5) *Paul is convinced by Timothy's faith*; [2TI 1:12](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:12), [2TI 3:14](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:14)

----------------------------------------------------

### Examples of conviction not resulting in repentance

## 6634: deliverance (id: 6634)

God frequently rescues people from danger, suffering and sin, often through human agency.

The source of deliverance
-------------------------

### Deliverance comes from God

**[PSA 3:8](https://ref.ly/Ps3:8)** *See also* [EXO 3:7–3:8](https://ref.ly/Exod3:7-Exod3:8); [PSA 18:2](https://ref.ly/Ps18:2); [DAN 3:16–3:17](https://ref.ly/Dan3:16-Dan3:17); [JON 2:9](https://ref.ly/Jonah2:9)

### There is no deliverance by other gods

[2KI 18:33](https://ref.ly/2Kgs18:33) parallel [ISA 36:18](https://ref.ly/Isa36:18)

### There is no escape from God

[ISA 43:13](https://ref.ly/Isa43:13)

### Deliverance may be declined

[MAT 26:53–26:54](https://ref.ly/Matt26:53-Matt26:54); ; [JHN 18:36](https://ref.ly/John18:36); ; [HEB 11:35](https://ref.ly/Heb11:35)

Different kinds of deliverance
------------------------------

### From danger

**[1SA 17:37](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:37)** *See also* [LUK 8:23–8:24](https://ref.ly/Luke8:23-Luke8:24); [2CO 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:9-2Cor1:10); [2TI 4:17](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:17)

### From illness

## 6636: drawing near to God (id: 6636)

Under the old covenant, coming near to God was closely linked with the sacrificial system, but under the new covenant Jesus Christ's sacrifice has given believers free access into God's presence.

Drawing near to God under the old covenant
------------------------------------------

### Access to God was restricted

**[EXO 24:1–24:2](https://ref.ly/Exod24:1-Exod24:2)** *See also* [EXO 19:20–19:24](https://ref.ly/Exod19:20-Exod19:24), [EXO 20:18–20:19](https://ref.ly/Exod20:18-Exod20:19); [LEV 21:21](https://ref.ly/Lev21:21); [DEU 5:22–5:27](https://ref.ly/Deut5:22-Deut5:27); [PSA 65:4](https://ref.ly/Ps65:4)

### Priests drew near to God in order to minister to him

**[EZK 44:15](https://ref.ly/Ezek44:15)** *See also* [LEV 10:1–10:3](https://ref.ly/Lev10:1-Lev10:3); [EZK 40:46](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:46), [EZK 42:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:13), [EZK 43:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek43:19), [EZK 45:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:4)

### The people drew near to God to offer worship

**[LEV 15:13–15:15](https://ref.ly/Lev15:13-Lev15:15)** *See also* [LEV 9:1–9:5](https://ref.ly/Lev9:1-Lev9:5); [PSA 96:8](https://ref.ly/Ps96:8), [PSA 100:2–100:4](https://ref.ly/Ps100:2-Ps100:4); [MIC 6:6–6:8](https://ref.ly/Mic6:6-Mic6:8)

Drawing near to God under the new covenant
------------------------------------------

**[HEB 10:19–10:22](https://ref.ly/Heb10:19-Heb10:22)** *See also* [1CO 8:8](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:8); [HEB 7:11–7:19](https://ref.ly/Heb7:11-Heb7:19), [HEB 10:1–10:10](https://ref.ly/Heb10:1-Heb10:10)

God prompts his people to draw near to him
------------------------------------------

**[ISA 55:1–55:3](https://ref.ly/Isa55:1-Isa55:3)** *See also* [ISA 55:6–55:7](https://ref.ly/Isa55:6-Isa55:7); [JER 3:21–4:2](https://ref.ly/Jer3:21-Jer4:2)

Some refuse to draw near to God
-------------------------------

**[ZEP 3:2](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:2)** *See also* [JER 2:30–2:31](https://ref.ly/Jer2:30-Jer2:31)

-------------------------------------------

### Israel

## 6638: election (id: 6638)

Scripture affirms that God chooses a people as his own, not on account of their numerical strength or moral merits, but on account of his love for them. Election is on the basis of divine grace, not human merit.

* **Associated Articles:** 6639: election, to salvation (ID: `6639@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6640: election, privileges of (ID: `6640@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6641: election, responsibilities of (ID: `6641@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6639: election, to salvation (id: 6639)

God chooses to bring individuals to salvation through faith in Jesus Christ.

Election is part of God's eternal decree
----------------------------------------

### Election is from eternity

**[EPH 1:4](https://ref.ly/Eph1:4)** *See also* [2TH 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:13); [2TI 1:9](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:9)

### Election is God's sovereign prerogative

**[ROM 9:15–9:24](https://ref.ly/Rom9:15-Rom9:24), [ROM 11:1–11:6](https://ref.ly/Rom11:1-Rom11:6)** *See also* [EXO 33:19](https://ref.ly/Exod33:19); [ISA 65:1](https://ref.ly/Isa65:1); [JER 18:1–18:12](https://ref.ly/Jer18:1-Jer18:12); [JHN 15:16](https://ref.ly/John15:16), [JHN 17:6](https://ref.ly/John17:6); [ROM 9:10–9:13](https://ref.ly/Rom9:10-Rom9:13); [EPH 2:10](https://ref.ly/Eph2:10)

### God's election places individuals within the covenant of grace

**[NEH 9:7–9:8](https://ref.ly/Neh9:7-Neh9:8)** *See also* [GEN 15:7–15:8](https://ref.ly/Gen15:7-Gen15:8), [GEN 15:18–15:21](https://ref.ly/Gen15:18-Gen15:21), [GEN 18:19](https://ref.ly/Gen18:19); [GAL 3:29](https://ref.ly/Gal3:29)

### Election is not on the basis of merit

**[1CO 1:26–1:31](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:26-1Cor1:31)** *See also* [DEU 7:7–7:8](https://ref.ly/Deut7:7-Deut7:8), [DEU 9:4–9:6](https://ref.ly/Deut9:4-Deut9:6); [JAS 2:5](https://ref.ly/Jas2:5)

God's election of his people is the foundation of his saving action
-------------------------------------------------------------------

### Election does not suspend God's use of the means of salvation

**[2TH 2:13–2:14](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:13-2Thess2:14)** *See also* [MAT 1:21](https://ref.ly/Matt1:21); [EPH 2:8–2:10](https://ref.ly/Eph2:8-Eph2:10); [JAS 1:18](https://ref.ly/Jas1:18); [1PE 1:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:2)

**[MAT 22:14](https://ref.ly/Matt22:14)** *See also* [ROM 8:29–8:30](https://ref.ly/Rom8:29-Rom8:30)

-------------------------------

**[ROM 11:28–11:36](https://ref.ly/Rom11:28-Rom11:36)**; **[EPH 1:3–1:14](https://ref.ly/Eph1:3-Eph1:14)** *See also* [1TH 1:2–1:4](https://ref.ly/1Thess1:2-1Thess1:4)

-----------------------------------------------------

## 6640: election, privileges of (id: 6640)

God chose a people to enjoy a unique relationship with him which entailed the privilege of belonging to him, sharing in all his inheritance, serving him, praising him and proclaiming him.

God elected Israel out of all the nations of the world
------------------------------------------------------

**[DEU 7:6](https://ref.ly/Deut7:6)** *See also* [DEU 14:1–14:2](https://ref.ly/Deut14:1-Deut14:2); [1KI 3:8](https://ref.ly/1Kgs3:8); [1CH 16:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:13); [PSA 105:6](https://ref.ly/Ps105:6), [PSA 105:43](https://ref.ly/Ps105:43), [PSA 135:4](https://ref.ly/Ps135:4); [ISA 41:8–41:9](https://ref.ly/Isa41:8-Isa41:9); [EZK 20:5–20:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:5-Ezek20:6)

### The election of the nation is anticipated in the election of the patriarchs

**[DEU 4:37–4:38](https://ref.ly/Deut4:37-Deut4:38)** *See also* [DEU 10:15](https://ref.ly/Deut10:15); [ACT 13:17–13:19](https://ref.ly/Acts13:17-Acts13:19)

Election was not based on merit
-------------------------------

**[DEU 7:7–7:8](https://ref.ly/Deut7:7-Deut7:8)** *See also* [DEU 9:4–9:6](https://ref.ly/Deut9:4-Deut9:6); [EZK 16:1–16:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:1-Ezek16:14)

God conferred privileges on the people he elected
-------------------------------------------------

### Election meant that God dwelled in their midst

**[2CH 6:6](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:6)** *See also* [1KI 14:21](https://ref.ly/1Kgs14:21) parallel [2CH 12:13](https://ref.ly/2Chr12:13); [2KI 21:7](https://ref.ly/2Kgs21:7) parallel [2CH 33:7](https://ref.ly/2Chr33:7); [2CH 6:34–6:35](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:34-2Chr6:35), [2CH 7:12](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:12), [2CH 7:16](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:16); [NEH 1:9](https://ref.ly/Neh1:9); [PSA 132:13](https://ref.ly/Ps132:13)

### Election meant that God showed divine favour

**[PSA 33:12](https://ref.ly/Ps33:12)** *See also* [PSA 65:4](https://ref.ly/Ps65:4), [PSA 106:4–106:5](https://ref.ly/Ps106:4-Ps106:5); [ISA 14:1](https://ref.ly/Isa14:1), [ISA 43:1](https://ref.ly/Isa43:1), [ISA 43:20](https://ref.ly/Isa43:20), [ISA 44:1–44:5](https://ref.ly/Isa44:1-Isa44:5), [ISA 45:4](https://ref.ly/Isa45:4); [ZEC 1:17](https://ref.ly/Zech1:17)

---------------------------------------------------

**[AMO 3:2](https://ref.ly/Amos3:2)** *See also* [2KI 23:26](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:26)

God's choice of Israel does not automatically imply election to salvation
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

## 6641: election, responsibilities of (id: 6641)

God's election lays responsibilities upon those who have been chosen. Election to salvation has the natural consequence of election to service.

Election to leadership
----------------------

## 6644: eternal life (id: 6644)

The state of being in a permanent living relationship with God, through Jesus Christ, begun in this life and consummated at the resurrection of believers.

* **Associated Articles:** 6645: eternal life, nature of (ID: `6645@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6646: eternal life, gift of (ID: `6646@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6647: eternal life, experience of (ID: `6647@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6645: eternal life, nature of (id: 6645)

Triumph over death and infinitely extended life. It also means a unique quality of life, knowing God in this life and sharing the life of Christ. Its source is God himself.

Eternal life is knowing God and enjoying his eternal blessings
--------------------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 17:3](https://ref.ly/John17:3)**; **[PSA 16:11](https://ref.ly/Ps16:11)** *See also* [PSA 21:4–21:6](https://ref.ly/Ps21:4-Ps21:6); [EPH 1:3–1:14](https://ref.ly/Eph1:3-Eph1:14)

### Eternal glory is the believer's inheritance

**[2CO 4:17](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:17)** *See also* [DAN 12:3](https://ref.ly/Dan12:3); [2TI 2:10](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:10); [1PE 5:4](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:4), [1PE 5:10](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:10)

### Contrasted with eternal judgment and rejection

**[MAT 25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:46)** *Interpreters differ over whether “eternal punishment” implies an experience that continues for ever, or annihilation which is eternal in the sense of being irreversible.* *See also* [DAN 12:2](https://ref.ly/Dan12:2); [MAT 25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:46); [JHN 3:16](https://ref.ly/John3:16); [2TH 1:8–1:9](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:8-2Thess1:9)

### The work of helping others come to eternal life

[JHN 4:35–4:36](https://ref.ly/John4:35-John4:36)

----------------------------

## 6646: eternal life, gift of (id: 6646)

Eternal life cannot be earned or merited but must be received as a gift from God.

Fruitless attempts to earn eternal life
---------------------------------------

**[JHN 5:39–5:40](https://ref.ly/John5:39-John5:40)** *It is possible to study the mere letter of Scripture while ignoring coming to its focus, Jesus Christ*; **[GAL 3:11–3:12](https://ref.ly/Gal3:11-Gal3:12)** *See also* [ROM 3:20](https://ref.ly/Rom3:20), [ROM 3:28](https://ref.ly/Rom3:28)

Jesus Christ is the source of eternal life
------------------------------------------

----------------------

## 6647: eternal life, experience of (id: 6647)

Eternal life is a present possession, to to be experienced here and now, but it also offers rich and joyful future prospects.

## 6648: expiation (id: 6648)

The removal of the guilt of sin in God's sight by the offering of a vicarious sacrifice which, in its death, bears the sin of the individual or nation concerned.

Expiation is necessary because sin is punishable by God
-------------------------------------------------------

**[EXO 32:30](https://ref.ly/Exod32:30)** *See also* [NUM 16:46–16:48](https://ref.ly/Num16:46-Num16:48); [DEU 21:8](https://ref.ly/Deut21:8); [PSA 79:8–79:9](https://ref.ly/Ps79:8-Ps79:9)

Expiation and the sacrificial system
------------------------------------

### Unintentional sins expiated by the sin offering

[LEV 4:1–5:6](https://ref.ly/Lev4:1-Lev5:6); ; [NUM 15:22–15:29](https://ref.ly/Num15:22-Num15:29)

### Unintentional sins requiring restitution expiated by the guilt offering

[LEV 5:14–6:7](https://ref.ly/Lev5:14-Lev6:7), [LEV 19:20–19:22](https://ref.ly/Lev19:20-Lev19:22)

### The nation's sins expiated on the annual Day of Atonement

**[EXO 30:10](https://ref.ly/Exod30:10)** *See also* [LEV 16:3–16:34](https://ref.ly/Lev16:3-Lev16:34); [HEB 9:7](https://ref.ly/Heb9:7)

### Blood as a symbol of substitutionary sacrifice

**[LEV 17:11](https://ref.ly/Lev17:11)** *See also* [EZK 45:19–45:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:19-Ezek45:20); [HEB 9:22](https://ref.ly/Heb9:22), [HEB 13:11](https://ref.ly/Heb13:11)

### The rite of expiation administered by the priests

**[LEV 9:7](https://ref.ly/Lev9:7)** *See also* [LEV 7:7](https://ref.ly/Lev7:7), [LEV 9:15](https://ref.ly/Lev9:15), [LEV 10:17–10:18](https://ref.ly/Lev10:17-Lev10:18); [NUM 6:11](https://ref.ly/Num6:11)

**[LEV 12:7–12:8](https://ref.ly/Lev12:7-Lev12:8)** *See also* [LEV 5:7–5:13](https://ref.ly/Lev5:7-Lev5:13), [LEV 14:21–14:32](https://ref.ly/Lev14:21-Lev14:32)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

### Sin offerings for occasions of dedication

**[EXO 29:31–29:33](https://ref.ly/Exod29:31-Exod29:33)** *See also* [LEV 8:14–8:15](https://ref.ly/Lev8:14-Lev8:15); [NUM 8:12](https://ref.ly/Num8:12); [2CH 29:21–29:24](https://ref.ly/2Chr29:21-2Chr29:24); [EZR 6:17](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:17)

## 6650: finding (id: 6650)

Discovering something or someone that is being looked for. The whole of Scripture points to God seeking out lost human beings and finding them. The delight of people at finding things (such as lost coins or wayward sons) is seen as a parable of the joy of God over repentant sinners.

Finding by searching
--------------------

### People do not always find what they are searching for

**[PRO 20:6](https://ref.ly/Prov20:6)** *See also* [GEN 27:36–27:40](https://ref.ly/Gen27:36-Gen27:40); [2SA 17:20](https://ref.ly/2Sam17:20)

### God is sometimes found without being sought

**[ROM 10:20](https://ref.ly/Rom10:20)** *See also* [ISA 65:1](https://ref.ly/Isa65:1); [ROM 9:30–9:31](https://ref.ly/Rom9:30-Rom9:31)

------------------------------

## 6652: forgiveness (id: 6652)

The freeing of a person from guilt and its consequences, including punishment; usually as an act of favour, compassion or love, with the aim of restoring a broken personal relationship. Forgiveness can involve both the remission of punishment and the cancellation of debts.

* **Associated Articles:** 6653: forgiveness, divine (ID: `6653@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6654: forgiveness, Jesus Christ's ministry of (ID: `6654@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6655: forgiveness, application of (ID: `6655@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6653: forgiveness, divine (id: 6653)

God forgives the sins of believers on the basis of the once for all sacrifice offered by Jesus Christ on the cross. Believers' sins are no longer held against them, on account of the atoning death of Jesus Christ.

God's nature and forgiveness
----------------------------

**[EXO 34:5–34:7](https://ref.ly/Exod34:5-Exod34:7)** *See also* [NUM 14:17–14:20](https://ref.ly/Num14:17-Num14:20); [NEH 9:16–9:17](https://ref.ly/Neh9:16-Neh9:17); [PSA 103:1–103:18](https://ref.ly/Ps103:1-Ps103:18); [ISA 43:25](https://ref.ly/Isa43:25); [MIC 7:18–7:20](https://ref.ly/Mic7:18-Mic7:20); [1JN 1:8–1:9](https://ref.ly/1John1:8-1John1:9)

God's promise of forgiveness
----------------------------

**[JER 31:31–31:34](https://ref.ly/Jer31:31-Jer31:34)** *See also* [2CH 7:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:14); [ISA 55:6–55:7](https://ref.ly/Isa55:6-Isa55:7); [HEB 8:8–8:12](https://ref.ly/Heb8:8-Heb8:12)

People's need of forgiveness
----------------------------

**[1JN 1:8–1:10](https://ref.ly/1John1:8-1John1:10)** *See also* [PSA 51:1–51:5](https://ref.ly/Ps51:1-Ps51:5); [ISA 6:1–6:5](https://ref.ly/Isa6:1-Isa6:5); [ROM 3:9](https://ref.ly/Rom3:9), [ROM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23)

## 6654: forgiveness, Jesus Christ's ministry of (id: 6654)

A central feature of Jesus Christ's ministry was his declaration that believers' sins were forgiven through their faith in him.

Jesus Christ's ministry of forgiveness was foretold
---------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/Matt1:20-Matt1:21)**; **[JHN 1:29](https://ref.ly/John1:29)**

--------------------------------------

Jesus Christ has authority on account of his divinity to forgive sins
---------------------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 9:1–9:8](https://ref.ly/Matt9:1-Matt9:8)** parallels [MRK 2:1–2:12](https://ref.ly/Mark2:1-Mark2:12), [LUK 5:17–5:26](https://ref.ly/Luke5:17-Luke5:26) *Jesus Christ's authority to forgive is authenticated by his healing of the paralytic.*

----------------------------------------------------------

**[MRK 2:5–2:7](https://ref.ly/Mark2:5-Mark2:7)** parallels [MAT 9:2–9:3](https://ref.ly/Matt9:2-Matt9:3), [LUK 5:20–5:21](https://ref.ly/Luke5:20-Luke5:21)

## 6655: forgiveness, application of (id: 6655)

## 6658: freedom (id: 6658)

The state of liberty that results from not being oppressed or in bondage. Scripture stresses that human beings lack freedom on account of sin, but that faith in Jesus Christ brings freedom from the power of sin and the law.

* **Associated Articles:** 6659: freedom, acts of in OT (ID: `6659@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6660: freedom, through Jesus Christ (ID: `6660@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6661: freedom, and the law (ID: `6661@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6662: freedom, abuse of Christian (ID: `6662@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6663: freedom, of the will (ID: `6663@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6659: freedom, acts of in OT (id: 6659)

The OT provides many examples of God delivering his people from bondage, of which the greatest is the exodus. These acts of deliverance foreshadow and prepare the way for the redeeming work of God through Jesus Christ, revealed in the NT.

God's people regain their freedom
---------------------------------

### The exodus from Egypt as an act of deliverance

**[EXO 20:2](https://ref.ly/Exod20:2)** *See also* [EXO 12:42](https://ref.ly/Exod12:42), [EXO 16:6](https://ref.ly/Exod16:6), [EXO 16:32](https://ref.ly/Exod16:32) *The people of Israel were frequently reminded that God had delivered them from Egypt*; [JOS 24:6](https://ref.ly/Josh24:6); [JDG 6:8](https://ref.ly/Judg6:8); [2SA 7:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:6); [1KI 8:16](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:16); [2CH 7:22](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:22); [PSA 80:8](https://ref.ly/Ps80:8); [JER 2:6](https://ref.ly/Jer2:6), [JER 11:4](https://ref.ly/Jer11:4); [HOS 12:9](https://ref.ly/Hos12:9); [AMO 2:10](https://ref.ly/Amos2:10); [MIC 6:4](https://ref.ly/Mic6:4); [HAG 2:5](https://ref.ly/Hag2:5); [HEB 8:9](https://ref.ly/Heb8:9); [JUD 1:5](https://ref.ly/Jude1:5)

### The return from exile in Babylon as an act of deliverance

**[ISA 35:3–35:10](https://ref.ly/Isa35:3-Isa35:10)** *See also* [ISA 43:14–45:5](https://ref.ly/Isa43:14-Isa45:5), [ISA 45:14–45:17](https://ref.ly/Isa45:14-Isa45:17), [ISA 49:8–49:26](https://ref.ly/Isa49:8-Isa49:26), [ISA 51:22–52:12](https://ref.ly/Isa51:22-Isa52:12), [ISA 54:1–54:17](https://ref.ly/Isa54:1-Isa54:17), [ISA 61:1–62:12](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1-Isa62:12); [EZK 36:24–36:36](https://ref.ly/Ezek36:24-Ezek36:36), [EZK 37:15–37:28](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:15-Ezek37:28)

----------------------------------------------------------------

[DEU 15:12–15:15](https://ref.ly/Deut15:12-Deut15:15) *the sabbath year: all servants to be freed after six years*; [LEV 25:10](https://ref.ly/Lev25:10), [LEV 25:39–25:43](https://ref.ly/Lev25:39-Lev25:43)

[EXO 3:8](https://ref.ly/Exod3:8) *The inheritance is the promised land of Canaan, which foreshadows the gospel inheritance of eternal life in the kingdom of God*; ; [NUM 14:7–14:8](https://ref.ly/Num14:7-Num14:8); ; [DEU 8:7–8:9](https://ref.ly/Deut8:7-Deut8:9); ; [EZK 20:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:6)

## 6660: freedom, through Jesus Christ (id: 6660)

Jesus Christ, the promised deliverer, sets his people free from the present effects of sin and from the power of sin and will finally deliver them completely from its presence.

The OT points ahead to a new and greater freedom and to a new deliverer
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

### The OT predicts Jesus Christ as the deliverer

**[ISA 61:1](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1)** *See also* [ISA 42:6–42:7](https://ref.ly/Isa42:6-Isa42:7)

### The redemption of the exodus foreshadows the redemption achieved by Jesus Christ

**[COL 1:13–1:14](https://ref.ly/Col1:13-Col1:14)** *See also* [1CO 10:1–10:4](https://ref.ly/1Cor10:1-1Cor10:4)

### Jesus Christ fulfils the OT predictions of him as deliverer

**[LUK 4:18–4:19](https://ref.ly/Luke4:18-Luke4:19)** *See also* [ROM 11:26](https://ref.ly/Rom11:26); [ISA 59:20](https://ref.ly/Isa59:20)

The freedom that comes through Jesus Christ
-------------------------------------------

**[JHN 8:32–8:36](https://ref.ly/John8:32-John8:36)** *See also* [MAT 1:21](https://ref.ly/Matt1:21)

### Jesus Christ sets his people free from the penalty of sin

**[1TH 1:10](https://ref.ly/1Thess1:10)** *See also* [JHN 3:36](https://ref.ly/John3:36); [ROM 8:1–8:2](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1-Rom8:2); [HEB 9:15](https://ref.ly/Heb9:15); [REV 1:5](https://ref.ly/Rev1:5)

### Jesus Christ sets his people free from the spiritual death that accompanies sin

**[ROM 6:1–6:7](https://ref.ly/Rom6:1-Rom6:7)** *See also* [EPH 2:1–2:5](https://ref.ly/Eph2:1-Eph2:5); [HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14)

### Jesus Christ sets his people free from the fear of death

**[HEB 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14-Heb2:15)**

### Jesus Christ will finally set his people free from death itself

**[1CO 15:22–15:23](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:22-1Cor15:23)** *See also* [ROM 5:12–5:17](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12-Rom5:17), [ROM 7:24](https://ref.ly/Rom7:24)

### Jesus Christ sets his people free from the power of sin

**[ROM 6:11–6:14](https://ref.ly/Rom6:11-Rom6:14)** *See also* [ROM 6:22–6:23](https://ref.ly/Rom6:22-Rom6:23)

### Jesus Christ sets his people free from the pollution of sin

## 6661: freedom, and the law (id: 6661)

Jesus Christ sets his people free from the condemnation and oppression of the law. Through the Holy Spirit, believers are able to fulfil the law obediently according to God's intentions.

Jesus Christ sets believers free from the law
---------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's life of perfect obedience to the law was the fulfilment of it

**[MAT 5:17](https://ref.ly/Matt5:17)** *See also* [GAL 4:4–4:5](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4-Gal4:5); [1PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22)

### Jesus Christ's death fulfils the demands of the law

**[2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21)** *See also* [HEB 7:27](https://ref.ly/Heb7:27), [HEB 9:11](https://ref.ly/Heb9:11), [HEB 9:26–9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:26-Heb9:28), [HEB 10:11–10:14](https://ref.ly/Heb10:11-Heb10:14); [1PE 2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:24), [1PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:18)

### On account of Jesus Christ's death, believers can be righteous independently of the law

**[ROM 3:21–3:26](https://ref.ly/Rom3:21-Rom3:26)** *See also* [JHN 1:17](https://ref.ly/John1:17); [ROM 10:4](https://ref.ly/Rom10:4); [PHP 3:9](https://ref.ly/Phil3:9)

Believers are set free from the law's condemnation
--------------------------------------------------

**[GAL 3:21–3:25](https://ref.ly/Gal3:21-Gal3:25)** *See also* [ROM 6:1–6:14](https://ref.ly/Rom6:1-Rom6:14), [ROM 7:1–7:6](https://ref.ly/Rom7:1-Rom7:6); [GAL 3:13](https://ref.ly/Gal3:13), [GAL 4:5](https://ref.ly/Gal4:5), [GAL 4:21–4:31](https://ref.ly/Gal4:21-Gal4:31) *The lives of Abraham, Sarah, Hagar, Ishmael and Isaac are interpreted figuratively, to illustrate the believer's freedom from the law's condemnation*; [GAL 5:1](https://ref.ly/Gal5:1); [EPH 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Eph2:14-Eph2:15); [COL 2:13–2:14](https://ref.ly/Col2:13-Col2:14)

The freedom of believers rests on the power of the Holy Spirit
--------------------------------------------------------------

**[ROM 7:1–7:6](https://ref.ly/Rom7:1-Rom7:6)**; **[2CO 3:17–3:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:17-2Cor3:18)** *See also* [ROM 8:1–8:17](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1-Rom8:17); [GAL 5:16–5:18](https://ref.ly/Gal5:16-Gal5:18), [GAL 5:22–5:26](https://ref.ly/Gal5:22-Gal5:26)

## 6662: freedom, abuse of Christian (id: 6662)

Although Christians have been set free from condemnation by grace, they remain under an obligation to be obedient to God. Abuses of Christian freedom result from a failure to take responsibilities towards God seriously.

Christian freedom can be abused
-------------------------------

### Believers are freed from condemnation

**[ROM 8:1](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1)** *See also* [ISA 50:8–50:9](https://ref.ly/Isa50:8-Isa50:9); [ROM 8:33–8:39](https://ref.ly/Rom8:33-Rom8:39); [COL 1:22](https://ref.ly/Col1:22); [REV 1:5](https://ref.ly/Rev1:5)

### Sin need not enslave believers

**[JHN 8:34–8:36](https://ref.ly/John8:34-John8:36)** *See also* [ROM 6:16–6:18](https://ref.ly/Rom6:16-Rom6:18), [ROM 7:14–7:25](https://ref.ly/Rom7:14-Rom7:25); [1CO 7:22–7:23](https://ref.ly/1Cor7:22-1Cor7:23); [2PE 2:19](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:19)

### Believers must resist sin

**[ROM 6:12](https://ref.ly/Rom6:12), [ROM 6:14](https://ref.ly/Rom6:14)** *See also* [HEB 12:1–12:2](https://ref.ly/Heb12:1-Heb12:2); [1JN 5:16–5:18](https://ref.ly/1John5:16-1John5:18)

### The false idea that grace gives believers the freedom to sin

**[ROM 6:1–6:2](https://ref.ly/Rom6:1-Rom6:2), [ROM 6:15](https://ref.ly/Rom6:15)** *See also* [ROM 3:5–3:8](https://ref.ly/Rom3:5-Rom3:8); [1CO 10:23](https://ref.ly/1Cor10:23); [GAL 2:17–2:21](https://ref.ly/Gal2:17-Gal2:21)

The dangers of abusing Christian freedom
----------------------------------------

### Becoming a stumbling\-block to others

**[1CO 8:9–8:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:9-1Cor8:12)** *See also* [ROM 15:1–15:3](https://ref.ly/Rom15:1-Rom15:3)

### Indulging oneself

**[GAL 5:13](https://ref.ly/Gal5:13)** *See also* [ROM 14:1–14:18](https://ref.ly/Rom14:1-Rom14:18)

### Using freedom to cover up evil

**[1PE 2:16](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:16)**

Examples of abuse of Christian freedom
--------------------------------------

### Falling back into deliberate sin

*See also* [ROM 6:1–6:2](https://ref.ly/Rom6:1-Rom6:2); [HEB 12:1](https://ref.ly/Heb12:1); [1JN 3:6](https://ref.ly/1John3:6), [1JN 5:16–5:18](https://ref.ly/1John5:16-1John5:18)

## 6663: freedom, of the will (id: 6663)

The ability to make decisions without being coerced by external forces. Scripture stresses that people are confronted with free choices between good and evil and commands them to choose good. However, it also notes that limitations are placed upon human actions through the enslaving power of sin.

Freedom of the will
-------------------

### Freedom of the will to choose between good and evil

**[DEU 11:26–11:28](https://ref.ly/Deut11:26-Deut11:28)** *See also* [DEU 30:15–30:16](https://ref.ly/Deut30:15-Deut30:16), [DEU 30:19](https://ref.ly/Deut30:19); [JOS 24:15](https://ref.ly/Josh24:15); [1CH 28:9](https://ref.ly/1Chr28:9); [JER 26:3](https://ref.ly/Jer26:3); [EZK 18:21–18:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:21-Ezek18:23)

### Freedom of the will to seek and find God

**[ISA 55:6](https://ref.ly/Isa55:6)** *See also* [AMO 5:4](https://ref.ly/Amos5:4); [ACT 2:21](https://ref.ly/Acts2:21); [ROM 10:11](https://ref.ly/Rom10:11); [ISA 28:16](https://ref.ly/Isa28:16); [REV 22:17](https://ref.ly/Rev22:17)

The effect of sin upon freedom of the will
------------------------------------------

### Sin prevents human beings from breaking free from its bondage

**[ROM 7:14–7:20](https://ref.ly/Rom7:14-Rom7:20)** *See also* [ROM 6:16](https://ref.ly/Rom6:16), [ROM 6:22](https://ref.ly/Rom6:22), [ROM 7:25](https://ref.ly/Rom7:25) *Paul stresses that it is only through Jesus Christ that human beings can be freed from servitude to sin.*

### Sin hardens human hearts

**[HEB 3:13](https://ref.ly/Heb3:13)** *See also* [DAN 5:20](https://ref.ly/Dan5:20); [ROM 1:21](https://ref.ly/Rom1:21); [EPH 4:17–4:19](https://ref.ly/Eph4:17-Eph4:19)

### God hardens human hearts

**[EXO 9:12](https://ref.ly/Exod9:12)** *See also* [EXO 4:21](https://ref.ly/Exod4:21), [EXO 10:20](https://ref.ly/Exod10:20), [EXO 14:4](https://ref.ly/Exod14:4), [EXO 14:8](https://ref.ly/Exod14:8); [DEU 2:30](https://ref.ly/Deut2:30); [JOS 11:19–11:20](https://ref.ly/Josh11:19-Josh11:20); [ROM 1:22–1:24](https://ref.ly/Rom1:22-Rom1:24), [ROM 9:17–9:18](https://ref.ly/Rom9:17-Rom9:18)

### Human beings harden their own hearts

## 6666: grace (id: 6666)

The unmerited favour of God, made known through Jesus Christ, and expressed supremely in the redemption and full forgiveness of sinners through faith in Jesus Christ.

* **Associated Articles:** 6667: grace, in OT (ID: `6667@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6668: grace, and Jesus Christ (ID: `6668@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6669: grace, and salvation (ID: `6669@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6670: grace, and Holy Spirit (ID: `6670@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6671: grace, and Christian life (ID: `6671@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6672: grace, in human relationships (ID: `6672@DictionaryBibleThemes`)

## 6671: grace, and Christian life (id: 6671)

The Christian life, from its beginning to its end, is totally dependent upon the grace of God.

God's grace compensates for human weaknesses
--------------------------------------------

**[2CO 12:8–12:9](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:8-2Cor12:9)**; **[1PE 5:10](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:10)** *See also* [1CO 2:1–2:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:1-1Cor2:5); [2CO 9:8](https://ref.ly/2Cor9:8); [HEB 2:14](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14), [HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15), [HEB 5:2](https://ref.ly/Heb5:2); [JAS 4:6](https://ref.ly/Jas4:6); [2PE 3:17–3:18](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:17-2Pet3:18)

## 6674: imputation (id: 6674)

The crediting by God to believers with righteousness on account of Jesus Christ. Paul argues that Abraham did nothing which earned him the status of being righteous in the sight of God. Rather, Abraham believed the promise of God, and for that reason was granted the status of being righteous before God. Likewise, all who trust in Jesus Christ have righteousness imputed to them\-\-that is, reckoned as if it was theirs. Imputation should not be confused with impartation. Believers are not made right ethically (impartation), but put right relationally (imputation). What God changes is not the character of believers but their legal standing before him. From this new position, believers are called to co\-operate with the Holy Spirit in sanctification so that their character increasingly reflects their new standing.

Righteousness imputed through faith not works
---------------------------------------------

### The example of Abraham

**[ROM 4:1–4:3](https://ref.ly/Rom4:1-Rom4:3)** *See also* [GEN 15:1–15:6](https://ref.ly/Gen15:1-Gen15:6); [ROM 4:9–4:22](https://ref.ly/Rom4:9-Rom4:22); [GAL 3:6–3:9](https://ref.ly/Gal3:6-Gal3:9)

### The testimony of David

**[ROM 4:6–4:8](https://ref.ly/Rom4:6-Rom4:8)** *See also* [PSA 32:1–32:2](https://ref.ly/Ps32:1-Ps32:2)

### The principle holds true for everyone

**[ROM 4:4–4:5](https://ref.ly/Rom4:4-Rom4:5), [ROM 4:23–4:24](https://ref.ly/Rom4:23-Rom4:24)** *See also* [1CO 1:30](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:30); [2CO 5:19](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:19); [GAL 3:7–3:9](https://ref.ly/Gal3:7-Gal3:9); [PHP 3:9](https://ref.ly/Phil3:9)

## 6676: justification (id: 6676)

The acquittal, or declaration of being righteous, before God as judge. It is a central aspect of Paul's understanding of what God achieved for believers through the death and resurrection of Jesus Christ.

* **Associated Articles:** 6677: justification, necessity of (ID: `6677@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6678: justification, and Jesus Christ's work (ID: `6678@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6679: justification, results of (ID: `6679@DictionaryBibleThemes`)

## 6679: justification, results of (id: 6679)

Justification brings a changed relationship with God and a future hope. It will also bring a change in behaviour.

The results of justification
----------------------------

### Peace with God, access to his presence and the hope of his glory

**[ROM 8:31–8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:31-Rom8:34)** *See also* [ROM 8:1–8:4](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1-Rom8:4); [GAL 3:13–3:14](https://ref.ly/Gal3:13-Gal3:14)

### Freedom from domination by sin

**[ROM 6:14](https://ref.ly/Rom6:14), [ROM 6:17–6:18](https://ref.ly/Rom6:17-Rom6:18)**

### Adoption into God's family

*See also* [ROM 8:15–8:17](https://ref.ly/Rom8:15-Rom8:17); [GAL 4:6–4:7](https://ref.ly/Gal4:6-Gal4:7)

### Righteousness in the sight of God

## 6682: mediation (id: 6682)

The achieving of fellowship and reconciliation between separated parties. Scripture declares that Jesus Christ is the only true mediator between God and humanity.

Jesus Christ is the only mediator between God and humanity
----------------------------------------------------------

## 6684: mediator (id: 6684)

An intermediary who intervenes betwen two separated or alienated parties, with the aim of achieving reconciliation and fellowship. Scripture declares that Jesus Christ is the only true mediator between God and humanity.

A person who brings together those who are separated from each other

## 6686: mercy (id: 6686)

A quality of compassion, especially as expressed in God's forgiveness of human sin. Scripture stresses God's forbearance towards sinners. In his mercy, God shields sinners from what they deserve and gives gifts that they do not deserve.

* **Associated Articles:** 6687: mercy, nature of God's (ID: `6687@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6688: mercy, demonstration of God's (ID: `6688@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6689: mercy, of Jesus Christ (ID: `6689@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6690: mercy, response to God's (ID: `6690@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6691: mercy, human (ID: `6691@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6687: mercy, nature of God's (id: 6687)

---------------

## 6690: mercy, response to God's (id: 6690)

God's merciful dealings with believers should move them to show similar acts of mercy to others, as well as to rejoice in his graciousness and proclaim it to others.

The proper response to God's mercy
----------------------------------

### A self\-giving faith

**[ROM 12:1](https://ref.ly/Rom12:1)** *See also* [PSA 13:5](https://ref.ly/Ps13:5), [PSA 52:8](https://ref.ly/Ps52:8); [EPH 2:8](https://ref.ly/Eph2:8); [1TI 1:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:16); [HEB 4:16](https://ref.ly/Heb4:16); [1PE 5:5](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:5); [JAS 4:6](https://ref.ly/Jas4:6)

**[MAT 6:12](https://ref.ly/Matt6:12)** parallel [LUK 11:4](https://ref.ly/Luke11:4) *See also* [MAT 6:14](https://ref.ly/Matt6:14), [MAT 18:21–18:35](https://ref.ly/Matt18:21-Matt18:35); [LUK 6:37](https://ref.ly/Luke6:37), [LUK 17:3–17:4](https://ref.ly/Luke17:3-Luke17:4); [2CO 2:7](https://ref.ly/2Cor2:7); [EPH 4:32](https://ref.ly/Eph4:32); [COL 3:13](https://ref.ly/Col3:13)

## 6691: mercy, human (id: 6691)

Believers are urged to show the same qualities of mercy and compassion towards one another as God demonstrates to them. A lack of mercy is regarded as characteristic of godless people.

The need for human mercy
------------------------

**[PRO 18:23](https://ref.ly/Prov18:23)** *See also* [DEU 28:49–28:50](https://ref.ly/Deut28:49-Deut28:50); [2SA 12:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:6); [1KI 3:26](https://ref.ly/1Kgs3:26); [JOB 19:21](https://ref.ly/Job19:21); [PRO 21:10](https://ref.ly/Prov21:10); [ISA 47:6](https://ref.ly/Isa47:6), [ISA 49:15](https://ref.ly/Isa49:15); [ZEC 7:9–7:11](https://ref.ly/Zech7:9-Zech7:11)

---------------------------------------

## 6694: mystery (id: 6694)

Normally, God's plan of salvation which, though once unknown to human beings, is now revealed by God.

God's character and purpose cannot be discerned by human reason
---------------------------------------------------------------

**[JOB 11:7](https://ref.ly/Job11:7)** *See also* [JOB 38:1–42:6](https://ref.ly/Job38:1-Job42:6)

God reveals his plans through dreams, interpreted by his servant
----------------------------------------------------------------

**[DAN 2:28](https://ref.ly/Dan2:28)** *Nebuchadnezzar's dreams require the interpretation that God discloses to Daniel before they can be understood as a revelation of divine purposes for Babylon and the surrounding nations.* *See also* [DAN 2:17–2:49](https://ref.ly/Dan2:17-Dan2:49), [DAN 4:9](https://ref.ly/Dan4:9)

### God's mysteries are revealed to a man inspired by his Spirit

**[DAN 4:18](https://ref.ly/Dan4:18)** *See also* [AMO 3:7](https://ref.ly/Amos3:7)

The mystery of God's kingdom
----------------------------

**[MAT 13:11](https://ref.ly/Matt13:11)** parallels [MRK 4:11](https://ref.ly/Mark4:11), [LUK 8:10](https://ref.ly/Luke8:10) *God's plan to establish his kingdom is revealed only to those chosen to receive it. To those “outside” it is hidden in parables.*

Mystery as God's plan of salvation
----------------------------------

### God's plan, now revealed, has been hidden for long ages

**[EPH 3:9](https://ref.ly/Eph3:9)** *The use of “mystery” in this sense is found particularly in Paul's letters.* *See also* [ROM 16:25](https://ref.ly/Rom16:25); [1CO 2:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:7); [COL 1:26](https://ref.ly/Col1:26)

### God's plan is fulfilled in Jesus Christ

**[EPH 1:9](https://ref.ly/Eph1:9)** *See also* [EPH 3:4](https://ref.ly/Eph3:4); [COL 2:2](https://ref.ly/Col2:2); [1TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:16) *The “mystery of godliness” is the revealed secret that produces godliness in people.*

### God's plan through Jesus Christ is for the salvation of Gentiles as well as Jews

**[EPH 3:6](https://ref.ly/Eph3:6)** *See also* [ROM 11:25](https://ref.ly/Rom11:25); [COL 1:27](https://ref.ly/Col1:27)

### Ultimately God's plan is for the transformation of the whole creation

**[EPH 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/Eph1:9-Eph1:10)** *See also* [1CO 15:51–15:53](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:51-1Cor15:53); [REV 10:7](https://ref.ly/Rev10:7), [REV 17:5–17:8](https://ref.ly/Rev17:5-Rev17:8)

### God's plan is revealed by his Spirit so that his servants may publicly proclaim it

**[EPH 3:8–3:9](https://ref.ly/Eph3:8-Eph3:9)** *See also* [EPH 3:4–3:6](https://ref.ly/Eph3:4-Eph3:6), [EPH 6:19](https://ref.ly/Eph6:19); [COL 1:25–1:27](https://ref.ly/Col1:25-Col1:27), [COL 4:3](https://ref.ly/Col4:3); [REV 10:7](https://ref.ly/Rev10:7)

### Mystery as other aspects of God's purposes, spiritually discerned

**[2TH 2:7](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:7)** *Paul's reference to “the secret power (literally “mystery”) of lawlessness” suggests that we know some things about evil only as God reveals them.* *See also* [1CO 13:2](https://ref.ly/1Cor13:2), [1CO 14:2](https://ref.ly/1Cor14:2)

### Mystery as an allegorical understanding of a biblical text, revealed to Paul by God

**[EPH 5:31–5:32](https://ref.ly/Eph5:31-Eph5:32)** *Paul sees [Ge 2:24](https://ref.ly/Gen2:24) as symbolising the unity between Jesus Christ and his church; the unity of husband and wife is a human reflection of that relationship.*

* **Associated Passages:** Job 11:7; Job 38:1-42:6; Daniel 2:28; Daniel 2:17-49; Daniel 4:9; Daniel 4:18; Amos 3:7; Matthew 13:11; Mark 4:11; Luke 8:10; Ephesians 3:9; Romans 16:25; 1 Corinthians 2:7; Colossians 1:26; Ephesians 1:9; Ephesians 3:4; Colossians 2:2; 1 Timothy 3:16; Ephesians 3:6; Romans 11:25; Colossians 1:27; Ephesians 1:9-10; 1 Corinthians 15:51-53; Revelation 10:7; Revelation 17:5-8; Ephesians 3:8-9; Ephesians 3:4-6; Ephesians 6:19; Colossians 1:25-27; Colossians 4:3; 2 Thessalonians 2:7; 1 Corinthians 13:2; 1 Corinthians 14:2; Ephesians 5:31-32; Genesis 2:24

## 6696: necessity (id: 6696)

That which makes certain actions or events occur. Scripture relates it to particular events which must happen to bring about God's plan of salvation and also to the behaviour that believers are to adopt as a result of their commitment to Jesus Christ.

The necessity of Jesus Christ's death and resurrection
------------------------------------------------------

**[LUK 24:25–24:27](https://ref.ly/Luke24:25-Luke24:27)** *See also* [MAT 16:21](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21) parallels [MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31), [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22); [LUK 17:25](https://ref.ly/Luke17:25), [LUK 24:44–24:47](https://ref.ly/Luke24:44-Luke24:47); [JHN 3:14–3:15](https://ref.ly/John3:14-John3:15), [JHN 20:9](https://ref.ly/John20:9)

-----------------------------------------

**[LUK 4:42–4:44](https://ref.ly/Luke4:42-Luke4:44)** *See also* [MAT 3:14–3:15](https://ref.ly/Matt3:14-Matt3:15); [LUK 2:49](https://ref.ly/Luke2:49), [LUK 13:31–13:33](https://ref.ly/Luke13:31-Luke13:33); [JHN 4:4](https://ref.ly/John4:4) *The necessity lay in Jesus Christ's mission not in geography*; [JHN 9:4](https://ref.ly/John9:4)

----------------------------------------------------

**[REV 1:1](https://ref.ly/Rev1:1)** *See also* [MRK 13:7–13:8](https://ref.ly/Mark13:7-Mark13:8) parallels [MAT 24:6–24:8](https://ref.ly/Matt24:6-Matt24:8), [LUK 21:9–21:11](https://ref.ly/Luke21:9-Luke21:11); [MRK 13:10](https://ref.ly/Mark13:10) parallel [MAT 24:14](https://ref.ly/Matt24:14); [1CO 15:50–15:55](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:50-1Cor15:55); [2CO 5:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:10); [REV 4:1](https://ref.ly/Rev4:1), [REV 20:1–20:3](https://ref.ly/Rev20:1-Rev20:3), [REV 22:6](https://ref.ly/Rev22:6)

## 6698: newness (id: 6698)

Through Jesus Christ, God has made possible a new relationship between himself and sinful humanity. This involves the renewal of human nature and eventually a renewal of creation itself.

The newness of the gospel
-------------------------

### The teaching of Jesus Christ was acclaimed as something new

**[MRK 1:27](https://ref.ly/Mark1:27)**

### The kingdom of God is like new cloth

**[LUK 5:36](https://ref.ly/Luke5:36)** parallels [MAT 9:16](https://ref.ly/Matt9:16), [MRK 2:21](https://ref.ly/Mark2:21)

### The kingdom of God is like new wine

**[LUK 5:37–5:38](https://ref.ly/Luke5:37-Luke5:38)** parallels [MAT 9:17](https://ref.ly/Matt9:17), [MRK 2:22](https://ref.ly/Mark2:22)

### A new covenant has been established between God and his people

**[JER 31:31](https://ref.ly/Jer31:31)**; **[HEB 9:15](https://ref.ly/Heb9:15)** *See also* [1CO 11:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:25); [2CO 3:6](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:6); [HEB 8:1–8:13](https://ref.ly/Heb8:1-Heb8:13), [HEB 10:20](https://ref.ly/Heb10:20), [HEB 12:24](https://ref.ly/Heb12:24)

The newness brought to believers through redemption
---------------------------------------------------

### Believers are called by a new name

**[ISA 62:2](https://ref.ly/Isa62:2)** *See also* [REV 2:17](https://ref.ly/Rev2:17)

### Believers are born anew

**[1PE 1:3](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:3)** *See also* [JHN 3:1–3:16](https://ref.ly/John3:1-John3:16)

### A new life is made possible for believers

**[ACT 5:20](https://ref.ly/Acts5:20)** *See also* [ROM 6:4](https://ref.ly/Rom6:4); [COL 3:10](https://ref.ly/Col3:10)

### Believers are a new creation

**[2CO 5:17](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:17)** *See also* [GAL 6:15](https://ref.ly/Gal6:15); [EPH 4:23–4:24](https://ref.ly/Eph4:23-Eph4:24)

**[JHN 13:34–13:35](https://ref.ly/John13:34-John13:35)** *See also* [1JN 2:7–2:8](https://ref.ly/1John2:7-1John2:8)

--------------------------------------------------------------

## 6700: peace (id: 6700)

The state of harmony that is available to believers through having a right relationship with God and others and is especially associated with the presence of the Holy Spirit.

* **Associated Articles:** 6701: peace, human search for (ID: `6701@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6702: peace, human destruction of (ID: `6702@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6703: peace, divine in OT (ID: `6703@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6704: peace, divine in NT (ID: `6704@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6705: peace, believers' experience of (ID: `6705@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6706: peace, and Holy Spirit (ID: `6706@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6701: peace, human search for (id: 6701)

Scripture teaches that peace is only found in God, but people try to find it elsewhere. A person's desire for peace varies according to his or her circumstances.

The places where people search for peace
----------------------------------------

### People search for peace in others

**[GEN 5:28–5:29](https://ref.ly/Gen5:28-Gen5:29)** *See also* [SNG 8:10](https://ref.ly/Song8:10)

### People search for peace in material possessions

**[ECC 4:8](https://ref.ly/Eccl4:8)** *See also* [JOB 21:7–21:13](https://ref.ly/Job21:7-Job21:13); [DAN 4:4](https://ref.ly/Dan4:4); [MAT 19:16–19:22](https://ref.ly/Matt19:16-Matt19:22); [LUK 12:16–12:19](https://ref.ly/Luke12:16-Luke12:19)

### People search for peace in God

**[PSA 4:8](https://ref.ly/Ps4:8)** *See also* [JOB 22:21](https://ref.ly/Job22:21); [PRO 19:23](https://ref.ly/Prov19:23); [ISA 26:3](https://ref.ly/Isa26:3); [LUK 7:37–7:50](https://ref.ly/Luke7:37-Luke7:50)

The dangers in searching for peace
----------------------------------

### It can lead to greed

**[ECC 4:6](https://ref.ly/Eccl4:6)** *See also* [MAT 23:25](https://ref.ly/Matt23:25)

### It can lead to suffering and bondage

[GEN 42:1–42:17](https://ref.ly/Gen42:1-Gen42:17); ; [JOS 9:3–9:27](https://ref.ly/Josh9:3-Josh9:27); ; [MRK 5:25–5:26](https://ref.ly/Mark5:25-Mark5:26)

### It can lead to destruction

**[1TH 5:3](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:3)** *See also* [2KI 20:12–20:19](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:12-2Kgs20:19); [LUK 16:19–16:26](https://ref.ly/Luke16:19-Luke16:26)

People's search for peace varies according to their circumstances
-----------------------------------------------------------------

### The desire can increase in times of suffering and difficulties

**[EXO 2:23](https://ref.ly/Exod2:23)** *See also* [JER 14:19](https://ref.ly/Jer14:19), [JER 47:2–47:6](https://ref.ly/Jer47:2-Jer47:6); [LAM 3:7–3:24](https://ref.ly/Lam3:7-Lam3:24); [EZK 7:23–7:27](https://ref.ly/Ezek7:23-Ezek7:27); [MRK 5:24–5:34](https://ref.ly/Mark5:24-Mark5:34) parallels [MAT 9:18–9:22](https://ref.ly/Matt9:18-Matt9:22), [LUK 8:42–8:48](https://ref.ly/Luke8:42-Luke8:48)

### The desire can diminish in times of comfort

**[EXO 8:12–8:15](https://ref.ly/Exod8:12-Exod8:15)** *See also* [JOB 12:5](https://ref.ly/Job12:5); [HOS 10:1](https://ref.ly/Hos10:1); [AMO 6:1](https://ref.ly/Amos6:1)

## 6702: peace, human destruction of (id: 6702)

Because of human sinfulness, God's provision of peace is always under threat. Scripture shows that this breaking of peace has implications for the whole of creation.

Causes of the destruction of peace
----------------------------------

### Sin and self\-centredness

**[ISA 57:21](https://ref.ly/Isa57:21)** *See also* [GEN 11:4–11:9](https://ref.ly/Gen11:4-Gen11:9); [ISA 59:7–59:8](https://ref.ly/Isa59:7-Isa59:8); [LUK 19:41–19:44](https://ref.ly/Luke19:41-Luke19:44)

**[ZEC 10:2](https://ref.ly/Zech10:2)** *See also* [EXO 32:7–32:10](https://ref.ly/Exod32:7-Exod32:10); [1TI 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:9-1Tim6:10)

## 6703: peace, divine in OT (id: 6703)

Providing peace for his creation is a characteristic of God. In the OT peace came through adherence to God's will as expressed in his spoken word, covenants and law. The Hebrew word “shalom” means “peace in all its fulness, in every aspect of life”.

Peace provided for God's people
-------------------------------

### Through obedience to God's spoken word

**[GEN 2:16–2:17](https://ref.ly/Gen2:16-Gen2:17)** *See also* [2KI 5:13–5:19](https://ref.ly/2Kgs5:13-2Kgs5:19); [JOB 22:21–22:22](https://ref.ly/Job22:21-Job22:22); [PSA 85:8](https://ref.ly/Ps85:8); [ISA 54:13](https://ref.ly/Isa54:13); [DAN 10:15–10:19](https://ref.ly/Dan10:15-Dan10:19)

**[DEU 29:9](https://ref.ly/Deut29:9)** *See also* [DEU 30:15–30:16](https://ref.ly/Deut30:15-Deut30:16); [MAL 2:1–2:6](https://ref.ly/Mal2:1-Mal2:6)

### Through obedience to God's laws

**[PSA 119:165](https://ref.ly/Ps119:165)** *See also* [LEV 26:3–26:12](https://ref.ly/Lev26:3-Lev26:12); [DEU 28:1–28:7](https://ref.ly/Deut28:1-Deut28:7); [2CH 14:2–14:7](https://ref.ly/2Chr14:2-2Chr14:7); [PSA 37:34–37:38](https://ref.ly/Ps37:34-Ps37:38); [PRO 3:13–3:17](https://ref.ly/Prov3:13-Prov3:17); [ISA 48:18](https://ref.ly/Isa48:18)

## 6704: peace, divine in NT (id: 6704)

God's ultimate provision of peace is discovered in the person and work of Jesus Christ. It is only through Christ that peace with God can be achieved and maintained.

Provision of peace through the Father
-------------------------------------

### Peace in a believer's relationship with the Father

**[ROM 5:1](https://ref.ly/Rom5:1)** *See also* [ROM 8:1](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1), [ROM 8:31–8:39](https://ref.ly/Rom8:31-Rom8:39); [1CO 1:2–1:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:2-1Cor1:3)

### Peace through the Father's provision for the believer

**[1TI 6:17](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:17)** *See also* [MAT 6:25–6:34](https://ref.ly/Matt6:25-Matt6:34) parallel [LUK 12:22–12:31](https://ref.ly/Luke12:22-Luke12:31); [MAT 7:7–7:11](https://ref.ly/Matt7:7-Matt7:11) parallel [LUK 11:9–11:13](https://ref.ly/Luke11:9-Luke11:13)

Provision of peace through Jesus Christ
---------------------------------------

### Through Jesus Christ's coming

**[LUK 2:10–2:14](https://ref.ly/Luke2:10-Luke2:14)** [ISA 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6-Isa9:7); ; [MIC 5:2–5:5](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2-Mic5:5); ; [ZEC 9:9–9:10](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9-Zech9:10); [LUK 2:25–2:32](https://ref.ly/Luke2:25-Luke2:32); ; [EPH 2:17](https://ref.ly/Eph2:17)

### Through Jesus Christ's teaching

**[JHN 16:33](https://ref.ly/John16:33)** *See also* [JHN 14:23–14:27](https://ref.ly/John14:23-John14:27), [JHN 15:3](https://ref.ly/John15:3)

### Through Jesus Christ's ministry

**[ACT 10:36](https://ref.ly/Acts10:36)** *See also* [MRK 4:35–4:41](https://ref.ly/Mark4:35-Mark4:41) parallels [MAT 8:23–8:27](https://ref.ly/Matt8:23-Matt8:27), [LUK 8:22–8:25](https://ref.ly/Luke8:22-Luke8:25); [LUK 4:33–4:35](https://ref.ly/Luke4:33-Luke4:35) parallel [MRK 1:23–1:25](https://ref.ly/Mark1:23-Mark1:25); [LUK 4:38–4:41](https://ref.ly/Luke4:38-Luke4:41) parallels [MAT 8:14–8:17](https://ref.ly/Matt8:14-Matt8:17), [MRK 1:29–1:34](https://ref.ly/Mark1:29-Mark1:34)

### Through Jesus Christ's ascension

**[ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34)** *See also* [LUK 24:51–24:53](https://ref.ly/Luke24:51-Luke24:53); [ACT 2:33–2:39](https://ref.ly/Acts2:33-Acts2:39)

## 6705: peace, believers' experience of (id: 6705)

Peace is the birthright of every believer in all circumstances. It is found only in God and is maintained through having a close relationship with him.

Peace for believers in differing situations
-------------------------------------------

### In times of sickness, pressure and hardships

**[PSA 41:1–41:3](https://ref.ly/Ps41:1-Ps41:3)**; **[MAT 11:28](https://ref.ly/Matt11:28)** *See also* [JOB 1:13–1:22](https://ref.ly/Job1:13-Job1:22), [JOB 2:7–2:10](https://ref.ly/Job2:7-Job2:10); [ACT 16:22–16:25](https://ref.ly/Acts16:22-Acts16:25); [2CO 12:7–12:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:7-2Cor12:10); [2TI 4:16–4:18](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:16-2Tim4:18)

### In times of death and grief

**[JHN 14:1–14:3](https://ref.ly/John14:1-John14:3)** *See also* [JOB 19:25–19:26](https://ref.ly/Job19:25-Job19:26); [2KI 22:18–22:20](https://ref.ly/2Kgs22:18-2Kgs22:20); [ISA 57:1–57:2](https://ref.ly/Isa57:1-Isa57:2); [1TH 4:13–4:18](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:13-1Thess4:18)

----------------------------------

### Forgiveness

### Hope

**[ROM 15:13](https://ref.ly/Rom15:13)** *See also* [ROM 5:1–5:5](https://ref.ly/Rom5:1-Rom5:5)

## 6708: predestination (id: 6708)

God's foreordination of all events and circumstances for the good of his people and the glory of his name.

Predestination depends on God's sovereignty
-------------------------------------------

### He is the Creator of all things

**[JER 32:17–32:19](https://ref.ly/Jer32:17-Jer32:19)** *See also* [GEN 1:1](https://ref.ly/Gen1:1); [JOB 38:1–38:4](https://ref.ly/Job38:1-Job38:4); [ISA 44:24–44:28](https://ref.ly/Isa44:24-Isa44:28), [ISA 45:12–45:13](https://ref.ly/Isa45:12-Isa45:13), [ISA 48:12–48:14](https://ref.ly/Isa48:12-Isa48:14)

### He rules over nature and history

**[PRO 16:4](https://ref.ly/Prov16:4)** *See also* [GEN 18:10–18:14](https://ref.ly/Gen18:10-Gen18:14); [PSA 67:4](https://ref.ly/Ps67:4); [PRO 16:9](https://ref.ly/Prov16:9), [PRO 16:33](https://ref.ly/Prov16:33), [PRO 21:1](https://ref.ly/Prov21:1); [MAT 8:23–8:27](https://ref.ly/Matt8:23-Matt8:27) parallels [MRK 4:35–4:41](https://ref.ly/Mark4:35-Mark4:41), [LUK 8:22–8:25](https://ref.ly/Luke8:22-Luke8:25); [MAT 10:29–10:30](https://ref.ly/Matt10:29-Matt10:30); [ACT 17:26](https://ref.ly/Acts17:26)

### His will is perfect

**[GEN 18:25](https://ref.ly/Gen18:25)** *See also* [EXO 33:19](https://ref.ly/Exod33:19); [DEU 32:4](https://ref.ly/Deut32:4); [JOB 8:3](https://ref.ly/Job8:3); [PSA 119:137](https://ref.ly/Ps119:137); [DAN 4:37](https://ref.ly/Dan4:37)

God's predestined purposes cannot be thwarted
---------------------------------------------

### Human beings cannot stand against his will

**[ROM 9:19–9:21](https://ref.ly/Rom9:19-Rom9:21)** *See also* [PSA 2:1–2:4](https://ref.ly/Ps2:1-Ps2:4); [PRO 19:21](https://ref.ly/Prov19:21), [PRO 21:30](https://ref.ly/Prov21:30); [ISA 14:24–14:27](https://ref.ly/Isa14:24-Isa14:27), [ISA 46:10–46:12](https://ref.ly/Isa46:10-Isa46:12); [DAN 4:35](https://ref.ly/Dan4:35)

### False gods are impotent before him

**[PSA 115:3–115:8](https://ref.ly/Ps115:3-Ps115:8)** *See also* [ISA 44:8–44:20](https://ref.ly/Isa44:8-Isa44:20), [ISA 45:20](https://ref.ly/Isa45:20), [ISA 48:14](https://ref.ly/Isa48:14)

### He brings good out of evil

**[GEN 50:20](https://ref.ly/Gen50:20)** *See also* [GEN 15:13–15:16](https://ref.ly/Gen15:13-Gen15:16), [GEN 45:4–45:8](https://ref.ly/Gen45:4-Gen45:8)

Predestination undergirds biblical prophecy
-------------------------------------------

### It explains the prophets' confidence

**[1KI 22:17–22:28](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:17-1Kgs22:28)** *See also* [1PE 1:10–1:12](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:10-1Pet1:12)

### It is demonstrated in the fulfilment of prophecy

The life and ministry of Jesus Christ was predestined
-----------------------------------------------------

### In that it was predicted by the prophets

**[ISA 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6-Isa9:7)** *See also* [ISA 11:1–11:10](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1-Isa11:10), [ISA 52:13–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa52:13-Isa53:12); [JER 23:5–23:6](https://ref.ly/Jer23:5-Jer23:6); [ACT 3:18](https://ref.ly/Acts3:18); [GAL 4:4–4:5](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4-Gal4:5)

### In the outcome it achieved

**[GEN 3:15](https://ref.ly/Gen3:15)**

God's purpose in predestination is to bless his people
------------------------------------------------------

### In the path their lives follow

**[ROM 8:28](https://ref.ly/Rom8:28)** *See also* [PSA 139:14–139:16](https://ref.ly/Ps139:14-Ps139:16); [JER 29:11](https://ref.ly/Jer29:11); [MAT 10:29–10:31](https://ref.ly/Matt10:29-Matt10:31) parallel [LUK 12:6–12:7](https://ref.ly/Luke12:6-Luke12:7)

**[ROM 8:29–8:30](https://ref.ly/Rom8:29-Rom8:30)** *See also* [GEN 12:1–12:3](https://ref.ly/Gen12:1-Gen12:3); [MAT 11:25–11:27](https://ref.ly/Matt11:25-Matt11:27); [MRK 4:11](https://ref.ly/Mark4:11); [JHN 6:37–6:44](https://ref.ly/John6:37-John6:44); [ACT 13:48](https://ref.ly/Acts13:48); [1TH 5:9](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:9)

### In their assurance of salvation

**[ROM 8:31–8:39](https://ref.ly/Rom8:31-Rom8:39)** *See also* [JHN 10:27–10:29](https://ref.ly/John10:27-John10:29), [JHN 17:2](https://ref.ly/John17:2); [EPH 1:3–1:14](https://ref.ly/Eph1:3-Eph1:14) *Predestination is basic to Christian certainty.*

### Regarding final perseverance

**[PHP 1:6](https://ref.ly/Phil1:6)** *See also* [PSA 138:8](https://ref.ly/Ps138:8); [JHN 6:37–6:40](https://ref.ly/John6:37-John6:40); [PHP 2:12–2:13](https://ref.ly/Phil2:12-Phil2:13); [JAS 5:11](https://ref.ly/Jas5:11)

**[EPH 2:10](https://ref.ly/Eph2:10)** *See also* [JER 1:4–1:5](https://ref.ly/Jer1:4-Jer1:5); [ACT 22:10](https://ref.ly/Acts22:10); [GAL 1:15–1:17](https://ref.ly/Gal1:15-Gal1:17)

------------------------

**[ISA 65:11–65:12](https://ref.ly/Isa65:11-Isa65:12)** *See also* [GEN 6:17](https://ref.ly/Gen6:17) *the flood*; [EXO 7:13](https://ref.ly/Exod7:13), [EXO 9:13–9:18](https://ref.ly/Exod9:13-Exod9:18); [JOS 11:20](https://ref.ly/Josh11:20); [2KI 19:25–19:26](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:25-2Kgs19:26); [ISA 14:24–14:27](https://ref.ly/Isa14:24-Isa14:27) *judgment on Assyria*; [ISA 19:12–19:14](https://ref.ly/Isa19:12-Isa19:14), [ISA 23:9](https://ref.ly/Isa23:9) *judgment on Tyre*; [JER 49:20](https://ref.ly/Jer49:20), [JER 50:45](https://ref.ly/Jer50:45) *judgment on Babylon*; [1PE 2:6–2:8](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:6-1Pet2:8); [ISA 8:14–8:15](https://ref.ly/Isa8:14-Isa8:15)

------------------------------------------------------

## 6710: privileges (id: 6710)

Spiritual and material benefits conferred upon people by God. They are given, not because of human merit, but because of God's graciousness, and therefore carry responsibilities with them.

Privileges as the gift of God, not the result of human merit
------------------------------------------------------------

**[1CO 4:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor4:7)** *See also* [LUK 1:26–1:38](https://ref.ly/Luke1:26-Luke1:38); [EPH 2:8–2:9](https://ref.ly/Eph2:8-Eph2:9); [PHP 3:4–3:9](https://ref.ly/Phil3:4-Phil3:9)

The privileged position of humanity in creation
-----------------------------------------------

**[PSA 8:3–8:6](https://ref.ly/Ps8:3-Ps8:6)** *See also* [GEN 1:26–1:28](https://ref.ly/Gen1:26-Gen1:28)

The privileged position of Israel
---------------------------------

**[ROM 9:4–9:5](https://ref.ly/Rom9:4-Rom9:5)** *See also* [DEU 7:7–7:9](https://ref.ly/Deut7:7-Deut7:9); [2SA 7:22–7:24](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:22-2Sam7:24); [ROM 11:1–11:12](https://ref.ly/Rom11:1-Rom11:12)

The privileged position of the believer
---------------------------------------

### The privilege of forgiveness and new life

## 6712: propitiation (id: 6712)

The satisfaction of the righteous demands of God in relation to human sin and its punishment through the sacrificial death of Jesus Christ upon the cross, by which the penalty of sin is cancelled and the anger of God averted. \[The NIV is distinctive at this point, in that it generally translates this term by “atonement” and related words.].

The need for propitiation: God's anger against sin
--------------------------------------------------

**[PSA 7:11](https://ref.ly/Ps7:11)**; **[ROM 2:5](https://ref.ly/Rom2:5)** *See also* [EXO 32:11–32:14](https://ref.ly/Exod32:11-Exod32:14); [NUM 32:8–32:15](https://ref.ly/Num32:8-Num32:15); [DEU 6:14–6:15](https://ref.ly/Deut6:14-Deut6:15); [2KI 23:26](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:26); [PSA 78:38](https://ref.ly/Ps78:38); [ISA 30:27–30:31](https://ref.ly/Isa30:27-Isa30:31); [DAN 9:16–9:19](https://ref.ly/Dan9:16-Dan9:19); [HOS 11:8–11:9](https://ref.ly/Hos11:8-Hos11:9); [MAT 25:41–25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:41-Matt25:46); [JHN 3:36](https://ref.ly/John3:36); [ROM 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18); [EPH 5:6](https://ref.ly/Eph5:6)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

## 6714: ransom (id: 6714)

## 6716: reconciliation (id: 6716)

The restoration of fellowship between God and humanity and the resulting restoration of human relationships. The NT affirms that the reconciliation of the world to God is only possible on the basis of the work of Jesus Christ.

* **Associated Articles:** 6717: reconciliation, of the world to God (ID: `6717@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6718: reconciliation, between believers (ID: `6718@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6717: reconciliation, of the world to God (id: 6717)

On account of sin, people are alienated from God and cut off from fellowship with him. Through Jesus Christ, God reconciles the world to himself, breaking down the barriers of hostility and estrangement.

A broken relationship through sin brings alienation from God
------------------------------------------------------------

**[ISA 59:2](https://ref.ly/Isa59:2)** *See also* [GEN 3:23–3:24](https://ref.ly/Gen3:23-Gen3:24) *the expulsion from Eden*; [GEN 4:13–4:14](https://ref.ly/Gen4:13-Gen4:14) *Cain's alienation from God*; [ISA 48:22](https://ref.ly/Isa48:22), [ISA 64:7](https://ref.ly/Isa64:7); [JER 33:5](https://ref.ly/Jer33:5); [LUK 18:13](https://ref.ly/Luke18:13) *the tax collector's prayer for mercy*; [ROM 5:10](https://ref.ly/Rom5:10), [ROM 8:7](https://ref.ly/Rom8:7); [EPH 2:1–2:3](https://ref.ly/Eph2:1-Eph2:3), [EPH 2:12](https://ref.ly/Eph2:12), [EPH 4:18](https://ref.ly/Eph4:18); [COL 1:21](https://ref.ly/Col1:21); [JAS 4:4](https://ref.ly/Jas4:4)

---------------------------------------------------------

## 6718: reconciliation, between believers (id: 6718)

True reconciliation between people is only possible after they have been reconciled to God through Jesus Christ. Believers are urged to settle differences among themselves in brotherly love.

The cause of the breakdown in relationships is sin
--------------------------------------------------

## 6720: redemption (id: 6720)

The buying back or release of an object or person. In Scripture redemption refers to God's ransoming of believers only through the death of Jesus Christ upon the cross and to all the benefits that this brings.

* **Associated Articles:** 6721: redemption, in everyday life (ID: `6721@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6722: redemption, in OT (ID: `6722@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6723: redemption, in NT (ID: `6723@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6724: redeemer, God as (ID: `6724@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6725: redeemer, Jesus Christ as (ID: `6725@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6721: redemption, in everyday life (id: 6721)

The purchase of a person's freedom or the buying back of an object from the possession of another. Scripture provides illustrations of these everyday meanings of the word.

The OT redemption of property, animals and individuals
------------------------------------------------------

### Redemption of property

**[LEV 25:24–25:28](https://ref.ly/Lev25:24-Lev25:28)** *See also* [LEV 27:15–27:20](https://ref.ly/Lev27:15-Lev27:20); [RUT 4:1–4:6](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:1-Ruth4:6); [JER 32:8](https://ref.ly/Jer32:8)

### Redemption of animals

**[EXO 13:13](https://ref.ly/Exod13:13)** *See also* [EXO 34:20](https://ref.ly/Exod34:20); [LEV 27:13](https://ref.ly/Lev27:13), [LEV 27:27](https://ref.ly/Lev27:27); [NUM 18:14–18:17](https://ref.ly/Num18:14-Num18:17)

### Redemption of individuals

**[EXO 30:12–30:16](https://ref.ly/Exod30:12-Exod30:16)** *See also* [EXO 13:12–13:13](https://ref.ly/Exod13:12-Exod13:13), [EXO 21:8](https://ref.ly/Exod21:8), [EXO 21:28–21:32](https://ref.ly/Exod21:28-Exod21:32), [EXO 34:19–34:20](https://ref.ly/Exod34:19-Exod34:20); [LEV 25:47–25:55](https://ref.ly/Lev25:47-Lev25:55); [NUM 3:44–3:51](https://ref.ly/Num3:44-Num3:51)

The redemption of the nation of Israel
--------------------------------------

**[EXO 6:6](https://ref.ly/Exod6:6)** *See also* [DEU 9:26](https://ref.ly/Deut9:26); [2SA 7:23–7:24](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:23-2Sam7:24) parallel [1CH 17:21–17:22](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:21-1Chr17:22); [NEH 1:10](https://ref.ly/Neh1:10); [PSA 77:15](https://ref.ly/Ps77:15), [PSA 78:35](https://ref.ly/Ps78:35), [PSA 106:10](https://ref.ly/Ps106:10); [ISA 43:1–43:3](https://ref.ly/Isa43:1-Isa43:3); [MIC 6:4](https://ref.ly/Mic6:4)

Redemption as release from sin
------------------------------

**[PSA 130:8](https://ref.ly/Ps130:8)** *See also* [ISA 40:2](https://ref.ly/Isa40:2)

The role of the redeemer
------------------------

### In helping close relatives regain property or freedom

**[LEV 25:25](https://ref.ly/Lev25:25)** *See also* [LEV 25:47–25:49](https://ref.ly/Lev25:47-Lev25:49), [LEV 27:15–27:20](https://ref.ly/Lev27:15-Lev27:20); [RUT 2:20](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:20), [RUT 3:9](https://ref.ly/Ruth3:9), [RUT 4:1–4:8](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:1-Ruth4:8)

## 6722: redemption, in OT (id: 6722)

The act of God by which he delivered his people from bondage. The exodus of Israel from Egypt and the later deliverance of Jerusalem from exile in Babylon are seen as definitive examples of God's redeeming acts.

God is the Redeemer of his people
---------------------------------

### God redeems his people from captivity out of love

**[DEU 7:8](https://ref.ly/Deut7:8)** *See also* [EXO 6:6–6:8](https://ref.ly/Exod6:6-Exod6:8), [EXO 15:13](https://ref.ly/Exod15:13); [PSA 130:7–130:8](https://ref.ly/Ps130:7-Ps130:8); [ISA 43:14](https://ref.ly/Isa43:14), [ISA 47:1–47:4](https://ref.ly/Isa47:1-Isa47:4), [ISA 63:16](https://ref.ly/Isa63:16); [JER 15:21](https://ref.ly/Jer15:21), [JER 31:11](https://ref.ly/Jer31:11), [JER 50:34](https://ref.ly/Jer50:34)

### His redemption guarantees security

**[ISA 43:1–43:4](https://ref.ly/Isa43:1-Isa43:4)** *See also* [ISA 44:21–44:28](https://ref.ly/Isa44:21-Isa44:28), [ISA 48:20](https://ref.ly/Isa48:20), [ISA 49:7](https://ref.ly/Isa49:7), [ISA 49:22–49:26](https://ref.ly/Isa49:22-Isa49:26), [ISA 52:9–52:12](https://ref.ly/Isa52:9-Isa52:12)

### He redeems from death

**[PSA 49:15](https://ref.ly/Ps49:15)** *See also* [JOB 5:20](https://ref.ly/Job5:20), [JOB 19:25–19:26](https://ref.ly/Job19:25-Job19:26); [HOS 13:14](https://ref.ly/Hos13:14)

### His redemption is associated with his holiness

**[ISA 41:14](https://ref.ly/Isa41:14)** *See also* [ISA 43:14](https://ref.ly/Isa43:14), [ISA 47:4](https://ref.ly/Isa47:4), [ISA 48:17](https://ref.ly/Isa48:17), [ISA 49:7](https://ref.ly/Isa49:7), [ISA 54:5](https://ref.ly/Isa54:5)

### He redeems by his mighty arm

**[LUK 1:51](https://ref.ly/Luke1:51)** *See also* [DEU 11:2](https://ref.ly/Deut11:2); [PSA 89:10](https://ref.ly/Ps89:10), [PSA 77:15](https://ref.ly/Ps77:15); [ISA 62:8](https://ref.ly/Isa62:8)

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 7:8; Exodus 6:6-8; Exodus 15:13; Psalms 130:7-8; Isaiah 43:14; Isaiah 47:1-4; Isaiah 63:16; Jeremiah 15:21; Jeremiah 31:11; Jeremiah 50:34; Isaiah 43:1-4; Isaiah 44:21-28; Isaiah 48:20; Isaiah 49:7; Isaiah 49:22-26; Isaiah 52:9-12; Psalms 49:15; Job 5:20; Job 19:25-26; Hosea 13:14; Isaiah 41:14; Isaiah 47:4; Isaiah 48:17; Isaiah 54:5; Luke 1:51; Deuteronomy 11:2; Psalms 89:10; Psalms 77:15; Isaiah 62:8

## 6723: redemption, in NT (id: 6723)

The culmination of the OT work of redemption is seen in the cross of Jesus Christ, by which believers are liberated from bondage to sin.

Redemption is achieved through Jesus Christ
-------------------------------------------

**[EPH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Eph1:7)**

Jesus Christ's teaching on redemption
-------------------------------------

**[MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45)** parallel [MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28) *See also* [MAT 26:26–26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:26-Matt26:28) parallels [MRK 14:22–14:25](https://ref.ly/Mark14:22-Mark14:25), [LUK 22:20–22:22](https://ref.ly/Luke22:20-Luke22:22)

Apostolic teaching on redemption
--------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is the redemption of believers

**[1CO 1:30](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:30)** *See also* [1TI 2:6](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:6); [TIT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:14)

## 6728: regeneration (id: 6728)

The radical renewal of a person's inner being by the work of God's Spirit.

The need for regeneration
-------------------------

**[JHN 3:3](https://ref.ly/John3:3)** *See also* [EPH 2:1](https://ref.ly/Eph2:1), [EPH 2:5](https://ref.ly/Eph2:5); [COL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Col2:13)

Regeneration is a work of God
-----------------------------

### It originates in God the Father

**[JHN 1:12–1:13](https://ref.ly/John1:12-John1:13)** *Regeneration cannot be controlled by human actions or rituals; it is an act of God's sovereign will.*

### It is made possible by the resurrection of Jesus Christ

**[1PE 1:3](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:3)** *See also* [EPH 2:4–2:5](https://ref.ly/Eph2:4-Eph2:5)

### It occurs through the hearing of the Christian gospel

**[JAS 1:18](https://ref.ly/Jas1:18)** *See also* [1PE 1:23–1:25](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:23-1Pet1:25) *The “word of God” is the good news about Jesus Christ.*

### It is effected by God's Spirit

**[JHN 3:5–3:8](https://ref.ly/John3:5-John3:8)** *See also* [JHN 6:63](https://ref.ly/John6:63); [TIT 3:5](https://ref.ly/Titus3:5)

Regeneration is given to those who believe in Jesus Christ
----------------------------------------------------------

**[1JN 5:1](https://ref.ly/1John5:1)**

Baptism is the sign of regeneration
-----------------------------------

**[JHN 3:5](https://ref.ly/John3:5)** *Water here is seen by some, though not all, interpreters as a reference to baptism, administered by the church to new converts as a sign of their new birth and their entry into the Christian community.* *See also* [ACT 2:38–2:39](https://ref.ly/Acts2:38-Acts2:39); [EPH 5:25–5:26](https://ref.ly/Eph5:25-Eph5:26); [TIT 3:5](https://ref.ly/Titus3:5)

The results of regeneration
---------------------------

### Entry into God's kingdom

**[JHN 3:5](https://ref.ly/John3:5)**

### A new holiness of life

**[1JN 3:9](https://ref.ly/1John3:9)** *See also* [1JN 5:18](https://ref.ly/1John5:18); [1PE 2:1–2:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:1-1Pet2:2)

### Love for other people

**[1JN 4:7](https://ref.ly/1John4:7)** *See also* [1JN 5:2](https://ref.ly/1John5:2)

### Victory over the world's sinful pattern of life

**[1JN 5:4](https://ref.ly/1John5:4)**

* **Associated Passages:** John 3:3; Ephesians 2:1; Ephesians 2:5; Colossians 2:13; John 1:12-13; 1 Peter 1:3; Ephesians 2:4-5; James 1:18; 1 Peter 1:23-25; John 3:5-8; John 6:63; Titus 3:5; 1 John 5:1; John 3:5; Acts 2:38-39; Ephesians 5:25-26; 1 John 3:9; 1 John 5:18; 1 Peter 2:1-2; 1 John 4:7; 1 John 5:2; 1 John 5:4

## 6730: reinstatement (id: 6730)

Restoration to a previous state or position. It is demonstrated in human relationships and also by God in his love and grace restoring fallen humanity and lifting up his people to their former place within his service.

The basis of reinstatement
--------------------------

### God does not remember sin

*See also* [PSA 103:12](https://ref.ly/Ps103:12); [ISA 38:17](https://ref.ly/Isa38:17), [ISA 43:25](https://ref.ly/Isa43:25); [EZK 20:44](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:44)

### God's unfailing love

[PSA 89:28](https://ref.ly/Ps89:28); ; [LAM 3:22](https://ref.ly/Lam3:22); ; [HOS 11:8](https://ref.ly/Hos11:8)

God's reinstatement of fallen humanity
--------------------------------------

### Humanity's unique calling

**[HEB 2:6–2:8](https://ref.ly/Heb2:6-Heb2:8)** *See also* [PSA 8:4–8:6](https://ref.ly/Ps8:4-Ps8:6); [GEN 1:26–1:27](https://ref.ly/Gen1:26-Gen1:27); [ISA 43:7](https://ref.ly/Isa43:7)

### Humanity's fall and reinstatement

**[ROM 3:23–3:24](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23-Rom3:24)**; **[2TH 2:14](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:14)** *See also* [ROM 5:15–5:19](https://ref.ly/Rom5:15-Rom5:19), [ROM 8:17](https://ref.ly/Rom8:17); [EPH 1:12](https://ref.ly/Eph1:12); [HEB 2:10](https://ref.ly/Heb2:10); [1PE 5:1](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:1)

God's reinstatement of Israel
-----------------------------

### The promise of reinstatement

**[MIC 4:8](https://ref.ly/Mic4:8)** *See also* [ISA 1:26](https://ref.ly/Isa1:26), [ISA 60:10](https://ref.ly/Isa60:10); [HAG 2:9](https://ref.ly/Hag2:9); [ZEC 1:17](https://ref.ly/Zech1:17), [ZEC 10:6–10:8](https://ref.ly/Zech10:6-Zech10:8)

### Reinstatement as God's people

**[HOS 2:23](https://ref.ly/Hos2:23)** *See also* [ROM 9:25](https://ref.ly/Rom9:25); [1PE 2:10](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:10)

### Reinstatement as God's bride

**[ISA 54:5–54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:5-Isa54:8)** *See also* [JER 3:12–3:14](https://ref.ly/Jer3:12-Jer3:14); [HOS 2:14–2:20](https://ref.ly/Hos2:14-Hos2:20)
