**[JER 33:10–33:16](https://ref.ly/Jer33:10-Jer33:16)** *See also* [2CH 30:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr30:9); [JER 31:16–31:17](https://ref.ly/Jer31:16-Jer31:17); [HOS 11:10–11:11](https://ref.ly/Hos11:10-Hos11:11)

God's reinstatement of his servants
-----------------------------------

[JDG 16:22](https://ref.ly/Judg16:22) *Samson's hair begins to grow again, indicating his renewed call to serve God*; ; [JER 15:19](https://ref.ly/Jer15:19) *God will continue to speak through a repentant Jeremiah*; ; [DAN 4:34–4:36](https://ref.ly/Dan4:34-Dan4:36) *Nebuchadnezzar's sanity and kingdom is restored*; ; [JON 3:1–3:2](https://ref.ly/Jonah3:1-Jonah3:2) *God renews Jonah's commission*; ; [JHN 21:15–21:17](https://ref.ly/John21:15-John21:17) *Jesus Christ reinstates Peter after his denial.*

---------------------------------

[GEN 40:13](https://ref.ly/Gen40:13) *Pharaoh's cupbearer reinstated*; ; [1SA 19:6–19:7](https://ref.ly/1Sam19:6-1Sam19:7) *David reinstated by Saul*; ; [2SA 9:7](https://ref.ly/2Sam9:7) *Mephibosheth reinstated by David*; ; [2SA 14:33](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:33) *Absalom reinstated by David*; ; [DAN 3:30](https://ref.ly/Dan3:30) *Nebuchadnezzar reinstates Shadrach, Meshach and Abednego*; ; [HOS 3:2–3:3](https://ref.ly/Hos3:2-Hos3:3) *Gomer reinstated as Hosea's wife*; ; [LUK 15:22–15:24](https://ref.ly/Luke15:22-Luke15:24) *the prodigal reinstated by his father*; ; [PHM 1:10](https://ref.ly/Phlm1:10) *Paul asks Philemon to reinstate his slave Onesimus*; ; [PHM 1:24](https://ref.ly/Phlm1:24) *John Mark, formerly rejected, has here been reinstated as Paul's companion.*

## 6732: repentance (id: 6732)

A change of mind leading to a change of action. It involves a sincere turning from sin to serve God and includes sorrow for, and confession of, sin and where possible restitution. At points, Scripture refers to God changing his plans in response to events.

* **Associated Articles:** 6733: repentance, nature of (ID: `6733@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6734: repentance, importance of (ID: `6734@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6735: repentance, examples of (ID: `6735@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6736: repentance, of God (ID: `6736@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6733: repentance, nature of (id: 6733)

Scripture stresses the necessity of repentance from sin if individuals and communities are to have full fellowship with God. It also uses the term to refer to God's relenting of sending judgment on his people, usually in response to human repentance.

Repentance is a requirement for fellowship with God
---------------------------------------------------

**[2KI 17:13](https://ref.ly/2Kgs17:13)**; **[1TH 1:9](https://ref.ly/1Thess1:9)** *See also* [PSA 34:14](https://ref.ly/Ps34:14); [ISA 55:7](https://ref.ly/Isa55:7); [ACT 14:15](https://ref.ly/Acts14:15); [JAS 4:7–4:10](https://ref.ly/Jas4:7-Jas4:10)

Repentance involves turning from sin
------------------------------------

### Sorrow for sin

**[PSA 51:17](https://ref.ly/Ps51:17)**; **[2CO 7:8–7:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor7:8-2Cor7:10)** *See also* [JOB 42:6](https://ref.ly/Job42:6); [PSA 34:18](https://ref.ly/Ps34:18); [ISA 57:15](https://ref.ly/Isa57:15), [ISA 66:2](https://ref.ly/Isa66:2); [JOL 2:12–2:13](https://ref.ly/Joel2:12-Joel2:13); [LUK 18:13](https://ref.ly/Luke18:13)

### Confession of sin

**[LUK 15:17–15:19](https://ref.ly/Luke15:17-Luke15:19)** *See also* [LEV 5:5](https://ref.ly/Lev5:5); [PSA 51:1–51:3](https://ref.ly/Ps51:1-Ps51:3); [PRO 28:13](https://ref.ly/Prov28:13); [HOS 14:1–14:2](https://ref.ly/Hos14:1-Hos14:2)

### Making appropriate restitution

Repentance involves turning to God
----------------------------------

### Faith in God

--------------------------

## 6734: repentance, importance of (id: 6734)

Repentance is of central importance because sin brings God's judgment and fellowship with God is only possible through full and sincere repentance. God, through his servants, calls people to repent as the only way to escape the judgment and receive the forgiveness and restoration which he offers.

The call to repentance
----------------------

**[LUK 5:32](https://ref.ly/Luke5:32)**; **[JAS 5:19–5:20](https://ref.ly/Jas5:19-Jas5:20)** *See also* [JER 25:4–25:6](https://ref.ly/Jer25:4-Jer25:6); [EZK 33:7–33:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek33:7-Ezek33:9); [MRK 1:4](https://ref.ly/Mark1:4) parallel [LUK 3:3](https://ref.ly/Luke3:3); [LUK 24:47](https://ref.ly/Luke24:47); [2TI 2:24–2:26](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:24-2Tim2:26)

Repentance opens the way for blessing
-------------------------------------

### It is the only way to escape God's judgment

**[EZK 18:30–18:32](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:30-Ezek18:32)** *See also* [JOB 36:12](https://ref.ly/Job36:12); [JER 18:7–18:8](https://ref.ly/Jer18:7-Jer18:8), [JER 26:3](https://ref.ly/Jer26:3); [HOS 11:5](https://ref.ly/Hos11:5); [JON 3:10](https://ref.ly/Jonah3:10); [LUK 3:8–3:9](https://ref.ly/Luke3:8-Luke3:9); [REV 2:5](https://ref.ly/Rev2:5)

### It prepares the way for God's kingdom

**[MAT 4:17](https://ref.ly/Matt4:17)** parallel [MRK 1:14–1:15](https://ref.ly/Mark1:14-Mark1:15) *See also* [MAT 3:2](https://ref.ly/Matt3:2)

### It brings forgiveness and restoration

**[2CH 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:13-2Chr7:14)**; **[ISA 55:7](https://ref.ly/Isa55:7)** *See also* [DEU 30:1–30:10](https://ref.ly/Deut30:1-Deut30:10); [NEH 1:8–1:9](https://ref.ly/Neh1:8-Neh1:9); [JOB 22:23–22:25](https://ref.ly/Job22:23-Job22:25), [JOB 36:10–36:11](https://ref.ly/Job36:10-Job36:11); [ISA 44:22](https://ref.ly/Isa44:22); [ACT 2:38–2:39](https://ref.ly/Acts2:38-Acts2:39), [ACT 3:19](https://ref.ly/Acts3:19), [ACT 5:31](https://ref.ly/Acts5:31), [ACT 11:18](https://ref.ly/Acts11:18)

God desires that all people should repent
-----------------------------------------

### He wants everyone to be saved

**[EZK 18:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:23)**

### His patience with the unrepentant

**[2PE 3:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:9)** *See also* [ISA 65:2](https://ref.ly/Isa65:2); [ROM 2:4](https://ref.ly/Rom2:4); [REV 2:21](https://ref.ly/Rev2:21)

### His discipline encourages repentance

**[JER 31:18–31:20](https://ref.ly/Jer31:18-Jer31:20)** *See also* [ISA 10:20–10:21](https://ref.ly/Isa10:20-Isa10:21), [ISA 19:22](https://ref.ly/Isa19:22); [HOS 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Hos2:6-Hos2:7), [HOS 6:1](https://ref.ly/Hos6:1)

Taking God's opportunity for repentance
---------------------------------------

**[ISA 55:6](https://ref.ly/Isa55:6)**; **[ACT 17:30–17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:30-Acts17:31)** *See also* [HEB 3:13–3:15](https://ref.ly/Heb3:13-Heb3:15), [HEB 4:7](https://ref.ly/Heb4:7); [PSA 95:7–95:8](https://ref.ly/Ps95:7-Ps95:8)

Refusing God's opportunity for repentance
-----------------------------------------

### Examples of those who refuse to repent

**[JER 35:15](https://ref.ly/Jer35:15)** *See also* [JER 5:3](https://ref.ly/Jer5:3); [MAT 11:20](https://ref.ly/Matt11:20), [MAT 21:32](https://ref.ly/Matt21:32); [REV 9:20–9:21](https://ref.ly/Rev9:20-Rev9:21), [REV 16:9–16:11](https://ref.ly/Rev16:9-Rev16:11)

### God confirms those who refuse to repent in their hardness of heart

[MAT 13:14–13:15](https://ref.ly/Matt13:14-Matt13:15) parallels [MRK 4:11–4:12](https://ref.ly/Mark4:11-Mark4:12), [LUK 8:9–8:10](https://ref.ly/Luke8:9-Luke8:10); ; [ACT 28:25–28:27](https://ref.ly/Acts28:25-Acts28:27); ; [ISA 6:10](https://ref.ly/Isa6:10)

Repentance may not remove the effects of human sin
--------------------------------------------------

[NUM 14:39–14:45](https://ref.ly/Num14:39-Num14:45) *The Israelites' repentance could not prevent the wandering that resulted from their refusal to enter the promised land*; ; [1SA 15:24–15:26](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:24-1Sam15:26) *Saul's repentance is too late to escape God's judgment on his kingship*; ; [2SA 12:13–12:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:13-2Sam12:14) *Despite David's repentance the son of his adulterous relationship with Bathsheba still died*; ; [HEB 12:16–12:17](https://ref.ly/Heb12:16-Heb12:17) *Esau's repentance could not bring back the birthright he had sold to Jacob.*

* **Associated Passages:** Luke 5:32; James 5:19-20; Jeremiah 25:4-6; Ezekiel 33:7-9; Mark 1:4; Luke 3:3; Luke 24:47; 2 Timothy 2:24-26; Ezekiel 18:30-32; Job 36:12; Jeremiah 18:7-8; Jeremiah 26:3; Hosea 11:5; Jonah 3:10; Luke 3:8-9; Revelation 2:5; Matthew 4:17; Mark 1:14-15; Matthew 3:2; 2 Chronicles 7:13-14; Isaiah 55:7; Deuteronomy 30:1-10; Nehemiah 1:8-9; Job 22:23-25; Job 36:10-11; Isaiah 44:22; Acts 2:38-39; Acts 3:19; Acts 5:31; Acts 11:18; Ezekiel 18:23; 2 Peter 3:9; Isaiah 65:2; Romans 2:4; Revelation 2:21; Jeremiah 31:18-20; Isaiah 10:20-21; Isaiah 19:22; Hosea 2:6-7; Hosea 6:1; Isaiah 55:6; Acts 17:30-31; Hebrews 3:13-15; Hebrews 4:7; Psalms 95:7-8; Jeremiah 35:15; Jeremiah 5:3; Matthew 11:20; Matthew 21:32; Revelation 9:20-21; Revelation 16:9-11; Matthew 13:14-15; Mark 4:11-12; Luke 8:9-10; Acts 28:25-27; Isaiah 6:10; Numbers 14:39-45; 1 Samuel 15:24-26; 2 Samuel 12:13-14; Hebrews 12:16-17

## 6735: repentance, examples of (id: 6735)

Scripture provides examples to illustrate the importance of repentance for individuals and communities.

The repentance of individuals
-----------------------------

### The call to personal repentance

**[ACT 2:38](https://ref.ly/Acts2:38)** *See also* [2TI 2:19](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:19)

### Examples of individual repentance

[NUM 22:31–22:35](https://ref.ly/Num22:31-Num22:35) *Balaam*; ; [2SA 24:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:10) parallel [1CH 21:8](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:8) *David, after taking a census*; ; [1KI 21:27–21:29](https://ref.ly/1Kgs21:27-1Kgs21:29) *Ahab*; ; [2KI 22:19](https://ref.ly/2Kgs22:19) *Josiah*; ; [JOB 42:6](https://ref.ly/Job42:6) *Job*; ; [PSA 51:1–51:17](https://ref.ly/Ps51:1-Ps51:17) *David, following his adultery with Bathsheba*; ; [LUK 15:21](https://ref.ly/Luke15:21) *the prodigal son*; ; [LUK 18:13](https://ref.ly/Luke18:13) *the tax collector in the temple*; ; [MAT 26:75](https://ref.ly/Matt26:75) parallels [MRK 14:72](https://ref.ly/Mark14:72), [LUK 22:61–22:62](https://ref.ly/Luke22:61-Luke22:62) *Peter's sorrow after denying Jesus Christ*; ; [JHN 21:15–21:17](https://ref.ly/John21:15-John21:17) *Peter's confession and reinstatement*; ; [ACT 8:22–8:24](https://ref.ly/Acts8:22-Acts8:24) *Simon the sorcerer's repentance may not have been genuine.*

Corporate repentance
--------------------

### Examples of corporate repentance

**[JER 18:7–18:8](https://ref.ly/Jer18:7-Jer18:8)**; **[MAT 3:1–3:6](https://ref.ly/Matt3:1-Matt3:6)** parallels [MRK 1:1–1:6](https://ref.ly/Mark1:1-Mark1:6), [LUK 3:1–3:6](https://ref.ly/Luke3:1-Luke3:6) *See also* [NUM 21:7](https://ref.ly/Num21:7) *Israel in the desert*; [JDG 10:15–10:16](https://ref.ly/Judg10:15-Judg10:16) *Israel in the time of the judges*; [1SA 7:3–7:4](https://ref.ly/1Sam7:3-1Sam7:4) *Israel, after asking for a king*; [ISA 19:22](https://ref.ly/Isa19:22) *Egypt turns to God in repentance*; [ACT 9:32–9:35](https://ref.ly/Acts9:32-Acts9:35) *the people of Lydda and Sharon*

### Leaders encouraged corporate repentance

**[EZR 10:1](https://ref.ly/Ezra10:1)** *See also* [2KI 23:1–23:7](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:1-2Kgs23:7) *Josiah leads Judah in repentance*; [2CH 15:8–15:15](https://ref.ly/2Chr15:8-2Chr15:15) *Asa leads Judah in repentance*; [2CH 30:6–30:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr30:6-2Chr30:9) *Hezekiah leads Israel and Judah in repentance*; [EZR 10:10–10:12](https://ref.ly/Ezra10:10-Ezra10:12) *Following the exile, Ezra leads the Israelites in repentance*; [JON 3:6–3:8](https://ref.ly/Jonah3:6-Jonah3:8) *The king of Nineveh leads the people in repentance.*

## 6738: rescue (id: 6738)

Deliverance from people or forces that are overwhelming. It implies a liberator with strength and wisdom to ensure true freedom. God's physical rescue of the Israelites points to the spiritual deliverance obtained by Jesus Christ.

When rescue is the only answer
------------------------------

**[PSA 35:10](https://ref.ly/Ps35:10)** *See also* [DEU 22:27](https://ref.ly/Deut22:27), [DEU 28:29](https://ref.ly/Deut28:29); [1SA 12:21](https://ref.ly/1Sam12:21); [ISA 42:22](https://ref.ly/Isa42:22); [DAN 8:4](https://ref.ly/Dan8:4), [DAN 8:7](https://ref.ly/Dan8:7); [HOS 5:14](https://ref.ly/Hos5:14); [MIC 5:8](https://ref.ly/Mic5:8); [ROM 7:24](https://ref.ly/Rom7:24)

God's power to rescue in times of need
--------------------------------------

[ISA 41:10](https://ref.ly/Isa41:10); ; [1CO 10:13](https://ref.ly/1Cor10:13); ; [2CO 12:9–12:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:9-2Cor12:10); ; [HEB 13:6](https://ref.ly/Heb13:6)

God's people cry to him for rescue
----------------------------------

**[JDG 10:15](https://ref.ly/Judg10:15)** *See also* [1SA 7:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam7:8); [PSA 22:11](https://ref.ly/Ps22:11), [PSA 35:17](https://ref.ly/Ps35:17), [PSA 43:1](https://ref.ly/Ps43:1), [PSA 69:13–69:14](https://ref.ly/Ps69:13-Ps69:14), [PSA 71:2](https://ref.ly/Ps71:2), [PSA 107:19](https://ref.ly/Ps107:19), [PSA 140:1](https://ref.ly/Ps140:1), [PSA 142:6](https://ref.ly/Ps142:6), [PSA 143:9](https://ref.ly/Ps143:9), [PSA 144:7](https://ref.ly/Ps144:7); [PRO 24:11](https://ref.ly/Prov24:11); [ROM 15:31](https://ref.ly/Rom15:31) *Paul's need for protection*

-----------------------------------

### From their enemies

## 6740: returning to God (id: 6740)

Scripture declares that all humanity has turned away from God, and must return to him. The term “repentance” is often used to refer to this process of returning to God and the inward and outward changes that it demands of people. Scripture also indicates that believers can wander away from God; they too must return to him.

All people have turned away from God
------------------------------------

**[ISA 53:6](https://ref.ly/Isa53:6), [ISA 64:6](https://ref.ly/Isa64:6)** *See also* [JOB 25:4](https://ref.ly/Job25:4); [JER 17:9](https://ref.ly/Jer17:9); [JHN 3:19](https://ref.ly/John3:19); [ROM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23)

Wayward people must return to God
---------------------------------

**[ISA 44:22](https://ref.ly/Isa44:22)**; **[HOS 14:1](https://ref.ly/Hos14:1)**; **[ZEC 1:3](https://ref.ly/Zech1:3)** *See also* [2CH 30:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr30:9); [NEH 1:9](https://ref.ly/Neh1:9); [JOB 22:23](https://ref.ly/Job22:23); [JER 24:7](https://ref.ly/Jer24:7); [LAM 3:40](https://ref.ly/Lam3:40); [HOS 6:1](https://ref.ly/Hos6:1), [HOS 12:6](https://ref.ly/Hos12:6); [JOL 2:12](https://ref.ly/Joel2:12)

## 6742: sackcloth and ashes (id: 6742)

Sackcloth is a coarse, black cloth made from goat's hair that was worn together with the burnt ashes of wood as a sign of mourning for personal and national disaster, as a sign of repentance and at times of prayer for deliverance.

Sackcloth and ashes worn as a sign of mourning for the dead
-----------------------------------------------------------

### By Jacob for Joseph

**[GEN 37:34](https://ref.ly/Gen37:34)**

### By David, Joab and the people for Abner

*See also* [2SA 3:31](https://ref.ly/2Sam3:31)

## 6744: sanctification (id: 6744)

The process of becoming consecrated to God, which is an integral aspect of being a member of the people of God. This process of being made holy through the work of the Holy Spirit ultimately rests upon the sacrificial death of Jesus Christ, which the OT anticipates and foreshadows.

* **Associated Articles:** 6745: sanctification, nature and basis of (ID: `6745@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6746: sanctification, means and results of (ID: `6746@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6747: sanctification, and Holy Spirit (ID: `6747@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6745: sanctification, nature and basis of (id: 6745)

The process of renewal and consecration by which believers are made holy through the work of the Holy Spirit. Sanctification is the consequence of justification and is dependent upon a person being in a right relationship with God.

Sanctification is grounded in the holiness of God
-------------------------------------------------

### God is holy

**[EZK 39:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:7)** *See also* [LEV 22:32](https://ref.ly/Lev22:32); [JOS 24:19](https://ref.ly/Josh24:19); [PSA 30:4](https://ref.ly/Ps30:4); [HOS 11:9](https://ref.ly/Hos11:9); [ISA 6:3](https://ref.ly/Isa6:3); [REV 6:10](https://ref.ly/Rev6:10)

### God demands that his people should reflect his holiness

**[LEV 19:2](https://ref.ly/Lev19:2)** *See also* [LEV 11:44–11:45](https://ref.ly/Lev11:44-Lev11:45), [LEV 20:7–20:8](https://ref.ly/Lev20:7-Lev20:8); [HEB 2:11](https://ref.ly/Heb2:11); [1PE 1:15–1:16](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:15-1Pet1:16)

### Sanctification is the will of God for his people

**[1TH 4:3](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:3)** *See also* [EPH 1:4](https://ref.ly/Eph1:4), [EPH 2:10](https://ref.ly/Eph2:10); [2TH 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:13); [1PE 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:1-1Pet1:2)

## 6746: sanctification, means and results of (id: 6746)

Sanctification results from the renewing work of the Holy Spirit and leads to the renewal of believers and their being equipped for ministry in the world.

---------------------------

### The work of the Holy Spirit

### Yielding to sinful desires

## 6750: sin-bearer (id: 6750)

A person or animal that acts in God's sight in a substitutionary capacity, to whom are transferred the sins of others, together with the corresponding penalty for those sins.

The principle of accountability necessitates a sin\-bearer
----------------------------------------------------------

### All are held responsible for their own sin and its consequences

**[LEV 5:17](https://ref.ly/Lev5:17)** *See also* [LEV 5:1](https://ref.ly/Lev5:1), [LEV 20:16–20:21](https://ref.ly/Lev20:16-Lev20:21), [LEV 24:15–24:16](https://ref.ly/Lev24:15-Lev24:16); [EZK 18:19–18:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:19-Ezek18:20)

### Individuals and nations come under God's judgment for their sin

**[EZK 4:4–4:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek4:4-Ezek4:6)** *Ezekiel's behaviour foreshadowed God's judgment on the sin of Israel and Judah.* *See also* [EZK 16:58](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:58), [EZK 18:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:4); [MAT 11:21–11:24](https://ref.ly/Matt11:21-Matt11:24) parallel [LUK 10:12–10:15](https://ref.ly/Luke10:12-Luke10:15); [ROM 1:18–1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18-Rom1:32), [ROM 6:23](https://ref.ly/Rom6:23)

God's gracious provision of a sin\-bearer in the OT
---------------------------------------------------

### God takes away the sin of those who repent

**[ISA 44:22](https://ref.ly/Isa44:22)** *See also* [2SA 12:13](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:13); [PSA 103:12](https://ref.ly/Ps103:12); [ZEC 3:4](https://ref.ly/Zech3:4)

### The sacrifice of an animal to remove sin

**[LEV 5:5–5:6](https://ref.ly/Lev5:5-Lev5:6)** *See also* [LEV 4:1–4:35](https://ref.ly/Lev4:1-Lev4:35), [LEV 5:14–6:7](https://ref.ly/Lev5:14-Lev6:7)

### The Day of Atonement and the removal of sin

**[LEV 16:8–16:10](https://ref.ly/Lev16:8-Lev16:10)** *The sacrificial goat expiated the sins of the people in the sight of God; the driving away of the scapegoat into the desert symbolised the removal of the sin of the community.* *See also* [LEV 16:15–16:19](https://ref.ly/Lev16:15-Lev16:19) *the sin offering*; [LEV 16:20–16:22](https://ref.ly/Lev16:20-Lev16:22) *the scapegoat*

The function of the priests in the sin\-bearing process
-------------------------------------------------------

### The priests were responsible for the sanctuary

**[NUM 18:1–18:7](https://ref.ly/Num18:1-Num18:7)**

### Strict regulations governed the performance of their service

**[LEV 22:9](https://ref.ly/Lev22:9)** *See also* [EXO 28:42–28:43](https://ref.ly/Exod28:42-Exod28:43), [EXO 30:17–30:21](https://ref.ly/Exod30:17-Exod30:21); [LEV 16:3–16:4](https://ref.ly/Lev16:3-Lev16:4)

### The priests bore the sin of the people in a representative capacity

**[EXO 28:36–28:38](https://ref.ly/Exod28:36-Exod28:38)** *See also* [LEV 10:17](https://ref.ly/Lev10:17)

Jesus Christ as sin\-bearer
---------------------------

### Jesus Christ bore the sins of the world on the cross

**[HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28)** *See also* [ISA 53:4–53:6](https://ref.ly/Isa53:4-Isa53:6), [ISA 53:10–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10-Isa53:12); [JHN 1:29](https://ref.ly/John1:29); [COL 2:14](https://ref.ly/Col2:14); [HEB 10:11–10:14](https://ref.ly/Heb10:11-Heb10:14); [1PE 2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:24); [1JN 3:5](https://ref.ly/1John3:5)

### Jesus Christ's intercessory role as high priest

**[1JN 2:1](https://ref.ly/1John2:1)** *See also* [ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34); [HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25)

* **Associated Passages:** Leviticus 5:17; Leviticus 5:1; Leviticus 20:16-21; Leviticus 24:15-16; Ezekiel 18:19-20; Ezekiel 4:4-6; Ezekiel 16:58; Ezekiel 18:4; Matthew 11:21-24; Luke 10:12-15; Romans 1:18-32; Romans 6:23; Isaiah 44:22; 2 Samuel 12:13; Psalms 103:12; Zechariah 3:4; Leviticus 5:5-6; Leviticus 4:1-35; Leviticus 5:14-6:7; Leviticus 16:8-10; Leviticus 16:15-19; Leviticus 16:20-22; Numbers 18:1-7; Leviticus 22:9; Exodus 28:42-43; Exodus 30:17-21; Leviticus 16:3-4; Exodus 28:36-38; Leviticus 10:17; Hebrews 9:28; Isaiah 53:4-6; Isaiah 53:10-12; John 1:29; Colossians 2:14; Hebrews 10:11-14; 1 Peter 2:24; 1 John 3:5; 1 John 2:1; Romans 8:34; Hebrews 7:25
* **Associated Articles:** 2306: Jesus Christ, as high priest (ID: `2306@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2315: Jesus Christ, as Lamb (ID: `2315@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5051: responsibility (ID: `5051@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6027: sin, God's remedy for (ID: `6027@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6614: atonement (ID: `6614@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6648: expiation (ID: `6648@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6712: propitiation (ID: `6712@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6752: substitution (ID: `6752@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7440: scapegoat (ID: `7440@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7766: priests (ID: `7766@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6752: substitution (id: 6752)

Jesus Christ died as the substitute for sinful humanity, taking humanity's place on the cross.

OT images of substitution
-------------------------

### Examples of substitution

**[GEN 22:13](https://ref.ly/Gen22:13)** *See also* [NUM 3:12–3:13](https://ref.ly/Num3:12-Num3:13), [NUM 3:41](https://ref.ly/Num3:41), [NUM 3:45](https://ref.ly/Num3:45), [NUM 8:18](https://ref.ly/Num8:18); [1SA 17:9](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:9); [1KI 20:42](https://ref.ly/1Kgs20:42); [LAM 5:7](https://ref.ly/Lam5:7); [EZK 4:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek4:4)

### Substitutes atoning for sin or acting as sin bearers

**[LEV 1:4](https://ref.ly/Lev1:4)** *See also* [EXO 28:38](https://ref.ly/Exod28:38); [LEV 16:21–16:22](https://ref.ly/Lev16:21-Lev16:22), [LEV 22:19–22:20](https://ref.ly/Lev22:19-Lev22:20)

### Anticipations of the substitutionary work of Jesus Christ

**[ISA 53:4–53:6](https://ref.ly/Isa53:4-Isa53:6)** *NT writers have interpreted the servant as Jesus Christ: see [Mt 8:17](https://ref.ly/Matt8:17) and [1Pe 2:23–25](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:23-1Pet2:25).* *See also* [PSA 69:9](https://ref.ly/Ps69:9)

----------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ died for believers

**[MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45)**; **[ROM 5:6](https://ref.ly/Rom5:6), [ROM 5:8](https://ref.ly/Rom5:8)**; **[1TH 5:10](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:10)** *See also* [JHN 10:11](https://ref.ly/John10:11), [JHN 11:50](https://ref.ly/John11:50); [ROM 14:15](https://ref.ly/Rom14:15); [2CO 5:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:14); [GAL 2:20](https://ref.ly/Gal2:20), [GAL 3:13](https://ref.ly/Gal3:13); [1TI 2:6](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:6); [TIT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:14); [HEB 2:9](https://ref.ly/Heb2:9); [1PE 2:21](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:21); [1JN 3:16](https://ref.ly/1John3:16)

### Jesus Christ died for sin

**[1PE 2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:24), [1PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:18)** *See also* [2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21); [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28)

-----------------------------------------

## 6754: union with Christ (id: 6754)

The sharing of believers in the life of Jesus Christ by faith, allowing them to share in all the benefits and riches that result from his person and work.

* **Associated Articles:** 6755: union with Christ, nature of (ID: `6755@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6756: union with Christ, significance of (ID: `6756@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 6755: union with Christ, nature of (id: 6755)

The nature of the union of Jesus Christ with believers is explained using a number of central images. The NT stresses the reality, closeness and considerable benefits of this union.

A covenantal relationship
-------------------------

### OT background

**[ISA 54:5–54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:5-Isa54:8)** *The marriage covenant is used to illustrate the intimacy of the relationship between God and his people.* *See also* [JER 3:14](https://ref.ly/Jer3:14), [JER 31:32](https://ref.ly/Jer31:32); [HOS 2:7](https://ref.ly/Hos2:7), [HOS 2:16](https://ref.ly/Hos2:16)

### In the NT

**[EPH 5:31–5:32](https://ref.ly/Eph5:31-Eph5:32)**

A relationship deepened through the incarnation
-----------------------------------------------

**[JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14)** *See also* [ROM 8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:3); [2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21); [GAL 4:4](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4); [PHP 2:7–2:8](https://ref.ly/Phil2:7-Phil2:8); [1TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:16); [HEB 2:14–2:18](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14-Heb2:18)

A relationship personally entered through faith
-----------------------------------------------

**[JHN 3:16](https://ref.ly/John3:16)** *See also* [JHN 1:12](https://ref.ly/John1:12), [JHN 2:11](https://ref.ly/John2:11), [JHN 7:38](https://ref.ly/John7:38); [ACT 16:31](https://ref.ly/Acts16:31); [ROM 3:22](https://ref.ly/Rom3:22), [ROM 8:1](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1), [ROM 10:9–10:10](https://ref.ly/Rom10:9-Rom10:10); [2CO 5:17](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:17); [GAL 2:16](https://ref.ly/Gal2:16)

A relationship enriched through the sacraments
----------------------------------------------

### Baptism

**[ROM 6:3–6:5](https://ref.ly/Rom6:3-Rom6:5)**; **[GAL 3:27](https://ref.ly/Gal3:27)** *See also* [MAT 28:19](https://ref.ly/Matt28:19); [ROM 6:8](https://ref.ly/Rom6:8); [COL 2:11–2:12](https://ref.ly/Col2:11-Col2:12)

### The Lord's Supper

[MAT 26:26–26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:26-Matt26:28) parallels [MRK 14:22–14:24](https://ref.ly/Mark14:22-Mark14:24), [LUK 22:17–22:20](https://ref.ly/Luke22:17-Luke22:20); ; [1CO 10:16](https://ref.ly/1Cor10:16), [1CO 11:23–11:29](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:23-1Cor11:29)

A relationship that affects every aspect of life
------------------------------------------------

**[1CO 6:17](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:17)** *See also* [JHN 15:1–15:8](https://ref.ly/John15:1-John15:8), [JHN 17:20–17:26](https://ref.ly/John17:20-John17:26); [ROM 8:9–8:11](https://ref.ly/Rom8:9-Rom8:11); [1CO 6:19–6:20](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:19-1Cor6:20); [GAL 2:20](https://ref.ly/Gal2:20)

It is a mysterious relationship
-------------------------------

**[COL 1:27](https://ref.ly/Col1:27)** *See also* [EPH 5:32](https://ref.ly/Eph5:32)

## 6756: union with Christ, significance of (id: 6756)

The union between Jesus Christ and believers is the basis for all exhortation to faithful, holy living, as well as to sharing in all his benefits.

For the believer
----------------

### Identification with Jesus Christ

**[MAT 10:40](https://ref.ly/Matt10:40)** *See also* [MAT 18:5](https://ref.ly/Matt18:5), [MAT 25:40](https://ref.ly/Matt25:40); [EPH 1:1](https://ref.ly/Eph1:1); [PHP 1:1](https://ref.ly/Phil1:1)

### Conformity to Jesus Christ

**[COL 3:1–3:4](https://ref.ly/Col3:1-Col3:4)** *See also* [MAT 16:24](https://ref.ly/Matt16:24) parallels [MRK 8:34](https://ref.ly/Mark8:34), [LUK 9:23](https://ref.ly/Luke9:23); [ROM 6:5](https://ref.ly/Rom6:5); [1CO 6:15–6:17](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:15-1Cor6:17); [2CO 4:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:10); [EPH 2:6](https://ref.ly/Eph2:6); [PHP 3:10–3:11](https://ref.ly/Phil3:10-Phil3:11); [1PE 4:13](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:13); [1JN 2:6](https://ref.ly/1John2:6), [1JN 2:28](https://ref.ly/1John2:28), [1JN 3:24](https://ref.ly/1John3:24), [1JN 5:20](https://ref.ly/1John5:20)

### Blessing in Christ

**[EPH 1:3–1:14](https://ref.ly/Eph1:3-Eph1:14)**

--------------
